### [37] [When New Generators Arrive: Lifelong Machine-Generated Text Attribution via Ridge Feature Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05626)
*Zhen Sun,Yifan Liao,Zhicong Huang,Jiaheng Wei,Cheng Hong,Yutao Yue,Xinlei He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: RidgeFT 提出了一种无需样本回放的轻量级解析更新框架，通过存储充分统计量并结合闭式岭回归，有效解决了终身机器生成文本归因中新旧知识难以平衡的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型不断涌现，机器生成文本（MGT）归因任务需要模型在识别新模型的同时保持对旧模型的识别能力，即实现“终身学习”。现有的方法在平衡新类适应与旧类保持方面表现不佳，且通常依赖样本回放，这引发了性能稳定性及效率问题。

Method: RidgeFT 是一种轻量级的解析更新框架，其核心步骤包括：1. 在初始生成器集上训练任务感知编码器；2. 当观察到新生成器时，存储类级别的紧凑充分统计量；3. 固定编码器，通过协方差校准抑制无关变异；4. 利用固定随机特征提升表示能力；5. 最终通过基于充分统计量的闭式岭回归（Ridge Regression）来实现新类别的增量学习。

Result: 在多主题评估及多种初始生成器设置下，RidgeFT 始终优于现有基准方法。在跨领域、跨骨干网络及不同增量协议中，RidgeFT 均取得了最优的宏平均 F1 分数（Macro-F1），在实现新类高效适应的同时，显著提升了对旧类的保留能力。

Conclusion: RidgeFT 通过利用特征稳定的解析更新方法，成功在无需样本回放的情况下解决了终身机器生成文本归因中的灾难性遗忘问题，证明了基于类级别充分统计量的闭式更新是处理此类任务的一种高效且简单的方案。

Abstract: Machine-generated text (MGT) attribution aims to identify the specific generator responsible for a given text, thereby providing fine-grained evidence for model accountability and misuse investigation. As new large language models continue to emerge, attribution models must continuously incorporate new generators while preserving their ability to recognize previously seen ones. Prior works have shown that this lifelong MGT attribution setting is challenging, and existing methods often struggle to achieve a stable balance between adapting to new classes and retaining old ones. To address this issue, we propose RidgeFT, a lightweight analytic update framework that does not rely on exemplar replay. RidgeFT trains a task-aware encoder on the initial generator set, stores compact class-wise sufficient statistics when each generator class is first observed, and then freezes the encoder for replay-free closed-form updates. It then suppresses generator-irrelevant variation through covariance calibration, improves representation capacity with fixed random features, and updates new classes through closed-form ridge regression based on class-level sufficient statistics. Across multi-topic evaluations with varying initial generator setups, RidgeFT consistently outperforms baselines. It achieves the best macro-F1 across domains, backbones, and incremental protocols, while also improving both old-class retention and new-class adaptation. These results suggest that feature-stable analytic updates provide a simple yet effective approach to lifelong MGT attribution.

</details>


### [38] [Bootstrapping Semantic Layer from Execution for Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05634)
*Youngwon Lee,Jaejin Kim,Seung-won Hwang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了GATE框架，通过在Text-to-SQL任务中利用执行反馈来动态解析模糊的数据基础（grounding），并将验证过的结果存入内存以便重用，从而解决了因语义描述不全导致的查询生成难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现实世界的Text-to-SQL任务中，由于数据库存储方式与用户表述之间存在差异，且往往缺乏完整的预定义语义层，导致模型在处理专业领域数据时存在多个潜在的基础假设（grounding hypotheses）歧义。现有方法难以解决这种基础信息缺失的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为GATE（Grounding After Test from Execution）的方法。该方法在生成SQL时保留多种基础假设，通过执行已生成部分来获取观察结果，筛选出被证据支持的假设，并将其转化为可重用的内存条目存储起来，供后续推理步骤调用。

Result: 在现实世界和受控的基准测试中，GATE方法均表现出优于强基准模型的效果，证明了利用执行反馈引导构建内存的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，执行反馈不仅可以作为验证手段，还能作为一种引导机制，用于构建可重用的执行基础内存，从而有效解决复杂Text-to-SQL任务中数据基础（grounding）缺失的问题，显著提升模型性能。

Abstract: Real-world text-to-SQL is often under-specified until user phrases are grounded in how the database stores values. Prior work attempts to address this by requiring a semantic layer to specify groundings in advance, but such specifications are often incomplete, especially in expert domains where domain-specific conventions are under-documented. As this leaves multiple grounding hypotheses open for the same SQL part, we introduce GATE (Grouding After Test from Execution), which bootstraps missing groundings from execution feedback. GATE keeps grounding hypotheses open while executing the already grounded parts to obtain observations. Then, only the hypothesis supported by that observation is grounded and stored as a memory entry, recording what was tested and how the open part should be written in SQL. These entries accumulate into execution-grounded memory, allowing later steps to reuse supported groundings. Across real-world and controlled benchmarks, GATE consistently improves over strong baselines, demonstrating that execution can serve not only as validation but also as a bootstrapping mechanism for reusable memory in text-to-SQL.

</details>


### [39] [QueryAgent-R1: Bridging Query Generation and Product Retrieval for E-Commerce Query Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05671)
*Dike Sun,Zheng Zou,Jingtong Zang,Qi Sun,Huaipeng Zhaoand Tao Luo,Xiaoyi Zeng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: QueryAgent-R1 是一种针对电商搜索的代理框架，通过将查询生成与实时库存检索相结合，并利用强化学习优化转化指标，成功解决了查询相关性与商品转化率之间的错位问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的电商搜索推荐系统多侧重于提升查询词层面的相关性，忽略了检索到的商品是否符合用户的实际购买意向。这种“相关但低转化”的错位现象导致了高点击率（CTR）与低转化率（CVR）之间的矛盾，亟需一种能够端到端对齐查询与下游用户转化偏好的新框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 QueryAgent-R1 的记忆增强型代理框架。核心创新包括：1. 链式检索优化（Chain-of-Retrieval），在生成查询词时引入实时库存反馈进行校验与修正；2. 强化学习中的一致性奖励机制（Consistency Reward），旨在同时优化查询相关性与下游用户转化（CVR）；3. 记忆抽象模块（Memory Abstraction），用于高效建模用户画像。

Result: 在离线数据集上的测试显示该模型优于现有主流基线；在大型生产平台的在线 A/B 测试中，QueryAgent-R1 实现了查询点击率（Query CTR）提升 2.9% 和引导转化率（Guided CVR）提升 3.1% 的显著效果。

Conclusion: QueryAgent-R1 证明了将检索环节与代理机制结合，并通过强化学习优化下游转化目标，是提升电商搜索系统整体性能的有效途径。该研究强调了搜索意图与商品转化一致性的重要性，为未来电商搜索推荐提供了新的优化范式。

Abstract: Query recommendation in e-commerce search aims to proactively suggest queries that match users' potential interests. However, existing methods mainly optimize query-level relevance, while neglecting whether the retrieved products align with users' downstream preferences. This mismatch often leads to high query click through rates (CTR) but low product conversion rates (CVR). To bridge this gap, we propose QueryAgent-R1, a memory-augmented agentic framework that improves end-to-end alignment via chain-of-retrieval optimization. Our QueryAgent-R1 grounds query generation in real inventory retrieval, allowing the agent to validate and refine queries based on retrieved products. We also design a consistency reward in the agentic reinforcement learning (RL) process to jointly optimize query relevance and downstream engagement. In addition, we construct a memory abstraction module for efficient user profiling. To support offline evaluation, we construct two datasets based on both proprietary industrial data and public datasets, on which QueryAgent-R1 consistently outperforms strong baselines. Moreover, on a large scale production platform, QueryAgent-R1 improves Query CTR by 2.9% and guided CVR by 3.1% in online A/B tests.

### [40] [Value-and-Structure Alignment for Routing-Consistent Quantization of Mixture-of-Experts Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05688)
*Hancheol Park,Geonho Lee,Tairen Piao,Tae-Ho Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对 MoE 模型量化过程中因路由不稳定性导致的性能下降问题，本文提出了 VSRAQ 方法，通过对齐量化前后的路由价值与决策结构，确保专家选择路径的一致性，在零推理额外开销的情况下提升了模型精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MoE 模型虽然通过稀疏激活提高了参数效率，但巨大的参数量使得量化成为部署的必然选择。然而，现有的量化方法会产生微小扰动，导致 MoE 模型出现路由不稳定性（即改变了 Token 的专家选择路径），从而严重损害模型性能。现有研究缺乏针对 MoE 路由特性的专门优化。

Method: 提出一种名为 VSRAQ（价值与结构路由对齐）的训练后量化（PTQ）方法，包含两个核心目标：1. 价值对齐（Value Alignment），旨在匹配量化前后的路由逻辑值（logits）或分数；2. 结构对齐（Structure Alignment），旨在保留专家排序及 Top-k 路由决策边界，从而确保量化后专家选择路径的稳定性。

Result: 实验结果表明，VSRAQ 能够显著提高量化过程中专家选择的一致性，在多项 MoE 基础模型测试中，其性能始终优于传统的仅基于重建的量化方法及其他已有的路由器感知基准方法。

Conclusion: VSRAQ 通过有效维持 MoE 模型在量化前后的路由一致性，成功解决了量化导致专家选择发生改变的问题，在不增加推理开销的前提下显著提升了量化 MoE 模型的性能。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) models scale foundation models efficiently by activating only a subset of experts for each token, but their large number of expert parameters still makes quantization essential for practical deployment. Unlike dense models, however, MoE models are sensitive to routing instability: small quantization-induced perturbations can change the top-$k$ expert selection, altering the computation path and degrading model quality. We propose Value-and-Structure Routing Alignment for Quantization (VSRAQ), a MoE-specific post-training quantization objective that preserves pre-quantization expert-selection behavior under quantization. VSRAQ combines two complementary objectives that jointly preserve expert-selection behavior: value alignment, which matches routing-relevant logits or scores, and structure alignment, which preserves expert ordering and top-$k$ decision boundaries. By maintaining routing consistency, VSRAQ reduces quantization-induced degradation without introducing any inference-time overhead and can be integrated into existing quantization frameworks. Experiments on recent MoE foundation models show that VSRAQ improves expert-selection consistency and consistently outperforms reconstruction-only and router-aware baselines.

### [41] [Rethinking LoRA Memory Through the Lens of KV Cache Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05698)
*Chunsheng Zuo,Liaoyaqi Wang,William Jurayj,William Fleshman,Benjamin Van Durme*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了文档LoRA（参数化记忆）与KV Cache（上下文记忆）的关系，发现LoRA在上下文缺失时能显著补充信息，证明其作为解码时参数化记忆的互补作用，且QA监督训练优于预测下一个token的预训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管参数化检索增强（如LoRA适配器）被用于减少模型对长输入上下文的依赖，但目前尚不清楚这种“参数化记忆”与模型KV Cache中的“上下文记忆”之间存在何种相互作用。

Method: 研究者通过逐步剔除文档的KV Cache（键值缓存）状态，观察文档LoRA在不同上下文保留程度下的贡献。通过对比在不同阶段应用适配器（如仅在回答生成阶段）以及不同的训练目标（QA监督学习对比原始上下文的Next-Token-Prediction），分析参数化记忆与上下文记忆的相互作用。

Result: 实验表明，当KV Cache信息充足时，文档LoRA贡献微乎其微；但在极度压缩上下文的情况下，LoRA可恢复13-21个ROUGE-L评分。研究发现，当基座模型已完成文档编码，仅在回答生成阶段应用LoRA时，其效果最佳。

Conclusion: 文档LoRA是一种有效的补充性记忆通道，其价值主要在上下文信息匮乏时显现。它更适合被视为“解码时的参数化记忆”而非传统的文档编码器。此外，使用QA任务进行微调比单纯的Next-Token-Prediction能产生更有效的适配器。

Abstract: Parametric retrieval augmentation encodes document information into lightweight, document-specific modules such as LoRA adapters, reducing the need to include all evidence as input context. However, it remains unclear how this parameter-side memory interacts with context-side memory stored in the KV cache. We study this interaction in document-level question answering by progressively evicting document key-value states and measuring when a document LoRA contributes beyond the retained context. We find that document LoRA adds little when the KV cache is largely intact, but becomes increasingly useful under aggressive compression, recovering 13-21 ROUGE-L points when no document context remains. The gain is largest when the base model encodes the document, and the adapter is applied only during answer generation, suggesting that document LoRA is better understood as decoding-time parametric memory than as a document encoder. Finally, QA-style supervision produces substantially stronger adapters than raw-context next-token-prediction. These results position document LoRA as a complementary memory channel whose value emerges precisely when context-side evidence is scarce.

</details>


### [42] [Beyond tokens: a unified framework for latent communication in LLM-based multi-agent systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05711)
*Yingzhuo Liu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文针对大语言模型多智能体系统中从自然语言通信向“潜空间通信”的范式转变，提出了一个三轴分析框架，系统梳理了现有技术路线并指出了该领域的发展瓶颈与未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于大语言模型的自然语言多智能体系统应用广泛，但自然语言通信协议存在推理成本高、离散化过程产生信息丢失以及语言本身具有歧义和冗余等结构性缺陷。为此，研究界开始探索直接交换连续表示（即潜空间通信）来绕过文本生成的瓶颈。

Method: 作者提出了一个统一的分类框架，通过三个正交维度对现有潜空间通信方法进行梳理：1) 通信内容（嵌入、隐藏状态、KV缓存等）；2) 发送-接收对齐机制（潜空间或层级对齐）；3) 信息融合方式（拼接、加法、注意力机制等）。基于此，作者系统归纳了18种代表性方法并总结出五种设计模式。

Result: 本文构建了一个涵盖潜空间通信的文献分类体系，识别了主流设计模式，并提出了当前领域面临的五个开放性挑战，包括跨架构兼容性、信道安全性、边缘侧压缩以及潜空间思维链的关系等，为后续研究提供了参考框架和词汇表。

Conclusion: 潜空间通信通过直接传输连续表示，有望突破传统自然语言通信在效率和信息保真度方面的瓶颈，是多智能体系统领域的重要演进方向。本文提出的三轴框架为系统评估该类方法提供了标准，并指明了跨架构对齐、安全性和压缩等关键研究方向。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems built on large language models (LLMs) have become a prevailing paradigm for tackling complex reasoning, planning, and tool-use tasks. The dominant communication protocol in such systems is natural language: agents exchange messages token-by-token, verbalising their internal reasoning so that peers can read, verify, and respond. While convenient and interpretable, this protocol suffers from three structural drawbacks -- high inference cost, irreversible information loss during discretization, and ambiguity/redundancy of natural language. A growing body of work therefore explores an alternative protocol -- latent communication -- in which agents exchange continuous representations (embeddings, hidden states, or KV-caches) directly, bypassing the bottleneck of text generation. This paper presents a unified framework for organising the rapidly expanding literature on latent communication. We analyse existing methods along three orthogonal axes: (1) WHAT information is communicated (Embeddings, Hidden States, KV-Caches, or other continuous state); (2) WHICH sender-receiver alignment is used (latent-space alignment and layer alignment); and (3) HOW the communicated information is fused into the receiver (concatenation, prepending, mathematical operations, cross-attention, or cache restoration). Under this 3-axis framework, we systematically categorise eighteen representative methods proposed between 2024 and 2026, identify five major design patterns, and surface a set of open challenges -- including cross-architecture alignment, security of latent channels, compression for edge deployment, and the relationship between latent communication and latent chain-of-thought. We hope that this framework both lowers the barrier to entry for new researchers and provides a vocabulary for comparing future work.

### [43] [Interpreting Style Representations via Style-Eliciting Prompts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05716)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构建了一个包含1,010个风格特征（覆盖26个类别）的数据集，通过提示大语言模型生成符合特定风格的文本，并基于此数据训练一个解码器，使其能够从输入文本的风格表示中逆向生成对应的风格诱导提示词（Style-eliciting Prompts）。

Abstract: Style representation learning is a powerful tool for authorship analysis and modeling writing style, yet the latent nature of learned representations makes them difficult to interpret. Recent work has attempted to explain these representations by generating natural language descriptions with large language models (LLMs) conditioned on input text. However, such descriptions are often prone to the LLM's biases and hallucinations, and they lack an explicit objective and practical utility. In this work, we propose a novel framework for interpreting style representations through style-eliciting prompts: natural language instructions designed to steer LLMs to generate text that reflects specific stylistic attributes. We curate 1,010 distinct style features spanning 26 stylistic categories and construct a dataset by prompting an LLM to generate text conditioned on these features. Using this data, we train a decoder to generate a style prompt from the style representation of the generated text. We evaluate our approach on three tasks: (1) recovering original style prompts from generated text, (2) generating text in the same style using the recovered prompts, and (3) steering LLM outputs to match the style of human-written texts. Experiments demonstrate that our method consistently outperforms strong baselines that directly prompt LLMs with target text, achieving superior performance in both style description and style imitation. These results highlight that style-eliciting prompts can provide a practical and interpretable interface to stylistic information encoded in style representations.

*Qiuyu Tian,Fengyi Chen,Yiding Li,Youyong Kong,Fan Guo,Yuyao Li,Jinjing Shen,Zhijing Xie,Yiyun Luo,Xin Zhang,Yingce Xia,Zequn Liu*

Abstract: Long-form narrative QA requires reasoning over evolving story worlds rather than isolated passages: answers may depend on earlier goals, changing character states, social relations, causal triggers, temporal position, and later consequences. Existing retrieval and graph-augmented generation methods improve evidence access, but their units--chunks, entities, relations, summaries, or tool actions--do not directly encode how evidence functions in a story. We introduce Narrative Knowledge Weaver(NKW), a source-grounded framework that aligns textual evidence, atomic facts, canonical graph structure, entity profiles, interactions, episodes, and storylines. ### [45] [AdaPLD: Adaptive Retrieval and Reuse for Efficient Model-Free Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05742)
*Runheng Liu,Jincheng Xie,Wen Hu,Xingchen Xiao,Heyan Huang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: AdaPLD 是一种无需训练的推测解码改进方法，通过融合语义检索和分支草稿构建，有效提升了无模型推测解码的加速比和稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的无模型推测解码方法（Model-free speculative decoding）在利用已有模型状态和文本进行草稿生成时存在局限性：一是基于词法检索的方法在面对文本变体时召回率较低；二是确定性的片段复制在面对上下文不确定性时较为脆弱。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AdaPLD 的方法。它通过结合词法锚定检索与语义相似度匹配来提升检索召回率，并采用分支复用假设（branched reuse hypotheses）来处理预测的不确定性，而非依赖单一的确定性文本片段。该方法无需训练即可实现。

Result: AdaPLD 在多个基准测试中表现优异，有效减少了目标模型的正向传递次数，最高可实现 3.10 倍的解码加速。

Conclusion: AdaPLD 是一种高效的训练无关解码加速方法，通过语义增强的检索和分支假设构建，显著缓解了现有无模型推测解码方法中存在的召回率低和对不确定性处理脆弱的问题，为大模型推理加速提供了新思路。

Abstract: Speculative decoding accelerates generation by verifying multiple drafted tokens in a single target-model forward pass, reducing sequential decoding iterations. Model-free variants avoid auxiliary draft models by reusing text and model states already available during generation, but their speedup depends on the reliability of the constructed drafts. We identify two limitations of existing reuse-based methods: lexically anchored retrieval has limited recall under surface-form variation, and deterministic span copying can be brittle when the retrieved context does not uniquely determine the continuation. We propose \emph{AdaPLD}, a training-free method that adaptively improves both retrieval and draft construction. AdaPLD preserves high-precision lexical reuse while using semantic similarity to recover additional reuse opportunities when lexical matching fails. It further constructs branched reuse hypotheses to account for continuation uncertainty, rather than relying on a single copied span. Across diverse benchmarks, AdaPLD reduces target-model forward passes and achieves up to $3.10\times$ decoding speedup.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间规划图对于治理至关重要，但解读这些图表需要极高的专业知识与推理能力。现有视觉语言模型（VLM）基准测试多集中在通用领域，缺乏针对城市规划这一专业领域深度认知过程的评估，难以满足实际业务需求。

Method: 构建了空间规划图数据库（SPMD），包含223张规划图和1629对专家标注的问答。提出了一个包含“感知、推理、关联、实施”四个递进维度的评估框架，用于测试模型对规划图的理解能力，并对比了不同代际模型（如Qwen3.6-Plus与GPT-4o）的性能。

Result: 实验显示模型性能虽有提升，但表现参差不齐。最新的Qwen3.6-Plus模型较GPT-4o有27%的显著提升，但所有模型在需要基于政策进行专业判断和复杂决策的“实施”类任务上仍表现不佳。

Conclusion: 目前的视觉语言模型（VLM）在处理空间规划图这一专业领域时仍存在局限性，特别是涉及评估性判断、政策敏感性和约束感知的任务。该研究强调了开发领域自适应多模态推理框架对于赋能未来城市规划的必要性。

Abstract: Spatial planning maps are central to territorial governance, translating planning objectives, regulations, and spatial strategies into visual forms for decision-making, public communication, and institutional coordination. Their interpretation, however, requires fine-grained visual perception, spatial reasoning, and policy-informed professional judgment, creating major challenges for both human learners and AI systems. With the rapid progress of Vision-Language Models (VLMs), their use in urban planning analysis is gaining attention, yet existing multimodal benchmarks mainly target general visual understanding and overlook the domain-specific cognitive processes of planning practice. To address this gap, we introduce PlanBench-V, the first comprehensive benchmark for evaluating VLMs in spatial planning map interpretation. We first build the Spatial Planning Map Database (SPMD), an expert-annotated dataset of 223 planning maps and 1629 question-answer pairs curated by professional planners, covering diverse geographic regions and cartographic styles. We then propose a theory-informed evaluation framework assessing four progressive capabilities: Perception, Reasoning, Association, and Implementation, corresponding to the cognitive pipeline of planning map interpretation. Extensive experiments across two generations of VLMs show clear progress but persistent limitations. The best 2026 agentic reasoning model, Qwen3.6-Plus, substantially outperforms the best 2025 model, GPT-4o, by 27%. Nevertheless, all models still struggle with implementation-oriented tasks requiring evaluative judgment, policy sensitivity, and constraint-aware decision-making. These findings reveal fundamental limitations of current VLMs in professional planning contexts and highlight the need for domain-adaptive multimodal reasoning frameworks. Code and data are available at https://plangpt.github.io.

### [47] [MARDoc: A Memory-Aware Refinement Agent Framework for Multimodal Long Document QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05749)
*Kaifeng Chen,Hongtao Liu,Qiyao Peng,Jian Yang,Yongqiang Liu,Xiaochen Zhang,Qing Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: MARDoc 是一种新型的多模态长文档问答框架，通过引入结构化记忆机制替代传统的长上下文累积，将任务解耦为检索、精炼、反思三个职能智能体，有效减少了推理过程中的噪声，提升了长文档处理与多跳推理的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态长文档智能体通常将所有交互轨迹、观察结果和推理过程混入单个不断增长的上下文中，随着交互深入，关键证据被稀释并产生噪声，导致多跳推理性能下降。因此需要一种更高效的记忆管理方案来提取并维护关键信息。

Method: 提出了 MARDoc 框架，将多模态长文档问答任务拆解为三个协同工作的专门智能体：1. Explorer（探测器）：负责多粒度多模态检索；2. Refiner（精炼器）：负责将交互记录提炼为结构化的证据与推理记忆；3. Reflector（反思器）：负责验证证据充分性并提供反馈。该系统摒弃了累积交互历史的方式，采用动态更新的结构化记忆。

Result: 在 MMLongBench-Doc 和 DocBench 数据集上的实验结果表明，MARDoc 的性能优于同基座模型的基线系统，验证了结构化记忆在智能体文档问答中的有效性。

Conclusion: MARDoc 通过引入结构化记忆管理机制，有效解决了多模态长文档问答中上下文噪声积累的问题。该研究证明了将检索、精炼和反思过程解耦并使用动态结构化记忆，能够显著提升智能体在复杂推理任务中的表现。

Abstract: Iterative retrieval-reasoning agents have recently shown promise for multimodal long-document question answering. However, most existing systems maintain a single growing context that mixes retrieval traces, observations, and intermediate reasoning. As interactions accumulate, key evidence becomes scattered and diluted, making multi-hop reasoning noisy. We propose MARDoc, a Memory-Aware Refinement Agent framework that decouples long-document QA into three specialized agents: an Explorer for multi-granularity multimodal retrieval, a Refiner for distilling interaction traces into structured evidence and reasoning memories, and a Reflector for checking evidence sufficiency and providing targeted feedback. Across iterations, the agents rely on a dynamically updated structured memory rather than a full accumulated interaction history. This design reduces context noise while preserving answer-critical facts and their logical dependencies. Experiments on MMLongBench-Doc and DocBench show that MARDoc achieves strong results, outperforming same-backbone baselines and demonstrating the effectiveness of structured memory for agentic document QA.

Abstract: While LLM-based agents excel at individual tasks, effective collaboration with realistic human partners remains challenging. To this end, this paper proposes CollabBench, a benchmark for evaluating and training collaborative agents in cooperative games. ### [49] [Can LLMs Be Constrained to the Past? Improving Knowledge Cutoff through Recall-Based Prompting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05804)
*Michiro Asai,Ailiang Lin,Yu Kishimoto,Takao Obi,Satoshi Kosugi,Kotaro Funakoshi,Manabu Okumura*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对大模型知识截止任务中直接问答的局限性，本文提出了自我回忆（SR）和问题回忆（QR）提示策略，有效提升了模型在截止日期限制下的推理和应答能力，并构建了MHEB基准以全面评估模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的知识截止提示方法主要依赖于直接生成答案，这种方式在处理与截止日期后知识存在因果关系但未被显式询问的问题时表现较差，限制了模型在处理复杂时间敏感任务时的可靠性。

Method: 提出了两种基于“回忆”的提示策略：1. 自我回忆（Self-Recall, SR）：引导模型重述其知识截止限制；2. 问题回忆（Question-Recall, QR）：要求模型在截止日期内回忆与问题相关的信息。同时，构建了多截止日期历史事件基准（MHEB）以进行系统性评估。

Result: 在三个现有基准测试上，SR和QR策略均优于传统的直接回答提示和分步推理基线。在反事实问题上表现尤为突出，且在MHEB测试中，SR与QR的结合策略始终展现出最佳的综合性能。

Conclusion: 研究表明，结合“自我回忆”（SR）和“问题回忆”（QR）两种策略能显著提升大模型在执行知识截止日期任务时的稳健性和准确性。特别是在处理反事实问题时，这种方法优于传统的直接回答和思维链方法。此外，多截止日期历史事件基准（MHEB）的构建为评估模型在不同截止日期条件下的表现提供了有力的工具。

Abstract: Prompted knowledge cutoff instructs a large language model (LLM) to act as if information beyond a specified cutoff date were unavailable. However, prior work mainly relies on direct-answer generation, which struggles when post-cutoff knowledge is not explicitly queried but is only causally related to the question. To address this limitation, we propose two recall-based prompting strategies: Self-Recall (SR), which asks the model to restate its cutoff constraint, and Question-Recall (QR), which requires the model to recall question-relevant information valid under the cutoff. Across three existing benchmarks, our methods outperform both direct-answer prompting and conventional step-by-step reasoning baselines, with particularly strong improvements on counterfactual questions. To investigate robustness across different cutoff settings, we further construct the Multi-cutoff Historical Event Benchmark (MHEB), which evaluates the same question under multiple cutoff years. Results show that knowledge cutoff performance varies with cutoff distance, while combining SR and QR consistently yields the best performance.

### [50] [ProSPy: A Profiling-Driven SQL-Python Agentic Framework for Enterprise Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05836)
*Zhaorui Yang,Huawei Zheng,Sen Yang,Yuhui Zhang,Haoxuan Li,Zhizhen Yu,Xuan Yi,Chen Hou,Defeng Xie,Chao Hu,Minfeng Zhu,Dazhen Deng,Haozhe Feng,Danqing Huang,Yingcai Wu,Peng Chen,Wei Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ProSPy是一个创新的SQL-Python代理框架，旨在解决企业级复杂数据库的Text-to-SQL难题，通过自动分析和分阶段推理，显著提升了数据查询与分析的准确性及鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型在企业级Text-to-SQL应用中面临挑战，主要包括：数据库模式庞大且异构、元数据缺失、SQL方言复杂、以及单一SQL语句难以完成复杂的分析任务。

Method: 提出ProSPy框架，将推理过程划分为四个阶段：1. 自动分析（Profiling）：提取细粒度数据证据；2. 模式修剪：根据任务需求裁剪大型数据库模式；3. SQL接口：获取中间视图；4. Python分析：利用Python处理复杂的下游数据逻辑，实现SQL与Python的优势互补。

Result: 在Spider 2.0-Lite和Spider 2.0-Snow数据集上表现优异，使用Claude-4.5-Opus模型时，执行准确率分别达到60.15%和60.51%，且在无需多数投票的情况下优于现有强基线模型，展现了良好的方言适配能力。

Conclusion: ProSPy证明了将基于SQL的高效数据库检索与基于Python的灵活数据分析相结合，是解决企业级复杂Text-to-SQL任务的有效途径。该框架通过自动化分析降低了对元数据的依赖，提升了多方言环境下的系统鲁棒性。

Abstract: Large language models have substantially advanced Text-to-SQL systems, yet applying them to enterprise-scale databases remains challenging. Real-world databases often contain large and heterogeneous schemas, incomplete metadata, dialect-specific SQL syntax, and complex analytical questions that are difficult to solve with a single SQL query. To address these challenges, we propose ProSPy, a Profiling-driven SQL--Python agentic framework for enterprise-scale Text-to-SQL. ProSPy structures the reasoning process into four stages: it first extracts fine-grained data evidence through automatic profiling, progressively prunes large schemas into task-relevant contexts, fetches intermediate views through a dialect-agnostic SQL interface, and finally performs flexible downstream analysis with Python. This design combines the efficiency of SQL over large databases with the flexibility of Python-based analysis, while reducing reliance on unreliable metadata and improving robustness across SQL dialects. Experiments on Spider 2.0-Lite and Spider 2.0-Snow show that ProSPy consistently outperforms strong baselines with both open-source and proprietary models, achieving execution accuracies of 60.15% and 60.51% with Claude-4.5-Opus, without majority voting. Further analysis shows that ProSPy is robust to SQL dialect variations and achieves a favorable trade-off between schema recall and precision.

### [51] [Mechanistic Insights into Functional Sparsity in Multimodal LLMs via CoRe Heads](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05843)
*Ruoxi Sun,Quantong Qiu,Juntao Li,Zecheng Tang,Yihang Lou,Min Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过提出“检索注意力质量”（RAM）指标，发现多模态大模型内部存在名为“CoRe头”的功能性稀疏结构，这些核心头负责关键视觉特征提取；研究证明该机制对推理性能至关重要，并可用于模型的高效加速与架构优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管多模态大模型在视觉-语言任务中表现卓越，但其从复杂且含噪的上下文中提取查询相关视觉特征的内部机制尚不明确。研究旨在揭示这些模型在处理多模态信息时是否存在特定的结构性规律或可解释机制。

Method: 研究引入了“检索注意力质量”（Retrieval Attention Mass, RAM）这一令牌级度量标准，用于识别并表征模型中负责跨模态检索的特殊注意力头，即“上下文感知检索”（CoRe）头。通过因果干预实验（消融实验）分析不同注意力头对模型性能的影响，并进行加速实验验证模型在利用稀疏性下的推理效率。

Result: 研究发现，MLLM中存在一小部分高度专业化的CoRe头，它们作为专门的信息提取器，负责关键特征的捕捉，而其余大部分注意力头则负责处理更广泛的上下文信息。实验表明，仅消融掉前5%的CoRe头就会导致多模态推理性能显著下降。此外，利用这种局部稀疏性可以在保持任务性能的同时，显著提升模型的推理速度。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了多模态大模型（MLLM）内部存在“功能性稀疏性”的结构特性。这一发现不仅深化了对多模态模型机制可解释性的理解，还为未来高效的模型架构设计和推理优化提供了重要的理论支撑。

Abstract: While Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) demonstrate remarkable proficiency on complex vision-language tasks, the mechanisms by which they extract query-relevant visual features from complex, noisy contexts remain opaque. In this paper, we present an in-depth interpretability study that uncovers a profound structural property within MLLMs: functional sparsity in cross-modal retrieval. Leveraging a token-level metric termed Retrieval Attention Mass (RAM), we identify and characterize a highly specialized subset of attention heads, referred to as Context-aware Retrieval (CoRe) heads. Across diverse visual domains and model scales, we observe a clear functional division: CoRe heads act as dedicated information extractors, while most other heads distribute attention over broader contextual regions. Causal interventions further demonstrate the necessity of these specialized heads. Ablating only the top 5% of CoRe heads causes significant degradation in multimodal reasoning performance, whereas ablating lower-ranked heads has minimal effect. Moreover, acceleration experiments validate the utility of CoRe heads, showing that leveraging this localized sparsity significantly accelerates inference while maintaining robust task performance. Our findings reveal a structural principle of functional sparsity within MLLMs, refining the current understanding of mechanistic interpretability and laying a theoretical foundation that can inspire future architecture design and model optimization.

</details>

In this work, we investigate whether CS capabilities learned from a limited set of seen language pairs can generalize to unseen language pairs through model merging and domain generalization methods. ### [53] [Forgive or forget: Understanding the context of hate in audio retrieval systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05857)
*Arghya Pal,Sailaja Rajanala,Raphael C. -W. Phan,Shekhar Nayak*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种模型无关的事后因果去偏框架，包含两个变体：Forgive（通过Logit调整进行重排序和过滤）和Forget（通过生成反事实有毒提示词来减轻有害检索）。框架引入了情感控制中介以平衡语义相关性与有害内容抑制。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在显著降低检索内容毒性的同时，仅对检索准确性造成了微小的损失，在安全性和可靠性之间实现了良好的平衡。

Conclusion: 本文提出的事后因果去偏框架通过情感控制中介，有效地解决了文本转音频系统中因上下文依赖带来的有害检索问题，在保持检索准确性的同时显著提升了安全性。

Abstract: Handling toxic retrieval in text-to-audio systems is challenging due to contextual dependencies. Existing strategies (e.g., rephrasing, summarization) risk altering intent or omitting details. We propose a post hoc causal debiasing framework with a sentiment-controlled mediator to preserve semantic relevance while suppressing harmful speech. Our approach is model-agnostic and integrates seamlessly with existing retrieval pipelines. Experiments show consistent toxicity reduction with minimal loss in retrieval accuracy, improving both safety and reliability.

### [54] [ReverseEOL: Improving Training-free Text Embeddings via Text Reversal in Decoder-only LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05858)
*Ailiang Lin,Zhuoyun Li,Yusong Wang,Keyu Mao,Kotaro Funakoshi,Manabu Okumura*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对解码器-仅 LLM 因果注意力机制带来的上下文信息缺失问题，本文提出了 ReverseEOL 方法，通过融合正反向输入生成的 embedding，显著提升了无训练文本嵌入的表示能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的仅解码器（decoder-only）大型语言模型（LLM）由于因果注意力（causal attention）机制的限制，导致前序 token 无法关注到后续的上下文，从而使得生成的无训练文本嵌入存在偏差，表示能力受限。

Method: 提出了一种名为“ReverseEOL（反向提示与显式单词限制）”的方法。该方法通过将输入文本进行反向处理，利用解码器-仅（decoder-only）模型生成反向 embedding，并将其与标准的正向 embedding 进行融合，从而获取原始因果注意力机制无法覆盖的上下文信息。

Result: 在 STS 和 MTEB 基准测试中，ReverseEOL 在多种不同架构和规模的 LLM 上均显著提升了现有无训练基准模型（training-free baselines）的性能。

Conclusion: ReverseEOL 是一种简单且通用的方法，通过结合正向和反向 embedding 有效弥补了仅解码器（decoder-only）架构 LLM 在生成文本嵌入时的信息偏差，显著提升了模型在无训练条件下的语义表示性能。

Abstract: Recent advances in Large Language Models (LLMs) have opened new avenues for generating training-free text embeddings. However, the causal attention in decoder-only LLMs prevents earlier tokens from attending to future context, leading to biased contextualized representations. In this work, we propose Reverse prompting with Explicit One-word Limitation (ReverseEOL), a simple yet effective method for enhancing the representational capability of frozen LLMs. ReverseEOL augments the standard forward embedding with an additional reversed embedding derived from the reversed input text. Since reversing the input exposes each token to context inaccessible in the original order, the resulting reversed embedding effectively provides complementary information to the original one. As a result, combining the forward and reversed embeddings yields a richer final representation. Comprehensive experiments on STS and MTEB benchmarks demonstrate that ReverseEOL significantly improves the performance of existing training-free baselines across a broad range of LLMs with diverse architectures and scales. Extensive ablations and analyses further confirm the necessity of our reversal mechanism.

</details>


### [55] [TARPO: Token-Wise Latent-Explicit Reasoning via Action-Routing Policy Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05859)
*Liting Zhang,Shiwan Zhao,Xuyang Zhao,Zichen Xu,Jianye Wang,Qicheng Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TARPO 是一种新的强化学习框架，允许大模型在每一步动态选择“离散 token 生成”或“连续隐式推理”，有效融合了二者的优势，显著提升了推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管隐式推理（Latent reasoning）在表达能力上优于离散思维链（CoT），但连续表示的确定性限制了强化学习（RL）中的策略探索空间。研究旨在解决如何在大模型中平衡离散 token 生成的随机性和连续隐式推理的表达能力，以提升推理效率和性能。

Method: 提出了 TARPO（Token-Wise Latent-Explicit Reasoning via Action-Routing Policy Optimization）框架。该方法引入了一个轻量级的动作头路由器（Action Head Router），在每一步通过观测隐藏状态来决策是执行离散 token 生成还是连续隐式推理。整个系统采用端到端强化学习进行联合优化，使用组相对优势（group-relative advantage）信号更新 LLM 主干网络和路由器。

Result: 实验表明，在 Qwen2.5 和 Llama-3.1-8B 等多种模型规模上，TARPO 在多个基准测试中均超越了现有的显式和隐式推理强化学习基线。分析显示，该模型能够学习到自适应的 token 级切换行为，并保持训练过程的稳定性。

Conclusion: TARPO 证明了通过结合离散 token 生成和连续隐式推理，可以在强化学习框架下实现更优的推理性能。该方法不仅保留了离散采样的随机性，还有效利用了连续表示的表达能力，为大模型推理优化提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Latent reasoning has emerged as a promising alternative to discrete Chain-of-Thought (CoT) in large language models (LLMs), enabling more expressive reasoning by operating over continuous representations. However, the inherently deterministic nature of continuous representations limits policy exploration in reinforcement learning (RL). To address this, we propose TARPO (Token-Wise Latent-Explicit Reasoning via Action-Routing Policy Optimization), a pure RL framework that adaptively switches between discrete token generation and continuous latent reasoning at each step. TARPO introduces a lightweight action head router that observes the current hidden state and samples a routing decision from a binary mode-selection space, preserving the stochasticity of discrete token sampling from the vocabulary. The LLM backbone and router are jointly optimized end-to-end with a shared group-relative advantage signal. Extensive experiments across Qwen2.5 (from 1.5B to 7B) and Llama-3.1-8B backbones demonstrate that TARPO consistently outperforms existing explicit and latent reasoning RL baselines across diverse benchmarks. Further analysis shows that TARPO learns adaptive token-wise switching behaviors while maintaining stable training dynamics. Our code is available at https://github.com/NKU-LITI/TARPO-master.

</details>


### [56] [Analysis of the Neglect-Zero Effect in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05864)
*Jin Tanaka,Daiki Matsuoka,Ryoma Kumon,Hitomi Yanaka*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究通过结构启动范式调查了大型语言模型是否具备人类的“零忽略效应”。实验结果显示，LLMs并未表现出这种认知偏差，表明其处理逻辑推理的机制与人类存在不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探讨大型语言模型（LLMs）的语言处理过程是否与人类认知过程相似。具体关注人类在推理中常见的一种认知偏差——“零忽略效应”，即人类往往倾向于忽略那些使命题因空集而变得空真（vacuously true）的“零模型”配置。通过这一研究，探究LLMs是否具备人类类似的逻辑偏差。

Method: 研究采用了基于“结构启动”（structural priming）的实验范式。通过设计特定的启动句（prime）引导模型考虑零模型，随后观察模型在处理目标句（target）时是否会受到启动句的影响（即是否会持续考虑零模型），并将其与不涉及零模型的推理行为进行比较，以验证模型是否存在零忽略偏差。

Result: 通过实验对比分析发现，模型在处理目标句时并没有表现出受启动句引导而考虑零模型的迹象。这表明在所考察的LLMs中，零忽略效应并未发生，即模型未表现出与人类一致的逻辑判断倾向。

Conclusion: 本研究的结果表明，大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理包含“零模型”（zero-models）的推理时，并不表现出人类所特有的“零忽略效应”（neglect-zero effect）。这暗示了大型语言模型在处理此类逻辑推理时，其内部处理机制可能与人类的认知过程存在本质差异。

Abstract: We investigate the extent to which the language processing of LLMs resembles human cognitive processes, focusing on a human cognitive bias called the $\textit{neglect-zero effect}$. This effect refers to the human tendency to ignore $\textit{zero-models}$, which are configurations that render a proposition vacuously true by virtue of an empty set. We focus on two types of inferences driven by the neglect-zero effect, and examine how LLMs process these inferences by comparing their behavior with that in an inference that does not involve the neglect-zero effect. For this purpose, we employ a paradigm based on $\textit{structural priming}$, where recent exposure to a preceding sentence (the $\textit{prime}$) facilitates the processing of a subsequent sentence (the $\textit{target}$) due to their structural similarity. We prepare primes to force LLMs to consider the zero-model, and analyze whether they also consider it in the target. The results suggest that the neglect-zero effect may not occur in the LLMs analyzed in this study. Our code is available at https://github.com/ynklab/neglect_zero

</details>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) drive significant financial innovations, yet their high-concurrency deployment is severely bottlenecked by KV cache memory overhead, which inflates infrastructure costs and throttles scalability. To address this, we propose YouZhi-LLM, a highly efficient financial LLM empowered by a comprehensive structural transition and training pipeline natively built on the Huawei Ascend ecosystem. At its algorithmic core, YouZhi-LLM features a layer-adaptive GQA-to-MLA transition framework that dynamically assigns per-layer FreqFold sizes, maximizing KV-cache compression while minimizing perplexity degradation. To recover representation capacity and inject domain expertise, the Ascend-based training pipeline seamlessly integrates generalized knowledge distillation with financial-specific supervised fine-tuning. Evaluations demonstrate the superiority of this systematic approach, with the adaptive transition reducing perplexity degradation by up to 35% over uniform baselines. Crucially, when evaluated on Ascend NPUs via vLLM-Ascend, the massive KV-cache reduction translates directly into deployment efficiency. Compared to their respective base models, YouZhi-7B yields a 12.3% improvement in average financial benchmark score alongside a 2.69$\times$ increase in maximum concurrency; similarly, YouZhi-14B achieves a 7.0% accuracy gain and a 2.43$\times$ concurrency boost, establishing a new paradigm for cost-effective, high-throughput financial inference.

### [58] [Evaluating Stochastic Collapse and Implicit Bias in Multimodal Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05874)
*Huiyuan Zheng,Houtao Zhang,Boyang Wang,Qingyi Si,Hongcheng Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了RandomBench基准，揭示了多模态大模型在面临等效选项时，无法维持随机分布，普遍存在“随机性崩溃”现象，且该偏差在不同语言和格式下表现顽固。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM评估过于关注 utility（实用性），忽视了逻辑中立场景下的行为表现。在旅行规划或日程安排等存在多个等效选择的场景中，确定性策略会导致行为重复且缺乏多样性，因此需要评估模型是否具备维持分布中立行为的能力。

Method: 1. 提出了RandomBench基准测试，专门用于评估MLLM在多个等效选项间的随机选择能力；2. 定义了三个评估指标：随机性指数（RI）、偏差一致性指数（BCI）和偏差不一致性指数（BII），以量化模型的熵和分布偏差。

Result: 实验发现“随机性崩溃”现象普遍存在：即使在明确指令要求随机选择时，模型的选择概率严重偏离均匀分布，例如Claude Sonnet 4.6的Top-1概率高达97%（理想应为25%），且随机性指数（RI）低至0.068。此外，这种偏差在不同语言和表现形式下均具有鲁棒性。

Conclusion: MLLMs在逻辑中立场景下普遍存在“随机性崩溃”现象，即模型难以维持预期的随机分布，表现出明显的偏好偏差。该研究揭示了现有模型在开放式决策任务中缺乏真正的多样性，为评估和改进MLLM的决策公平性与多样性提供了重要基准。

Abstract: Current evaluations for Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) overwhelmingly focus on utility-driven objectives, leaving model behavior under logic-neutral scenarios largely underexplored. Stochasticity is essential in scenarios where multiple actions are equally valid, such as recommending travel itineraries or daily schedules where multiple options have similar utility. In such settings, deterministic policies may lead to repetitive behaviors and reduced coverage of valid alternatives. To bridge this gap, we propose RandomBench, a benchmark designed to evaluate whether MLLMs can maintain distributionally neutral behavior when selecting among equivalent options. We further introduce three metrics, including RI, BCI, BII, to quantify entropy and distributional bias. Experiments reveal a pervasive phenomenon termed Stochastic Collapse, where MLLMs fail to maintain uniform randomness under explicit random instructions, with top-1 probabilities reaching 97% from the ideal one quarter baseline and RI dropping to 0.068 in Claude Sonnet 4.6. Extensive ablation studies further demonstrate that these deviations persist across languages and representation formats, highlighting the robustness of distributional collapse in logic-neutral decision settings.

### [59] [Staying with the Uncertainty: Uncertainty-Scaffolding Strategies for Artificial Moral Advisors in LLM-to-LLM Simulated Conversations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05890)
*Salvatore Greco,Hainiu Xu,Jacopo Domenicucci,Yulan He,Sylvie Delacroix*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探索了人工智能道德顾问如何通过“保持不确定性”策略来优化道德困境对话，发现这些策略虽不直接改变用户立场，但显著提升了对话质量和参与度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）正日益被用作人工智能道德顾问（AMA），但目前的模型往往倾向于给出单一、确定的建议。该研究旨在探索如何通过特定对话模式，引导用户“保持不确定性”，从而更好地处理复杂的道德困境。

Method: 研究者设计了三种不确定性策略（透视倍增、张力保持、过程反思）作为AMA的干预手段，并与三种控制条件（基准、说服型、奉承型）进行对比。通过用户与采用不同策略的LLM进行道德困境对话，并结合对话前后的问卷调查，评估了不同策略及两种角色提示格式（声明式与叙事式）对对话效果和用户信念的影响。

Result: (1) 没有单一的模型在模拟用户代理中占据主导地位，开源模型通过跨角色分歧实现模糊性，闭源模型通过单一角色内的避险（hedging）实现；(2) 声明式角色设定更利于捕捉初始立场的多元性，叙事式角色设定则能展现更真实的信念修正；(3) 六种AMA策略产生的对话模式具有显著差异；(4) 不确定性策略的主要价值在于维持更高质量的互动参与度，而非单纯改变用户的立场。

Conclusion: 研究表明，人工智能道德顾问（AMA）不应仅仅追求说服用户，而应通过特定的不确定性策略（如透视倍增、张力保持和过程反思）来提升对话质量。研究揭示了模型类型、角色设定方式（声明式 vs. 叙事式）以及对话策略对道德决策对话互动的具体影响，强调了在道德领域中“保持不确定性”的重要性。

Abstract: LLMs are increasingly deployed as Artificial Moral Advisors (AMA) in a variety of contexts: what kind of conversational patterns should they display? In this paper, we study how AMA can help their interlocutors "stay with the uncertainty". We propose three modes of uncertainty (Perspective-Multiplying, Tension-Preserving, Process-Reflecting) and compare them against three control conditions (Baseline, Persuasive, Sycophantic). A user-agent LLM engages in a dialogue on an ethical dilemma with an AMA following a specific uncertainty strategy, and completes pre- and post-conversation questionnaires. We further examine the effect of two persona prompt formats (Declarative and Narrative). We found that (1) no single model dominates as a simulated user agent, with open models aligning with human ambiguity through between-persona divergence and closed models through within-persona hedging; (2) declarative personas better capture initial stance diversity while narrative personas show more realistic belief revision; (3) all six AMA strategies produce distinguishable conversational patterns; and (4) uncertainty strategies differ not in how much stance revision they produce, but in the quality of engagement they sustain.

</details>


### [60] [EMBER: Efficient Memory via Budgeted Evidence Retention for Long-Horizon Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05894)
*Yilong Li,Suman Banerjee,Tong Che*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对长时记忆任务中内存预算有限的问题，本文提出了EMBER模型。通过学习型策略智能地将原始历史压缩为“证据胶囊”，在受限预算下实现了远超传统方法的证据保留效果，显著提升了后续检索与问答的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在处理长时程任务时，受限于Token预算，智能体无法完全保留所有原始历史记录。当内存中缺乏相关信息时，检索整个原始文档会带来巨大的计算成本和延迟。因此，研究如何在已知查询前，以有限的预算保留最具价值的证据，成为提升长时记忆效率的关键。

Method: 提出了EMBER（Evidence-backed Memory-Based Evidence Retention），这是一种学习型的证据留存策略。该方法在信息摄入阶段将源文档转化为“证据胶囊”（证据原文、检索键和元数据的组合），并利用后查询结果反馈进行训练，从而在有限的Token预算下优化证据的留存效果。

Result: 在LongMemEval-RR基准测试中，EMBER-14B模型在8192个Token的预算下达到了0.3017的F1分数，显著优于最强的非EMBER基线模型（0.1765）。实验表明，该方法在提升F1、检索召回率（Retain-Recall）和读取召回率（Read-Recall）方面均表现优异。

Conclusion: EMBER证明了通过学习型策略进行预算化的预查询证据留存，能够有效提升长时记忆智能体在受限上下文窗口下的信息检索与推理能力，优于传统的简单保留方法。

Abstract: Long-horizon agents can archive large histories, but future answers still incur retrieval, rereading, and context costs. When retained memory misses answer-relevant evidence, the system must return to larger portions of the raw history. We study budgeted evidence survival: before the query is known, which source evidence should be retained so that it remains recoverable and usable under a fixed retained source-evidence token budget? We instantiate this setting as Budgeted Pre-Query Retention, where memory is written during ingestion and later read without access to the full raw stream. We introduce EMBER, a learned retention policy that constructs a compact, source-backed evidence state. EMBER stores evidence capsules: verbatim source excerpts paired with retrieval keys and update metadata, preserving both grounding and read-time access. Post-query outcome feedback trains the writer to preserve evidence across the ingestion-retrieval-answer chain. On LongMemEval-RR, our LongMemEval-derived retained-evidence protocol, EMBER-14B reaches 0.3017 F1 at the 8192-token retained-evidence comparison point, compared with 0.1765 for the strongest non-EMBER budgeted baseline. Across retained source-evidence budgets, EMBER improves F1, Retain-Recall, and Read-Recall, indicating that long-horizon memory depends on retaining evidence within the budget rather than rereading larger histories.

</details>


### [61] [Representing Research Attention as Contextually Structured Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05895)
*Jessica Rodrigues,Angelo Salatino,Gard Jenset,Scott Hale*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对传统学术关注度指标缺乏时空结构信息的问题，本文提出“关注度流”模型，通过捕捉关注度的动态演变和情境特征，提供了一种更稳健、更具解释力的科研评价新范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的学术关注度多以聚合指标（如被引频次）呈现，忽视了关注度随时间在不同情境下的演变过程，导致关注度的解读与呈现之间存在错位，因此需要一种能保留时空演变结构的表征方法。

Method: 提出了“关注度流”（Attention Flows）概念，将其作为一种编码关注度组织方式及其随时间演变的结构化表征。通过构建基于类比推理（Analogy-style reasoning）的基准测试，对比了信号、序列和基于流的表征，并验证了其在部分观测和结构扰动下的稳健性。

Result: 实验结果显示，“关注度流”表征在支持结构化比较方面表现更优，尤其是在受时间演变或情境分布影响的场景中；此外，这种方法在面临部分数据缺失或结构扰动时具有更高的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了将学术关注度建模为“情境化结构”的有效性，并提出“关注度流”是一种更具鲁棒性和信息量的研究评价表征方法，为理解学术影响力的演变提供了新视角。

Abstract: Research attention is widely used as an indicator of visibility, influence, and societal uptake, yet it is typically represented as aggregated counts that do not preserve how attention develops across contexts over time. This creates a mismatch between how attention is interpreted and how it is represented. We propose attention flows as contextually structured representations that encode the organisation of attention and its evolution over time. We evaluate whether these representations capture transferable structure by constructing a benchmark based on analogy-style reasoning across research outputs. Comparing signal, sequence, and flow-based representations, we find that flow representations more effectively support structural comparison, particularly in settings where attention is shaped by temporal progression or context distributions. We further show that learned flow representations improve robustness under partial observation and structural perturbation. Overall, these results support modelling attention as a contextually structured phenomenon and provide a basis for more informative approaches to research evaluation.

</details>


### [62] [Reducing Hallucinations in Complex Question Answering using Simple Graph-based Retrieval-Augmented Generation (long version)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05901)
*Christopher J. Wedge,Joshua Stutter,Danny Dixon,Jacek Cała*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出在RAG系统中集成轻量级图结构工具，通过向量搜索与图查询的协同作用，显著降低了大模型问答中的幻觉现象，提升了复杂问答任务的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）虽强大但易产生幻觉，且无法直接处理训练数据之外的私有知识。现有的检索增强生成（RAG）方案仍存在局限性，作者旨在通过引入轻量级图结构来弥补纯向量检索的不足，以提高模型处理复杂问题时的真实性和准确性。

Method: 作者设计了一个代理（Agentic）系统，结合了传统的向量搜索和专门针对轻量级图结构的图查询工具。该系统在经过整理的英语维基百科子集上进行构建，并利用MoNaCo基准测试集对复杂问答任务的效果进行评估。

Result: 实验结果表明，引入图工具后，系统在事实正确性方面的精确率和召回率显著提升，幻觉现象减少了一半，且在细粒度真实性得分上取得了最高分，同时token消耗量的增加幅度在可控范围内。

Conclusion: 通过在RAG系统中引入轻量级图结构和对应的查询工具，可以显著提升问答系统的准确性和真实性，有效抑制幻觉问题，同时保持较低的算力成本，证明了结构化知识图谱与大语言模型结合的巨大潜力。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have fundamentally transformed the landscape of Natural Language Processing. Despite these advances, LLMs and LLM-based systems remain prone to a variety of failure modes. Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems have emerged as a common deployment scenario seeking to both avoid the well known risk of the LLM "hallucinating" information, and to enable reasoning and question answering over proprietary information that the LLM did not have access to during training without resorting to expensive model fine-tuning.
  In this work, we explore the idea of using a lightweight graph structure with a relatively simple graph schema, to support the RAG subsystem via a dedicated toolset. We design an agentic system with a variety of vector search and graph query tools operating over a structured dataset based on a curated subset of English Wikipedia articles, and evaluate its performance on questions from MoNaCo, a challenging Wikipedia QA benchmark of complex query answering tasks.
  Our results show that the introduction of graph-based tools can significantly increase the precision and recall of factual correctness, can halve the number of hallucinated answers, and achieves the highest fine-grained truthfulness score among the three evaluated scenarios. All this with a modest increase in token usage.

### [63] [ACE-SQL: Adaptive Co-Optimization via Empirical Credit Assignment for Text-to-SQL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05906)
*Xiaobing Chen,Ai Jian,Eryu Guo,Zhiqi Pang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ACE-SQL 是一种通过强化学习实现模式检索器与 SQL 生成器协同优化的新框架，它利用执行反馈动态调整检索目标，有效解决了复杂模式下的 Text-to-SQL 难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 Text-to-SQL 方法在处理大规模复杂数据库时存在不足：一是全模式生成方式导致搜索空间过大；二是采用独立的检索器进行静态监督训练，导致检索出的模式与生成器当前的生成能力不匹配，限制了执行精度。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ACE-SQL 的强化学习框架，核心机制是“基于经验信度分配的自适应协同优化”。该方法通过生成器在线采样构建候选列池，并利用执行成功的样本动态更新检索器的优化目标，从而实现检索器与生成器的双向适应（Bidirectional Adaptation）。

Result: ACE-SQL 在 BIRD Dev 数据集上达到了 65.3% 的执行准确率，且平均每个查询仅需 0.93k 输出 token，在保持高效率的同时实现了性能的显著提升。

Conclusion: ACE-SQL 证明了在 Text-to-SQL 任务中，通过强化学习将模式检索器与 SQL 生成器进行联合协同优化，能够显著提升模型在复杂数据库上的执行准确率。这种基于执行反馈的动态目标调整机制，解决了传统静态监督学习带来的检索目标与生成策略不匹配的问题。

Abstract: Text-to-SQL maps natural language questions to executable SQL queries. Modern databases often contain large and complex schemas, making schema linking a critical step for accurate SQL generation. Existing methods either rely on full-schema generation, which leaves schema linking implicit within a large search space, or use a separate retriever trained with static gold-column supervision, whose targets may be suboptimal for the current generator policy. To address this issue, we propose Adaptive Co-optimization via Empirical Credit Assignment for Text-to-SQL (ACE-SQL), a reinforcement learning (RL) framework that jointly optimizes schema retrieval and SQL generation under execution feedback. ACE-SQL constructs an online column-set pool from generator rollouts and derives adaptive on-policy retrieval targets from the column set most frequently associated with execution-correct rollouts. This induces bidirectional adaptation, where the retriever adapts toward column sets that the generator can execute correctly, while the generator adapts to the retriever's evolving schema selections under execution feedback. With approximately 3k synthetic Text-to-SQL question-database pairs for RL training, ACE-SQL achieves 65.3% greedy execution accuracy on BIRD Dev while using 0.93k output tokens per query. The repository is available at https://github.com/xbchen1/ACE-SQL.

</details>


### [64] [Better Literary Translation: A Multi-Aspect Data Generation and LLM Training Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05924)
*Zhihao Lin,Ziqi Zhu,Hao Huang,Guanghui Wang,Peiyang He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对文学翻译数据稀缺难题，本文通过多维度LLM协同生成高质量偏好数据，结合SFT与GRPO强化学习训练，打造出性能比肩顶级商用模型的开源文学翻译模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文学翻译面临高质量标注数据稀缺的挑战，且需在表达流畅度与文学效果之间取得平衡，现有方法难以有效处理这一复杂需求。

Method: 提出了一种多维度迭代优化框架：1. 使用针对不同质量维度的专业化LLM生成高质量翻译参考及偏好数据；2. 使用生成的数据进行监督微调（SFT）；3. 比较了直接偏好优化（DPO）与显式奖励建模的群体相对策略优化（GRPO），发现GRPO效果更好。

Result: 生成的参考翻译在SFT中使CEA100得分提升8.65点；GRPO相较DPO进一步提升了1.51点；LitMT-8B和14B模型在MetaphorTrans基准测试上分别达到67.25和69.07分，媲美Claude Sonnet 4.5，并展现出良好的跨领域泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的多维度迭代优化框架显著提升了文学翻译质量，证明了高质量合成数据及特定奖励建模方法（GRPO）在文学翻译任务中的有效性，使小型模型在文学翻译表现上达到与顶尖闭源大模型相当的水平。

Abstract: Literary translation poses unique challenges due to the scarcity of high-quality annotated data and the need to balance expression fluency with literary effect. We present a multi-aspect iterative refinement framework that generates high-quality translation references and preference data through specialized LLM translators, each targeting a distinct quality dimension. We leverage the generated data for supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning. Experiments show that our generated references outperform the original ground truth for SFT by 8.65 CEA100 points. For reinforcement learning, we find that DPO leads to performance degradation in this setting, while leveraging an explicit reward model for GRPO yields an additional 1.51 point improvement. We attribute this to the stability of two-stage training and GRPO's online exploration capability. Our resulting models, LitMT-8B and LitMT-14B, achieve 67.25 and 69.07 CEA100 respectively on the MetaphorTrans English-to-Chinese literary translation benchmark, competitive with Claude Sonnet 4.5 at 68.43, and demonstrate strong generalization to out-of-domain literary work (i.e., O. Henry).

### [65] [Epistemic Injustice in Language Models: An Audit of Pretraining Filters and Guardrails](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05936)
*Marco Antonio Stranisci,A Pranav,Rossana Damiano,Christian Hardmeier,Anne Lauscher*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了语言模型内容审核系统存在系统性偏见，它们未能准确识别有害信息，反而对边缘化群体的提及内容进行过度审查，导致了“认知抹除”现象。系统判定与人类判断高度不一致，现有的黑名单驱动模式急需改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨现代语言模型在预训练数据过滤和推理阶段的内容审核机制，分析这些机制如何导致“认知抹除”（epistemic erasure），以及自动化审查系统与人类价值观之间存在的冲突。

Method: 研究者对四个预训练过滤器和三个推理时护栏系统进行了审计。评估基于包含性别和区域来源提及的Common Crawl数据集，并辅以一个包含500条句子的手动标注子集，旨在对比自动化系统的判定结果与人类注释者的判断差异。

Result: 分析发现，过滤机制高度依赖词汇黑名单，导致隐私信息和显性仇恨言论被遗漏，同时显著高估了针对边缘化群体的中性或正面内容。人类评估员认为这些被系统标记的语句中，有88.5%的过滤内容和91.3%的护栏内容应被保留，说明当前系统未能理解复杂的人类表征危害与语境。

Conclusion: 研究表明，现有的过滤与审核系统在处理敏感内容时表现出明显的偏差，不仅无法有效识别真正的仇恨言论，反而通过“认知抹除”机制，对边缘化群体（如跨性别者、女性及中美洲人）的内容进行了不合理的过度过滤。这暴露了当前内容审查技术在处理复杂社会背景和人类价值观时的局限性。

Abstract: Modern language models rely on pretraining filters to remove undesirable content from training corpora and inference-time guardrails to suppress undesirable outputs during deployment. In this paper, we examine how these filtering and moderation decisions produce forms of epistemic erasure and reveal tensions both across automated systems and between these systems and human judgment. We audit four pretraining filters and three inference-time guardrails on Common Crawl sentences containing gender and regional-origin mentions, together with a manually annotated subset of 500 sentences. Our analysis shows that filtering and guardrail decisions are strongly associated with blocklist-based lexical cues, while frequently failing to flag content containing private information or explicit hate speech. At the same time, marginalized groups, particularly transgender people, women, and Central Americans, are significantly over-flagged across systems. Human annotators, by contrast, would retain 88.5\% of filter-flagged and 91.3\% of guardrail-flagged content, often recognizing representational harms arising from tensions of content removal that current systems fail to capture. Taken together, our findings document a form of epistemic erasure in which mentions of marginalized groups are disproportionately removed before pretraining and additionally suppressed again at inference time.

</details>


### [66] [Large Language Models are Perplexed by some Political Parties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05937)
*Paul Lerner,François Yvon*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了大型语言模型普遍存在政治偏见：它们对极右翼及民族主义政党文本的理解难度更高（表现为更高的困惑度），且这种偏见主要源于预训练阶段，无法通过后续的指令微调消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在政治领域的应用日益广泛，但学术界对其政治公平性缺乏深入研究。本文旨在揭示LLMs在处理不同政治倾向文本时是否存在偏见，并探讨这种偏见的来源。

Method: 研究人员使用“困惑度”（Perplexity）作为评估政治公平性的指标，假设一个公平的模型应对所有政治派别的文本赋予相等的概率。通过评估10个大型语言模型在37种语言的3个数据集上的表现，量化模型对不同政治倾向文本的理解难度。

Result: 实验发现，LLMs对极右翼和民族主义政党文本的困惑度普遍高于社会民主党派。这种政治偏见与翻译公平性存在显著相关性，且该结论适用于基础模型（Base LLMs）和经过指令微调的模型，表明偏见主要来源于预训练数据。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型在政治公平性方面存在系统性偏见。这种偏见根植于预训练阶段，且指令微调（Instruction-tuning）难以有效消除或改善这种偏差。未来在训练阶段需要更加注重语料的多样性与平衡性。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used, including in political applications, but their political fairness has been little studied. We assess it using perplexity, posing that a fair model should give equal probability to all political groups. However, we find, across ten LLMs and three datasets covering 37 languages, that LLMs are more perplexed by the texts of far right and nationalist parties than of social-democratic parties. We find this to be consistent with previous work on translation fairness, to the point that perplexity correlates with downstream translation metrics. Our method is applicable to both base LLMs as well as their instruction-tuned counterpart, and we find that both are highly correlated, suggesting that the political fairness of LLMs stems from their pretraining, and is hardly affected by instruction-tuning.

### [67] [Measuring the sensitivity of LLM-based structured extraction to prompt, model, and schema choices in clinical discharge summaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05970)
*Martin Murin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种无需人工标注的评估框架，发现大语言模型在临床提取任务中的不一致性主要源于模式定义的语义模糊（如区分“缺失”与“未记录”）以及模型架构的选择，而非提示词的措辞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在临床文本结构化提取中应用广泛，但目前缺乏对其输出在不同配置（如提示词、模型大小）下敏感性的深入理解。现有研究多关注固定基准测试的准确率，而忽略了实际部署中配置选择对提取可重复性的影响。

Method: 该研究采用“固定提取任务、变量控制法”进行评估，无需人工标注基准。具体方法包括：使用三个版本的提示词和两个不同规模的模型对MIMIC-IV v3.1出院总结进行提取；通过Cohen's kappa系数度量跨提示词的一致性；对比模型对同一笔记的提取差异；以及通过将三分类标签压缩为二分类来分析模式（schema）对不一致性的贡献。

Result: 1. 在三分类临床标志提取中，模型规模的改变导致了一致性分布的重组而非绝对提升；2. 将三分类折叠为二分类后，大部分跨提示词的不一致性消失，说明分歧主要集中在“缺失”与“不记录”的判断上；3. 在多分类任务中，改变模型会导致约一半笔记的主导标签变更，而改变提示词仅影响约八分之一，且较大模型在“其他”类别的分配上更为谨慎。

Conclusion: 研究表明，临床信息提取的不一致性主要源于模式定义中的“缺失”与“不记录”之间的语义模糊，而非简单的提取错误。在大规模临床部署中，相比提示词工程，模型本身的选择对分类任务的影响更为决定性。该研究提供了一种无需人工标注即可评估模型提取稳定性的可复用方法。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly used for structured extraction from clinical free-text notes, but the sensitivity of their output to upstream configuration choices is less understood than their accuracy on fixed benchmarks. This work measures that sensitivity without human-annotated ground truth, by holding the extraction task fixed and varying one choice at a time. The fixed schema comprises 17 clinical documentation flags on a three-way yes/no/not_documented value set and a 47-tag vocabulary for the primary admission reason. Three prompt variants expressing this schema were each run at two model sizes on MIMIC-IV v3.1 discharge summaries. Cross-prompt agreement was measured by Cohen's kappa on ICD-stratified subsets. A paired same-note comparison isolated the effect of model choice, and a post-hoc collapse of the three-way flags to binary tested the schema's contribution to disagreement. On the three-way flags, the two models reach the same pooled cross-prompt agreement (median kappa 0.69 and 0.68); the larger model raises agreement on some fields and lowers it on others, a redistribution rather than the absence of an effect. Collapsing the schema to binary dissolves most of the cross-prompt disagreement, locating it on the absence-versus-silence distinction rather than on whether the finding is present. On the multi-class admission categorization, changing the model reassigns the dominant tag on close to half of all notes while changing the prompt phrasing reassigns it on roughly one in eight, and the larger model places far less mass on residual catch-all categories (44% to 26%). These patterns indicate a schema-imposed source of disagreement concentrated on the absence-versus-silence axis and a dominance of model over prompt phrasing on multi-class categorization, identified by a reusable methodology for auditing extraction reproducibility on a population-scale deployment.

### [68] [Beyond Alignment: Value Diversity as a Collective Property in Multicultural Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05985)
*Shaoyang Xu,Jingshen Zhang,Long P. Hoang,Jinyuan Li,Wenxuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出“价值多样性”作为多智能体系统的新评价指标，研究发现当前大语言模型驱动的智能体社会存在明显的同质化倾向，且社会互动会进一步削弱多样性，导致集体决策范围变窄。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体文化评价过度关注“价值对齐”（即单智能体与特定文化的匹配度），忽略了系统整体是否保留了应有的文化多元性。作者旨在填补这一空白，提出并验证一个能反映多智能体系统整体文化多样性的评价框架。

Method: 研究人员提出使用“价值多样性”作为系统级评价维度，通过计算不同文化背景智能体在共享价值调查（基于世界价值观调查）中响应的差异性来衡量。实验涵盖了19种文化和18种底层模型，并进行了多种系统配置测试，包括评估单一模型与混合模型系统，以及分析社会互动对多样性的影响。

Result: 1. 价值多样性与价值对齐之间几乎没有相关性，两者代表不同的系统特性；2. 当前的多元文化智能体系统在价值多样性上远低于人类社会；3. 采用混合底层模型的系统虽能略微提升多样性，但无法填补与人类社会的差距；4. 社会互动会促使智能体趋同，导致决策过程中的集体同质化，缩小了集体决策的广度。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了“价值多样性”作为多元文化多智能体系统的重要评价指标，并揭示了当前基于大语言模型的智能体社会存在显著的同质化倾向。研究强调，仅关注单智能体的“价值对齐”是不够的，必须在系统层面重视并维护文化多样性。

Abstract: Multicultural multi-agent systems are increasingly deployed in globally diverse settings, where different agents are grounded in different cultural backgrounds. Existing cultural evaluation focuses on value alignment: how closely a single agent matches a target culture. Yet alignment is a per-agent property and cannot reveal whether a system, taken as a whole, preserves the cultural plurality it is meant to represent. We propose value diversity as a system-level evaluation axis for multicultural agent systems, defined through the dissimilarity between culturally conditioned agents' responses on a shared value survey. Using the World Values Survey, we evaluate 19 cultures and 18 backbone models across a wide range of system configurations. We find that diversity is largely uncorrelated with alignment, indicating that the two capture complementary system properties, and that current multicultural agent systems fall substantially below human societies in value diversity. Mixed-backbone systems narrow this gap but do not close it, and the gap persists across culture compositions and agent scales. Social interaction further erodes diversity by driving agents toward consensus, and a participatory budgeting case study shows that this homogenization narrows the breadth of collective decision-making. Together, our results establish value diversity as a distinct evaluation axis for multicultural multi-agent systems and reveal a persistent homogenization tendency in current LLM-based societies. Our code and data are publicly available at https://github.com/iNLP-Lab/MultiAgent-Diversity.

</details>


### [69] [The Generator-Eraser Paradox: Community Guidelines for Responsible LLM-Assisted Dialect Resource Creation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06004)
*Wajdi Zaghouani*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探讨了大语言模型在方言资源开发中的双刃剑效应，提出了“生成者-抹除者悖论”理论框架及12项操作指南，以帮助社区在利用AI技术的同时，保护方言的真实性和多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型（LLM）虽能加速方言资源开发（如辅助标注、元数据丰富等），但也可能通过强化优势语言变体、同质化拼写等方式加剧方言消失，导致语言多样性减损。研究旨在解决这一矛盾，为方言资源建设提供规范框架。

Method: 1. 理论构建：借鉴社会语言学变异论和语料库语言学，形式化“生成者-抹除者悖论”（Generator-Eraser Paradox）；2. 指南制定：推导出12条社区导向的实操设计指南；3. 案例分析：以阿拉伯语方言为对象进行深入研究，对比现有资源并验证指南的适用性。

Result: 研究明确了“生成者-抹除者悖论”，提出了12项可落地的方言资源开发与归档设计要求，并通过阿拉伯语方言案例展示了这些准则如何应对双层语言现象、拼写变异及社区治理等挑战。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架与指南为方言社区和资源构建者提供了方法论支持，旨在平衡大语言模型在方言资源开发中的加速作用与对语言多样性的保护，强调在技术应用中维护方言真实性、变体多样性及社区治理的重要性。

Abstract: Dialect resources occupy a unique position at the intersection of scientific description, cultural preservation, and computational infrastructure. Large language models offer powerful capabilities for accelerating dialect resource development through retrieval-grounded drafting, corpus navigation, metadata enrichment, and annotation workflow support. However, the same systems pose substantial risks: they can contribute to dialect erasure by privileging prestige varieties, homogenizing orthography, and enabling synthetic feedback loops that reduce linguistic diversity over time. These risks are particularly acute for language varieties characterized by diglossia, limited written standardization, or marginalized speaker communities. This paper makes three contributions. First, we integrate insights from variationist sociolinguistics and corpus linguistics to formalize the generator-eraser paradox as a theoretical framework for understanding the dual nature of LLM-assisted dialect work. Second, we derive 12 community guidelines that operationalize this framework into implementable design requirements for dialect resource creation and documentation. Third, we provide an in-depth case study of Arabic dialects, including a structured comparison of widely used resources, to demonstrate how these guidelines address language-specific challenges including diglossia, orthographic variability, and community governance. The contribution is conceptual and operational rather than experimental, with the goal of enabling dialect communities and resource builders across languages to adopt LLMs without sacrificing authenticity, variation, or sovereignty.

</details>


### [70] [Contextualized Prompting For Stance Detection On Social Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06022)
*Tilman Beck,Shakib Yazdani,Simon Kruschinski,Marcus Maurer,Iryna Gurevych*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了如何利用上下文信息提升大模型在社交媒体上的零样本立场检测能力，发现只有高质量的LLM生成目标描述能稳定提升效果，而过多的噪声上下文（如用户历史推文）反而会损害性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社交媒体文本具有短小、噪声大且极度依赖上下文的特点。现有的零样本大语言模型提示方法往往缺乏对这些上下文信息的有效整合，导致其在处理含糊不清的推文时性能受限，亟需探索如何通过引入外部上下文来提升立场检测的准确性。

Method: 作者系统性地研究了将不同类型的上下文特征融入大模型（LLM）零样本提示词的方法。这些特征包括：1. 现实世界数据（如用户个人简介）；2. 衍生数据（如政治倾向）；3. LLM生成数据（如目标描述）。研究在四个基准数据集（含一个新建的德语推特数据集）上进行了广泛评估，并对比了不同上下文来源对立场检测性能的具体影响。

Result: 实验表明，并非所有上下文都有益：只有LLM生成的目标描述能持续提升准确率；包含用户元数据的影响不稳定甚至有害；引入用户其他推文往往会因输入噪声过大而降低模型性能。定性分析发现，LLM目前难以区分哪些上下文信息对于特定立场检测任务是有用的，哪些是无关干扰。

Conclusion: 在大规模语言模型进行零样本立场检测时，上下文信息的引入是一把双刃剑。虽然经过精心设计的模型生成目标描述能够稳定提升效果，但盲目添加用户元数据或同用户历史推文反而可能因为噪声干扰而损害模型性能。研究强调了在处理社交媒体噪声数据时，筛选有效上下文信息的必要性。

Abstract: Stance detection on social media is challenging due to short, noisy, and context-dependent language. While large language models (LLMs) show zero-shot generalization, they are typically prompted without contextual information, which limits their ability to interpret ambiguous posts. In this work, we systematically investigate the impact of incorporating real-world (e.g., user biographies), derived (e.g., political party), and LLM-generated (e.g., target descriptions) contextual features into zero-shot prompting for stance detection on Twitter. Our evaluation spans four benchmark datasets, including a new high-quality German Twitter stance dataset. Across multiple LLMs, we find that integrating contextual information improves performance, but only under specific conditions. LLM-generated target descriptions consistently enhance accuracy, while other user metadata has mixed or even detrimental effects. Notably, we show that the inclusion of other tweets by the same user, often beneficial in supervised learning, can impair performance due to input noise. Our qualitative analysis reveals that LLMs struggle to distinguish task-specific useful information from irrelevant context. Our findings highlight both the promise and challenges of prompting with context information in noisy real-world settings. We publish code and data at this \href{https://github.com/tilmanbeck/stance-context-twitter}{page}.

### [71] [EGTR-Review: Efficient Evidence-Grounded Scientific Peer Review Generation via Multi-Agent Teacher Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06025)
*Xinpeng Qiu,Wang Yihu,Zhifeng Liu,Xiaochen Wang,Jimin Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了 EGTR-Review，一种通过多智能体蒸馏实现证据充分、来源可查且低成本的自动论文审稿生成框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型（LLM）的审稿方法存在评价笼统、缺乏证据支持、溯源性弱以及复杂多智能体系统推理成本过高等问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 EGTR-Review 的框架：首先构建一个包含结构化拆解、关键元素提取、外部证据检索、验证推理等多阶段的多智能体教师系统；随后通过任务前缀驱动的多任务学习，将教师模型的推理轨迹和最终反馈蒸馏至轻量级学生模型，并结合证据加权目标函数优化训练。

Result: 在公开评审数据集上的实验表明，EGTR-Review 的学生模型在自动指标、LLM 判分及人工评估中均优于基线模型，同时显著降低了 Token 消耗和推理时间，并保持了良好的事实基础和来源可追溯性。

Conclusion: EGTR-Review 通过多智能体教师蒸馏，成功构建了一个既具备事实依据和来源可追溯性，又具有高效推理能力的轻量级审稿生成模型，为解决现有 LLM 审稿工具在成本与质量之间的矛盾提供了一种有效的范式。

Abstract: Scientific peer review generation has attracted increasing attention for reducing reviewing burdens and providing timely feedback. However, existing Large Language Model (LLM)-based methods often produce generic comments with insufficient evidence support and weak source traceability, while complex multi-agent systems incur high inference costs. To address these challenges, we propose EGTR-Review, an Evidence-Grounded and Traceable Review Generation framework via Multi-Agent Teacher Distillation. EGTR-Review first constructs a multi-agent teacher that performs structure-aware paper decomposition, key-element extraction, external scholarly evidence retrieval, evidence-state labeling, verification reasoning, and review synthesis. It then distills both intermediate reasoning trajectories and final review comments into a lightweight student model through task-prefix-driven multi-task learning. An evidence-weighted objective further reduces the influence of weak, missing, or non-verifiable supervision. Experiments on public peer-review datasets show that EGTR-Review (Student) outperforms strong prompt-based, fine-tuned, and structured/agentic baselines across automatic metrics, LLM-as-Judge evaluation, and human evaluation, while maintaining strong factual grounding and source traceability with substantially lower token consumption and inference time. Our code, prompts, configurations, and sample data are available on GitHub.

### [72] [NAVIRA: Decoupled Stochastic Remasking for Masked Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06031)
*Andrey Fomenko,Maksim Kryzhanovskiy,Svetlana Glazyrina,Roman Ischenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对掩码扩散语言模型中重掩码过程的耦合问题，本文提出了 NAVIRA 推理策略，通过将令牌质量评估与重生成过程解耦，并结合随机重掩码机制，有效解决了错误上下文污染问题，提升了生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有掩码扩散语言模型（如 PRISM）在推理时存在“纠正问题”，即用于检测低质量令牌和生成替换令牌的过程耦合在同一次前向传播中，导致错误的令牌仍会作为后续生成的上下文条件，造成错误传播。

Method: 提出了一种名为 NAVIRA 的推理时解码策略：1. 解耦机制：将令牌质量评估（评分）与令牌重生成过程分为两次独立的前向传播，避免错误令牌污染上下文；2. 随机重掩码：采用温度控制的随机策略来确定需要重掩码的位置，以平衡生成文本的流畅度与多样性。

Result: 在 1.7 亿参数的模型上进行的实验表明，NAVIRA 的解耦机制显著提升了生成文本的流畅度；通过调度随机重掩码策略，在保证熵值（多样性）的同时，获得了更高的 LLM-judge 评分。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在掩码扩散语言模型中，重掩码策略（remasking policy）与模型学习到的质量信号同样重要。通过将检测与重生成过程解耦，并引入随机性调度，可以有效提升生成文本的质量与多样性。

Abstract: Masked diffusion language models generate text by iteratively unmasking many tokens in parallel, but this speed comes with a correction problem: tokens generated in the same step are predicted from marginal distributions, and early local dependency errors can later contaminate the context. PRISM addresses this by learning token-level quality scores and remasking unreliable tokens, but its inference rule is coupled: the same forward pass both detects low-quality tokens and computes logits for their replacements, so the erroneous tokens still condition regeneration. We propose NAVIRA, an inference-time decoding policy that separates these two operations and samples remasking positions stochastically. A first forward pass scores tokens; selected tokens are masked; a second forward pass regenerates from the cleaned context. Temperature-controlled remasking reduces repeated correction of the same positions and balances fluency against diversity. In controlled experiments with a 170M masked diffusion language model, decoupling improves fluency, while scheduled stochastic remasking preserves entropy and achieves stronger LLM-judge scores under larger forward-pass budgets. These results show that remasking policy, not only the learned quality signal, is central to reliable masked-diffusion text generation.

</details>

Method: 采用轻量级的迁移学习方法，将普拉克里特语（Prakrit）映射为 IndicTrans2 模型中现有的印地语（Hindi，hin_Deva）语言标签，无需修改预训练模型的词元化器（tokenizer）、词表或模型架构。

Conclusion: 通过脚本兼容的语言路由（language routing）策略，可以在无需调整模型架构或词表的情况下，实现对低资源古典语言的迁移学习。然而，该方法的性能受到数据匮乏和方言差异的显著限制。

Abstract: We study English-to-Prakrit machine translation in a low-resource setting where the target language is unsupported by IndicTrans2. We adapt the multilingual model by mapping Prakrit to the Hindi language tag (hin_Deva) without modifying the tokenizer, vocabulary, or architecture. Using a 1,474-pair Maharashtri Prakrit parallel corpus and evaluation on a 20-sample Ardhamagadhi test set, we report corpus BLEU improvements over an untuned baseline. The results indicate that script-compatible language routing can enable feasible transfer to unsupported classical languages, while highlighting limitations due to data scarcity and dialect mismatch. Our code and trained models are released to the public for further exploration https://github.com/D3v1s0m/indictrans2-prakrit-mt.

### [74] [IA-RAG: Interval-Algebra-Driven Temporal Reasoning for Dynamic Knowledge Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06044)
*Xiaoman Wang,Yaoze Zhang,Wenzhuo Fan,Hongwei Zhang,Ding Wang,Guohang Yan,Song Mao,Botian Shi,Yunshi Lan,Pinlong Cai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: IA-RAG是一种创新的分层时序RAG框架，通过引入区间代数和子图时序优化机制，实现了对复杂时间结构的高效建模与推理，大幅提升了模型在时序问答任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RAG及Graph RAG框架通常将知识视为静态或仅使用粗粒度的时间戳，无法捕捉事件间的时长、重叠、包含等丰富的时序结构，导致模型在处理复杂时间推理解题时表现不佳。

Method: 提出了一种名为IA-RAG的分层时序RAG框架：1. 将事实建模为“区间事件单元”（IEU）；2. 构建“主题森林”来组织这些单元，并使用艾伦区间代数（Allen's Interval Algebra）管理时间依赖关系；3. 引入“子图时间收紧”（Sub-graph Time Tightening）机制以处理不确定或不完整的时间边界；4. 支持基于区间代数的隐式时序语义检索。

Result: 在TimeQA、TempReason和ComplexTR等多个时序问答基准测试中，IA-RAG展现出卓越的性能，特别是在处理复杂的组合式时序推理任务时，显著优于现有的基准模型。

Conclusion: IA-RAG通过引入区间代数和层级时间森林结构，有效解决了大模型在处理复杂时序知识时的局限性，证明了将时间作为一等公民纳入检索框架对于提升复杂时序推理能力的必要性。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) has shown strong effectiveness in grounding Large Language Models (LLMs) with external knowledge. However, existing RAG and Graph RAG frameworks largely treat knowledge as static or associate time with coarse-grained timestamps or metadata, failing to capture rich temporal structures such as duration, overlap, and containment. We propose IA-RAG, a hierarchical temporal RAG framework that models knowledge as time intervals and performs retrieval under formal temporal constraints. IA-RAG represents facts as Interval Event Units (IEUs) and organizes them into a hierarchical Thematic Forest, where temporal dependencies are governed by Allen's Interval Algebra. To handle incomplete or uncertain temporal boundaries, IA-RAG further introduces a Sub-graph Time Tightening mechanism that refines fuzzy intervals through logical constraints within connected event subgraphs. In addition, IA-RAG supports implicit temporal semantic retrieval through interval-algebra-guided traversal. Experiments on multiple temporal question answering benchmarks, including TimeQA, TempReason, and ComplexTR, demonstrate that IA-RAG achieves strong temporal retrieval and reasoning performance, particularly on complex compositional temporal reasoning tasks. Our code is released at https://github.com/xiaoAugenstern/LogicalRAG_TemporalQA.

### [75] [Automatic Labelling of Speech Translation Errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06047)
*Dominik Macháček,Maike Züfle,Ondrej Klejch*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 为了解决语音翻译系统缺乏错误评估机制的问题，研究提出了STEL（语音翻译错误标注）方法，并验证了当前多模态模型在识别ST错误方面尚有巨大提升空间，且强调了语音特征在错误检测中的核心作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 语音翻译（ST）系统中的错误会严重损害系统可信度并可能导致严重后果，但目前尚缺乏针对语音翻译质量评估和置信度估计的标准化方法。研究旨在填补这一空白，提出评估ST错误的方法论。

Result: 1. 现有模型（XCOMET和Qwen2.5-Omni）在STEL任务上的准确度仅为人类的一半左右；2. 直接处理语音信息对于STEL任务至关重要；3. 纯文本系统和语音处理系统在识别翻译错误与语音处理错误方面具有互补性。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了语音翻译错误标注（STEL）这一新领域。研究表明，虽然现有模型（如XCOMET和Qwen2.5-Omni）在STEL任务上的表现仍远落后于人类，但结合文本和语音信息的分析是必要的。未来该方向的研究需要更深入地整合多模态能力，以准确识别语音处理和翻译层面的双重错误。

Abstract: Errors in speech translations reduce trustworthiness of Speech Translation (ST) systems and can have serious consequences. Yet currently there is no established methodology for evaluating confidence and quality estimation of speech translations. To initiate progress in this direction, we propose Speech Translation Error Labelling (STEL). We create an annotation protocol, a small authentic end-to-end evaluation dataset, and we analyse how existing text-only and speech-processing systems perform the STEL task. Our results show that text-only XCOMET and multimodal LLM Qwen2.5-Omni are able to perform the STEL task in roughly half the precision of humans. We also find that direct speech processing is necessary for the STEL task, and that the current text-only and speech-processing systems are complementary in labelling translation-only vs. speech-processing errors in ST.

### [76] [Multi-task Learning is Not Enough: Representational Entanglement in Dual-output Second Language Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06065)
*Seung Hwan Cho,Young-Min Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了多任务学习在第二语言语音识别中存在的“任务纠缠”问题，即共享表示可能导致语义任务的提升以牺牲表面转录性能为代价，并指出了该现象与语言间表面-语义差异的相关性，为改进MTL架构提供了指导方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多任务学习（MTL）研究通常假设共享表示能促进不同任务的共同提升。然而，在第二语言语音识别中，这种假设并未在所有语言对中成立（特别是韩语与英语的差异），研究旨在探索为何多任务学习在提升语义理解的同时，会导致表面转录性能的下降。

Method: 研究人员通过对比韩语和英语在L2语音识别中的表现，利用多任务学习架构同时进行表面转录和语义识别。通过Levenshtein编辑距离量化表面与语义的差异，并结合编码器表示分析与跨任务解码器分析，揭示了任务纠缠对识别性能的具体影响机制。

Result: 研究发现，MTL在英语任务中显著损害了表面转录性能，且该降幅与表面-语义差异（通过编辑距离衡量）呈正相关。分析表明，英语任务在编码器层面出现了高度的任务纠缠，而韩语任务则能保持较好的任务表示区分度；此外，解码器层的适应能力也受到编码器纠缠的制约。

Conclusion: 在第二语言（L2）自动语音识别的多任务学习（MTL）中，盲目共享表示会导致编码器层面的任务纠缠，进而损害表面转录任务的性能。未来的研究应致力于设计能够缓解这种纠缠的架构，以平衡语义理解与表面转录的需求。

Abstract: Second-language (L2) speech recognition often requires transcriptions of pronunciations and intended meanings. Multi-task learning (MTL) is a natural approach because it assumes that shared representations benefit both outputs. However, this paper shows that this assumption does not hold across Korean and English. MTL improves meaning but degrades surface transcription, especially in English, where the degradation scales with surface-meaning divergence measured by Levenshtein edit distance.Encoder analysis links these patterns to encoder-level entanglement, with Korean preserving distinct task representations while English produces nearly identical ones. Cross-task decoder analysis shows that the meaning dual-output decoder adapts with a unique representation, while the surface dual-output decoder remains constrained by the encoder. These findings motivate the design of MTL frameworks that mitigate encoder-level entanglement to reduce surface degradation in dual-output L2 automatic speech recognition.
