### [77] [SkillComposer: Learning to Evolve Agent Skills for Specification and Generalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06079)
*Qi Zhang,Zhaopeng Feng,Xiaonan Shi,Xiaomeng Hu,Chu Liu,Pengjun Xie,Xiaobin Wang,Jieping Ye,Bryan Hooi,Haobo Wang,Junbo Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有智能体技能构建方法泛化性差的问题，本文提出了SkillComposer框架，通过“创建、改进、合并”的迭代机制，使语言模型能够自我演化并构建可迁移的通用技能，显著提升了模型在各类智能体与代码任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前智能体技能构建方法多为一次性提取，难以平衡任务特定技能的“不可迁移性”与抽象技能的“指导不足”。研究旨在解决缺乏显式技能规范和泛化机制的问题，从而提升模型在推理时的能力。

Method: 提出了SkillComposer框架，将技能构建分解为三个可学习的操作：创建（create）、改进（improve）和合并（merge）。该框架利用系统化的拒绝采样方案进行训练，支持离线构建通用库、在线任务优化以及两者的混合部署模式。

Result: 在τ²-Bench、LiveCodeBench v6和AppWorld等基准测试中表现优异。SkillComposer-4B模型使27B规模的执行器在智能体任务上提升了4.5分，在代码任务上提升了3.4分，并表现出良好的跨领域泛化能力。

Conclusion: SkillComposer证明了通过“创建、改进、合并”这三个可学习的操作，智能体能够实现自我演化并构建通用的技能库。技能组合不仅是一种可迁移的元能力，更为技能增强推理提供了一套切实可行的方案。

Abstract: Agent skills, which consist of reusable strategies that guide agent reasoning and action, have shown strong potential for improving model capability at inference time. However, current skill construction methods treat the problem as one-shot extraction, overlooking a fundamental tension: a skill tailored to the specific task fails to transfer, while the abstracted skill often provides insufficient guidance. We attribute this fragility to the absence of explicit mechanisms for skill specification and generalization. To address this gap, we introduce SkillComposer, a framework that decomposes skill construction into three learnable operations: create, improve, and merge. Trained via systematic rejection sampling recipe, SkillComposer enables language models to self-evolve skills at inference time and supports three deployment modes: offline for building generalized libraries, online for task-specific refinement, and hybrid for combining both. Comprehensive experiments on $τ^2$-Bench, LiveCodeBench v6, and AppWorld show that SkillComposer consistently outperforms baselines. Our SkillComposer-4B improves a 27B executor by up to +4.5 on agent tasks and +3.4 on code tasks, while generalizing across domains and task types unseen during training. Analysis reveals that merge and improve address orthogonal quality dimensions and that skill composition is a transferable meta-ability, providing a practical recipe for skill-augmented inference.

</details>


### [78] [LatentSkill: From In-Context Textual Skills to In-Weight Latent Skills for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06087)
*Aofan Yu,Chenyu Zhou,Tianyi Xu,Zihan Guo,Rong Shan,Zhihui Fu,Jun Wang,Weiwen Liu,Yong Yu,Weinan Zhang,Jianghao Lin*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LatentSkill 框架通过超网络将文本技能转化为 LoRA 权重，实现了技能存储的“权重空间化”。该方法在显著降低上下文开销的同时，提升了智能体的任务执行性能，并增强了技能的模块化与组合能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体系统依赖文本技能提示，但这会导致上下文开销巨大且技能内容以明文暴露。研究者希望通过将技能编码为可重用的权重空间组件，来解决性能瓶颈并提升模块化能力。

Method: 提出 LatentSkill 框架，利用预训练的超网络（Hypernetwork）将文本形式的技能转化为即插即用的 LoRA 适配器。这种方法将技能知识从上下文空间转移到权重空间，从而消除了每步所需的技能 Token，同时保持了技能的模块化加载、缩放和组合能力。

Result: 在 ALFWorld 和 Search-QA 任务中，LatentSkill 表现优于传统的上下文技能基线。ALFWorld 任务成功率在已知和未知分割下分别提升了 21.4 和 13.4 个百分点，且预填充 Token 减少了 64.1%；Search-QA 任务精确匹配度提升 3.0 点，技能 Token 开销降低 72.2%。此外，生成的 LoRA 展现了结构化的语义几何特性，支持参数空间的组合操作。

Conclusion: LatentSkill 证明了将技能存储在权重空间而非上下文空间不仅可行，而且在效率、性能和模块化方面均优于传统的上下文提示方法，为构建更高效、更安全的智能体系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: Agent systems increasingly use textual skills to encode reusable task procedures, but injecting these skills into the prompt at every step incurs substantial context overhead and exposes skill content as plaintext. We present LatentSkill, a framework that converts textual skills into plug-and-play LoRA adapters through a pretrained hypernetwork. LatentSkill stores skill knowledge in weight space rather than context space, removing per-step skill tokens while preserving modular loading, scaling, and composition. On ALFWorld and Search-QA, LatentSkill outperforms the corresponding in-context skill baseline while using substantially fewer prefill tokens: it improves ALFWorld success by 21.4 and 13.4 points on the seen and unseen splits with 64.1% fewer prefill tokens, and improves Search-QA exact match by 3.0 points with 72.2% lower skill-token overhead. Further analysis shows that generated skill LoRAs form a structured semantic geometry, can be precisely controlled via the LoRA scaling coefficient, and can be composed through parameter-space arithmetic when skill components are aligned. These findings suggest that weight-space skills provide an efficient, modular, and less exposed substrate for extending LLM agents.

### [79] [CHALIS: A Challenge Dataset for Language Identification in Difficult Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06088)
*Michal Tichý,Jindřich Libovický*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了 CHALIS 数据集，用于评估语言识别系统在亲缘语言辨别和正字法噪声处理方面的能力，实验证实了现有主流模型在这些挑战性场景下的局限性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了一个名为 CHALIS 的新基准数据集，包含两部分：一是收集了互通性强的亲缘语言对（如捷克语/斯洛伐克语、西班牙语/加泰罗尼亚语等）的共享句子；二是引入了多种正字法噪声，包括跨脚本转写、去变音符号、同形异义词攻击以及网络俚语。研究使用该数据集对四种主流语言识别系统进行了评估。

Result: 实验表明，所有被测试的语言识别系统在处理亲缘语言和正字法噪声时均表现出显著的性能下降，尤其在针对亲缘语言中的低资源语言以及跨脚本转写输入的识别上表现尤为脆弱。

Conclusion: 现有的主流语言识别系统在处理亲缘语言和正字法噪声时表现不佳，该研究强调了在这些复杂场景下开发更稳健模型的重要性。CHALIS 数据集为评估和改进语言识别系统的鲁棒性提供了标准基准。

Abstract: We present CHALIS (Challenging Language Identification Samples), a new benchmark dataset explicitly designed to address difficult cases in language identification: cousin languages and orthographic noise. Our dataset has two parts: First, we collected sentences shared across mutually intelligible language pairs (Czech/Slovak, Spanish/Catalan, Portuguese/Galician, Danish/Norwegian). The second part tests for orthography noise: we transliterate text across multiple scripts, remove diacritics, simulate homoglyph attacks, and use Internet slang. We evaluate four widely used language identification systems on CHALIS and demonstrate that all struggle substantially in these scenarios, especially on lower-resource languages within cousin pairs and on transliterated input. The resource is publicly available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/michal-tichy/CHALIS.

### [80] [IR3DE: A Linear Router for Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06098)
*Eros Fanì,Oğuzhan Ersoy*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 IR3DE 的轻量级、基于岭回归的推理路由器，能够高效地将不同 prompt 指派给最合适的领域专家 LLM。该方法不仅计算成本低、性能优秀，还支持动态扩展专家模型，无需频繁重训。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的推理路由方法存在局限性：要么仅关注通用模型间的成本优化，要么需要大量训练来支持领域专家的路由选择。因此，研究人员旨在寻找一种既廉价、快速，又能高效处理领域专家任务匹配的轻量级路由解决方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为 IR3DE（基于岭回归的领域专家路由器）的方法。该方法通过岭回归（Ridge Regression）算法对 prompt 进行快速评估并路由至最适合的领域专家模型。其核心优势在于线性模型的低计算开销，以及在无需从头重新训练的情况下，支持领域专家模型的动态增减。

Result: 在因果语言建模（CLM）设置中，IR3DE 的性能与现有基准相当；在推理任务设置中，其性能超越了现有基准，达到了 98.4% 的归一化性能。此外，该方法显著降低了计算成本，并支持在不重新训练路由器的情况下动态调整专家模型池。

Conclusion: IR3DE 通过简单的线性回归方法有效解决了领域专家模型之间的路由选择问题。该研究证明，在无需复杂训练的情况下，轻量级的路由策略即可实现高性能的专家任务匹配，且具备高度的灵活性和可扩展性，非常适合动态调整专家模型的实际应用场景。

Abstract: Foundational Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate proficiency on a wide range of general tasks, and achieve remarkable results on various specialized tasks via domain-expert LLMs. With the ever-growing list of available LLMs, inference routers are being proposed to select the most appropriate LLM for each prompt. However, existing routing methods either optimize cost across weak-to-strong generalist LLMs or require substantial training to support domain-expertise routing. In this paper, we propose IR3DE, a Ridge Regression-based Router for Domain Experts that provides cheap and fast routing decisions for each prompt. We evaluate IR3DE in two Causal Language Modeling (CLM) settings where the tasks are next-token prediction for all domains, and one reasoning setting where each domain has its own distinct reasoning task. Despite being a linear router, IR3DE achieves performance comparable to the other baselines in both CLM settings, and surpassing them in the reasoning setting, with a normalized performance of 98.4%. Moreover, IR3DE enables the addition or removal of new domain experts without requiring the router to be retrained from scratch, allowing a dynamic set of LLMs to be served with minimal disruption to the router itself. Our code is available at: github.com/gensyn-ai/IR3DE.

### [81] [Harnessing Structural Context for Entity Alignment Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06109)
*Xingyu Chen,Yuanning Cui,Zequn Sun,Wei Hu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有实体对齐基础模型对结构化上下文利用不足的问题，本文提出了ContextEA框架，通过增强跨图交互与结构化得分校准，显著提升了模型在不同知识图谱间的对齐迁移效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的实体对齐（EA）基础模型在处理结构化上下文方面存在不足，表现为编码过程中的跨图交互较弱，且最终的候选排序过分依赖粗粒度的相似度计算，限制了模型在未见知识图谱上的泛化性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为ContextEA的编码器-解码器框架：1. 编码器端引入了跨知识图谱交互编码器，利用锚点桥接统一两个知识图谱，并进行早期的关系感知跨图传播；2. 解码器端设计了结构校准解码器，利用实体级、邻域级、关系级和锚点感知的结构证据对对齐分数进行校准。

Result: 在OpenEA、SRPRS和DBP数据集的29个实体对齐基准上进行了测试。实验结果显示，ContextEA在所有三个基准组中均优于经过微调的基准模型，表现出极强的跨知识图谱迁移能力。

Conclusion: 显式利用结构化上下文是提升实体对齐基础模型性能的有效途径。ContextEA模型通过改进编码器和解码器的结构化处理能力，显著增强了模型在未见知识图谱上的迁移能力，证明了该方法在知识融合任务中的优越性。

Abstract: Entity alignment (EA) aims to identify equivalent entities across heterogeneous knowledge graphs (KGs) and is a key component of knowledge fusion and cross-KG reasoning. The recent EA foundation model demonstrates that alignment knowledge, once pretrained, can be directly applied to diverse previously unseen KG pairs. However, it still underuses structural context in two places: cross-KG interaction is weak during encoding, and final candidate ranking still relies too heavily on coarse similarity. We address these limitations with ContextEA, an enhanced encoder-decoder framework for transferable EA. On the encoder side, we introduce a cross-KG interaction encoder that unifies the two KGs with anchor bridges and performs earlier relation-aware cross-graph propagation. On the decoder side, we introduce a structural calibration decoder that calibrates alignment scores with entity-level, neighborhood-level, relation-level, and anchor-aware structural evidence. This design strengthens both structural context construction and structural context exploitation while remaining lightweight. Experiments on 29 EA datasets in OpenEA, SRPRS, and DBP show consistent gains over strong transferable baselines. Notably, the pretrained ContextEA already surpasses the finetuned baselines on all three benchmark groups, demonstrating substantially stronger transfer to unseen KGs. These results suggest that explicitly harnessing structural context is an effective direction for improving EA foundation models.

### [82] [Ouvia: A User-centered Framework for Measuring Usability of Speech Translation in Real-World Communication Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06177)
*Giuseppe Attanasio,Beatrice Savoldi,Daniel Chechelnitsky,Matteo Negri,Marine Carpuat,Maarten Sap,André F. T. Martins*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对语音翻译（ST）脱离实际使用场景的问题，本文提出了Ouvia评估框架，通过1750次真实对话测试发现，现代ST系统可用性不足且存在人口统计学偏见，并验证了QA评估指标优于传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语音翻译（ST）评估主要集中在脱离实际语境的测试集和整体质量指标上，忽略了终端用户的实际沟通需求。为了解决这一脱节问题，研究者旨在建立一个能够衡量真实场景中用户对语音翻译输出的感知可用性的评估框架。

Method: 作者开发了名为Ouvia的评估框架，通过定制的Web应用程序，在医疗和日常场景中收集了超过1750次真实的一对一语音翻译交互。实验涵盖了四种不同的语音翻译系统、三种英语方言以及两种性别，并对比了不同的评估指标（如QA基础的评估）与实际可用性之间的相关性。

Result: 研究发现，现代语音翻译系统在真实场景中的表现有限，仅约一半的交互被用户评价为“可用”；不同人口统计学群体之间存在显著的可用性差距；此外，基于问答（QA）的评估指标比标准的整体质量指标能更准确地预测实际可用性。

Conclusion: 当前的语音翻译评估方法主要依赖于脱离语境的整体质量指标，这无法准确反映终端用户的实际沟通需求。本研究提出的Ouvia框架强调了情境化、以用户为中心的评估方式的重要性，指出评估不仅应关注翻译的“整体质量”，更应关注技术在不同人口统计学群体中的实际可用性。

Abstract: Speech translation (ST) is increasingly adopted in user applications, yet its evaluation largely focuses on decontextualized testbeds and holistic quality, rather than end users' communication needs. We introduce Ouvia, an evaluation framework for measuring user-perceived usability of speech translation outputs in real-world settings. Ouvia focuses on one-to-one communication: an English speaker needs to convey a request to a Portuguese speaker, and the message is automatically translated. Through a custom web app and multi-phase study design, we collect more than 1,750 such interactions in healthcare and everyday situations, mediated by four ST systems, involving speakers from three English dialects and two genders. We find that modern ST serves people only to a limited extent -- only around half of interactions are rated as usable -- with significant gaps in reported usability across demographic groups. Moreover, among quality metrics, we find that QA-based evaluation is a substantially stronger predictor of real-world usability than standard approaches. Together, these findings stress the importance of situated, user-centered evaluation frameworks that go beyond holistic quality scores and attend to who the technology serves -- and how well.

### [83] [The Tell-Tale Norm: $\ell_2$ Magnitude as a Signal for Reasoning Dynamics in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06188)
*Jinyang Zhang,Hongxin Ding,Yue Fang,Weibin Liao,Muyang Ye,Junfeng Zhao,Yasha Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究发现隐藏状态的 L2 范数是 LLM 推理强度的内在信号，并据此提出了一套无需训练、即插即用的推理优化策略，有效增强了模型的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前对于大语言模型（LLM）推理过程的理解尚缺乏一种具有模型内在特性的、原则性的层级动态信号。研究者希望通过探索模型内部信号，以更好地感知和干预 LLM 的推理逻辑。

Method: 1. 使用稀疏自动编码器（SAE）作为诊断探针，分析模型内部的推理特征激活情况；2. 建立 L2 范数与潜在几何结构的理论联系，证明 L2 范数对 SAE 推理特征激活强度的边界约束；3. 通过经验相关性分析和因果干预验证 L2 范数的有效性；4. 开发了三种无需训练的推理时优化技术：自适应层级推理递归、内源推理状态引导以及 L2 指导下的响应选择。

Result: 实验表明，LLM 的内部推理在深层表现为推理特征激活的急剧增加，且 L2 范数能准确捕捉这一过程。应用提出的三种推理时缩放技术，在多种模型架构和基准测试中均显著提升了推理性能。

Conclusion: 本研究通过理论与实验证明，隐藏状态的 L2 范数可作为大模型推理强度的内在指标。该发现不仅揭示了模型内部的推理动态，还提供了一套无需额外训练的推理时间缩放技术，显著提升了模型的推理性能，为理解和控制黑盒模型提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Recent work has sought to understand Large Language Models (LLMs) reasoning, yet a principled, model-intrinsic signal that captures its layer-wise reasoning dynamics remains underexplored. We bridge this gap by demonstrating that the l2 norm of hidden states serves as an endogenous signal of the model's reasoning intensity. Using Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) as a diagnostic probe, we observe that LLMs' internal reasoning is marked by a sharp increase in reasoning feature activations concentrated in late layers. Motivated by this pattern, we establish a formal link between reasoning intensity and the model's latent geometry and theoretically prove that the l2 norm of hidden states bounds the activation strength of SAE reasoning features. Empirical correlation analysis and causal interventions further validate the l2 norm as a faithful indicator, where heightened norms consistently correspond to critical reasoning steps. We then introduce three test-time scaling techniques guided by l2 norms: (i) Adaptive Layer-wise Reasoning Recursion, (ii) Endogenous Reasoning State Steering, and (iii) l2-guided Response Selection, which requires no additional training or data and is compatible with advanced inference engines. Experiments across model architectures and benchmarks show that l2-norm-based techniques significantly improve reasoning performance, offering a principled yet simple lens to perceive and control LLM latent reasoning dynamics. Our code is available at https://github.com/zjy1298/The-Tell-Tale-Norm.

Existing approaches often struggle with contextual understanding, answer consistency, and generalization across diverse domains. In this work, we propose a question answering system based on large language models, where the input consists of a textual context and a corresponding question, and the output is a concise and accurate answer. The motivation behind this research lies in addressing the limitations of current QA systems, particularly their tendency to produce irrelevant or imprecise responses despite having access to the correct context. Our methodology involves fine-tuning a pre-trained LLM on a benchmark QA dataset to improve its contextual comprehension and answer extraction capabilities. Specifically, we utilize the Stanford Question Answering Dataset (SQuAD1.1), which provides high-quality context-question-answer triplets for supervised training and evaluation. Experimental results show that the fine-tuned Roberta-base model achieves the highest performance, attaining a ROUGE-L score of 86.84%, a BLEU score of 28.24%, and a BERTScore of 95.38%. ### [85] [Dense Contexts Are Hard Contexts: Lexical Density Limits Effective Context in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06203)
*Giovanni Dettori,Matteo Boffa,Danilo Giordano,Idilio Drago,Marco Mellia*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 词汇密度是决定大型语言模型长上下文表现的关键因素；即使长度相同，信息越密集，模型的检索性能下降越明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 既有研究通常认为输入长度和关键信息位置是导致大型语言模型（LLM）长上下文性能下降的主要原因。本文旨在探讨“词汇密度”（即上下文引入独特信息的速率）是否也是导致LLM上下文窗口性能衰减的关键但被忽视的因素。

Method: 研究人员使用了三个“大海捞针”式的基准测试，在保持输入长度（约12k tokens）和目标位置一致的前提下，通过改变输入内容的词汇密度（即单位长度内包含的不同信息量）来观察模型性能变化。同时，通过在各基准测试中控制密度变量，排除了任务类型等干扰因素，并验证了降低密度对恢复模型性能的作用。

Result: 实验发现，随着词汇密度的增加，LLM的性能会出现急剧下降（从近乎完美下降到低于60%的检索得分）。即便在相同的长度和位置条件下，高密度输入也会导致模型有效上下文窗口显著萎缩。降低密度能够有效恢复模型的检索性能。

Conclusion: 有效的上下文容量不仅取决于输入长度和信息位置，还直接受词汇密度（信息含量）的制约。对于高密度信息输入，即使模型在长文本任务中表现良好，其性能也会大幅下降。因此，评估和优化模型时必须将词汇密度视为关键维度。

Abstract: Input length and the position of relevant information are widely cited as the primary causes of degraded LLM long-context performance. Here, we study lexical density -- the rate at which a context introduces distinct information -- as a third, largely overlooked factor that systematically reduces the effective context window of LLMs. We quantify the impact of lexical density on open-weight LLMs (9B-685B) using three "find-the-needle" style benchmarks with identical length (~12k tokens) and controlled needle position, but increasing density of information. We observe a sharp performance collapse in higher-density benchmarks: models that are near-perfect in sparse contexts drop below 60% retrieval score on denser ones. To rule out task-type confounds, we vary and control the density within each benchmark while keeping all other properties unchanged. Reducing density generally restores performance, especially in the high-density regimes where degradation appears. These results show that effective context capacity is a function of lexical density, with direct implications for real-world LLM systems operating on compact, information-rich inputs.

</details>


### [86] [FiLM-Based Speaker Conditioning of a SpeechLLM for Pathological Speech Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06211)
*Fernando López,Santosh Kesiraju,Jordi Luque*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出利用FiLM技术将说话人信息注入冻结的ASR编码器，实现对病理语音的有效适配，在不损害基础模型能力的前提下显著提升了病理语音识别性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自动语音识别（ASR）在标准语音处理方面已取得显著进展，但针对神经系统疾病导致的病理语音识别仍面临巨大挑战。现有方法往往需要进行全量微调，计算成本高且容易导致模型性能退化，因此亟需一种更高效、更具鲁棒性的适配策略。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于特征线性调制（FiLM）的说话人条件化方法。该方法利用x-vector提取说话人特征，并将其注入到冻结的ASR Transformer编码器的每一层中，从而在不修改预训练模型权重的情况下，使内部表征适应特定的病理语音说话人。此外，研究还将其与传统微调、参数高效微调以及后处理方法进行了对比。

Result: 实验结果表明，基于FiLM的说话人条件化ASR在性能上与现有的适配策略（如全量微调和参数高效微调）具有竞争力。此外，该方法在处理病理语音的同时，能够很好地保持模型在非条件化语音上的识别能力，并保留了回答语音相关问题的功能。

Conclusion: 通过FiLM进行说话人条件化是一种高效且鲁棒的病理语音ASR适配方法。它无需微调基础模型参数即可提升病理语音识别性能，同时保持了模型的通用性，在跨语言（英语和西班牙语）场景下展现出良好的泛化能力和任务保留能力。

Abstract: Automatic speech recognition (ASR) has advanced remarkably for standard speech; however, pathological speech from neurological conditions remains a significant challenge. We investigate speaker conditioning via Feature-wise Linear Modulation (FiLM), injecting x-vector-derived information into each transformer layer of a frozen ASR encoder to adapt internal representations to individual pathological speakers without modifying base model weights. We benchmark this for the ASR task against standard and parameter-efficient fine-tuning baselines, complemented by post-processing, on Spanish and English pathological speech. Additionally, we evaluate if the adapted model preserves the ability to answer speech-related questions. Results show that speaker-conditioned ASR is competitive with established adaptation strategies while retaining performance on non-conditioned speech.

</details>


### [87] [From Self to Other: Evaluating Demographic Perspective-Taking in LLM Hate Speech Annotation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06266)
*Paloma Piot,Javier Parapar*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文研究了大语言模型通过人格化提示模拟人类仇恨言论感知的能力。研究发现，虽然简单的身份提示效果有限，但采用 Llama 3.1 进行“替代性预测”可以较好地模拟人类的社会分歧模式，为自动标注提供了一种更可靠的对齐方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仇恨言论检测具有高度的主观性，不同背景的人对同一内容的看法存在差异。由于大规模采集多群体标注数据成本高昂且难以扩展，研究者提出利用人格化大语言模型模拟多样化视角。本文旨在探究这些模型是否确实能真实反映人类群体间的观点分歧及社会判断规律。

Method: 研究评估了三种评估模型社会判断能力的维度：(i) 不同群体身份（personas）之间是否存在类似人类的群体间分歧；(ii) 模型在面对针对自身群体的内容时是否表现出“群体内敏感性”；(iii) 模型能否准确预测其他群体的反应。研究通过对比不同大语言模型在这些维度的表现，特别是应用“替代性预测”提示词工程的效果，来验证模型对人类主观偏见的模拟能力。

Result: 实验发现，没有单一模型能完全一致地涵盖所有三个维度的要求；模型性能表现出高度的依赖性；仅靠最小化的身份提示无法可靠地生成预期的多样化观点。不过，使用 Llama 3.1 进行“替代性预测”能够产生最高水平的跨群体一致性，在大多数人口统计学轴向上最接近人类的意见分歧模式。

Conclusion: 尽管大语言模型在模拟人类社会判断方面表现出模型依赖性，且仅靠简单的身份提示难以可靠地复现多样化观点，但通过使用 Llama 3.1 配合“替代性预测”（vicarious prompting）策略，可以更有效地逼近人类的群体间分歧模式，为实现与人类判断对齐的自动化标注提供了可行路径。

Abstract: Hate speech detection is inherently subjective: people from different demographic groups perceive the same content very differently. Collecting enough annotations from multiple demographic groups is costly and difficult to scale. Persona-conditioned Large Language Models (models prompted to adopt a specific demographic identity) have been proposed as a way to simulate diverse perspectives at scale. But do they actually reflect how different groups disagree? We evaluate three aspects of human social judgement: (i) whether personas from different groups disagree in human-like ways (inter-group disagreement), (ii) whether they become more sensitive when content targets their own identity (in-group sensitivity), and (iii) whether they can accurately predict how another group would react (vicarious prediction). Our results show that no model consistently captures all three dimensions, and performance is highly model-dependent and does not emerge reliably from minimal identity prompts alone. However, vicarious prompting with Llama 3.1 yields the highest cross-group agreement in most demographic axes and provides the closest overall approximation to human disagreement patterns, indicating that this configuration may provide a more reliable setting for automatic annotation aligned with human judgements.

### [88] [Many Circuits, One Mechanism: Input Variation and Evaluation Granularity in Circuit Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06267)
*Alireza Bayat Makou,Jingcheng Niu,Subhabrata Dutta,Iryna Gurevych*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究指出，神经网络模型中由电路发现算法提取的结构差异往往是“幻觉特化”，并不代表模型内部存在不同的计算机制。研究强调应通过边级评估和跨条件测试来审视电路的真实功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前电路发现方法普遍假设“结构的差异即代表机制的差异”。作者旨在验证这一假设的有效性，探究在任务保持不变但输入统计量变化时，提取出的不同电路结构是否真正反映了功能的特异性。

Method: 研究使用了文字序列复制（Literal Sequence Copying）任务，在五个Pythia系列模型（70M-1.4B）中针对不同令牌频率分布提取了75个电路。通过跨频率频带的交叉测试（cross-condition transfer）、因果干预（causal interchange）以及对比源级（source-level）与边级（edge-level）的评估方法，系统分析了电路结构与功能之间的关系。

Result: 实验揭示了“幻觉特化”（phantom specialization）现象：尽管针对不同输入统计量提取出的电路在结构上明显不同，但它们实际上实现了相同的计算逻辑。研究发现，这些电路之间存在高度的跨频带功能通用性，且核心子集即可恢复绝大部分性能；同时，相同的频带内也会提取出结构不同的电路，证实了算法是在一个等价类中采样，而非发现唯一机制。

Conclusion: 电路发现算法提取的结构差异并不等同于模型内部机制的差异。研究表明，结构层面的差异往往源于算法从等价类中随机采样，而非捕捉到了独特的计算过程。因此，单一电路的结构特征不能作为解释模型特定行为的充分证据。

Abstract: Circuit discovery methods identify subgraphs that explain specific model behaviors, and structural differences between discovered circuits are commonly interpreted as evidence of distinct mechanisms. We test this assumption by varying input statistics while holding the task fixed, and show that the resulting structural differences exhibit apparent specialization but do not correspond to functional differences, a pattern we term phantom specialization. Using Literal Sequence Copying across four token-frequency bands plus a control condition in five Pythia models (70M-1.4B), we extract 75 circuits and find that structurally distinct circuits implement the same computation: band-specific edges transfer broadly across bands, a core shared across most bands recovers at least 99% of circuit performance, and causal interchange interventions confirm that internal representations are interchangeable across frequency bands. Repeated extractions within the same frequency band further suggest that discovery algorithms sample from an equivalence class of valid subgraphs rather than recovering a unique mechanism. Standard evaluation practice obscures this pattern: source-level evaluation inflates apparent faithfulness, while edge-level evaluation reveals the many-to-one mapping from structure to function. Our results show that structural differences between circuits are not sufficient evidence for distinct mechanisms, and that exposing this requires edge-level evaluation and cross-condition transfer tests.

</details>


### [89] [FOXGLOVE: Understanding Goal-Oriented and Anchored Writing Feedback from Experts and LLMs on Argumentative Essays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06271)
*Yijun Liu,Yifan Song,John Gallagher,Sarah Sterman,Tal August*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文发布了FOXGLOVE数据集，用于系统对比人类教师与大语言模型（LLM）在写作反馈中的表现。研究发现LLM生成的反馈虽然篇幅更长且评分较高，但在精准锚定问题和启发式教学（提问）方面仍与人类专家存在差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型（LLM）被广泛用于生成写作反馈，但目前尚缺乏关于其在写作反馈的核心要素（目标导向、句子锚定、优先级）上与人类专家对比的系统性研究，缺乏基准数据以了解两者在教学策略上的异同。

Method: 研究者构建了FOXGLOVE数据集，包含696条人类教师反馈和1644条由四个前沿LLM生成的反馈。通过专家对反馈质量进行评分，并从目标导向性、句子锚定、优先级分配以及语言复杂性等多维度进行定量与定性的系统对比分析。

Result: 研究发现，人类教师与LLM在反馈目标和文章位置分布上具有相似性；然而，LLM在锚定特定句子方面与教师存在分歧，且反馈语言更复杂、提问更少。在质量评价上，尽管LLM获得的评分较高，但这种优势很大程度上归因于其反馈篇幅更长。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，尽管大型语言模型（LLM）在反馈质量的某些维度上能获得专家好评，但其优势在很大程度上受制于反馈长度，且在针对性（锚定特定句子）和教学策略（如使用提问引导）上仍与人类教师存在显著差异。FOXGLOVE数据集为后续研究评估和优化AI辅助写作反馈提供了重要的基准。

Abstract: While large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used to generate writing feedback, there remains no systematic comparison of LLM and expert feedback on the dimensions that writing research identifies as central to revision: goal-orientation, anchoring to specific sentences, and prioritization. We introduce FOXGLOVE, a dataset of 696 feedback comments written by trained writing instructors on 69 twelfth-grade argumentative essays, paired with 1,644 comments generated from four frontier LLMs under a shared protocol, totaling 2,340 comments. We provide expert quality ratings on a subset of both instructor and LLM comments. We find that instructors and LLMs distribute feedback similarly across goals and essay positions, yet instructors and models diverge on the specific sentences on which to provide feedback. Additionally, we find that models tend to write more complex feedback and use fewer questions than instructors. LLM feedback also receives higher ratings on most dimensions of quality, as rated by instructors, but much of this advantage appears to be attributable to lengthier comments. FOXGLOVE enables systematic comparison of where human and LLM feedback align, diverge, and differ.

</details>


### [90] [LLMs Can Leak Training Data But Do They Want To? A Propensity-Aware Evaluation of Memorization in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06286)
*Gianluca Barmina,Peter Schneider-Kamp,Lukas Galke Poech*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了PropMe框架和SimpleTrace工具，旨在区分大语言模型中“潜在的记忆能力”与“实际的泄露倾向”。研究发现，虽然模型可以通过诱导泄露数据，但在日常使用中极少发生此类情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型记忆评估主要关注模型在“被强制引导”下复现训练数据的能力，但这并不代表模型在日常使用中会频繁出现此类行为，缺乏对真实应用场景下泄露倾向的评估。

Method: 1. 提出了PropMe（倾向感知）评估框架，对比前缀引导的对抗性攻击与非对抗性评估。2. 引入了度量转换方法，将现有评估函数转化为倾向性指标。3. 开发了SimpleTrace追踪流水线，基于infini-gram对生成内容进行确定性归因，并计算 verbatim（逐字）、近逐字及倾向性记忆指标。

Result: 1. 能力与倾向之间存在显著差距：前缀攻击比普通提示词更能诱导模型产生记忆内容，但在非对抗性评估中，模型的记忆倾向评分依然较低。2. 持续预训练（DFM Decoder）可以降低对原始训练数据集（Common Pile）的记忆及其倾向，证明记忆能力是可以随着训练重点的改变而减弱的。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，评估语言模型记忆泄露风险时，应同时考虑“能力（可被诱导泄露的最坏情况）”与“倾向（自然使用下的真实泄露倾向）”。研究发现，模型在非对抗性场景下很少复现训练数据，且持续预训练可以有效降低模型的记忆倾向。

Abstract: Large language models can reproduce training data, but existing memorization evaluations mostly measure whether models can be forced to do so, rather than whether they do so under ordinary use. We introduce PropMe, a propensity-aware framework for memorization evaluation that contrasts prefix-based capability attacks with non-adversarial evaluations. We propose a metric transformation that, applied to existing functions, allows to create propensity metrics. We further introduce SimpleTrace, a lightweight tracing pipeline built on infini-gram that deterministically attributes model generations to large-scale training corpora and computes verbatim, near-verbatim, and propensity-transformed memorization metrics. Evaluating two fully-open models: Comma and DFM Decoder on two datasets: Common Pile and Dynaword in two languages, we find a consistent gap between capability and propensity: prefix attacks elicit substantially stronger memorization signals than generic or dataset-specific prompts, while propensity scores remain low overall. Thus, the models can reveal training data when directly elicited, but rarely do so in more common non-adversarial settings. We also find that DFM Decoder, which is continually pre-trained from Comma, exhibits reduced memorization and memorization propensity for Common Pile, confirming that memorization capability can decrease when later training emphasizes partially different data. Our results suggest, and we encourage, that memorization audits should report both worst-case extractability and ordinary leakage propensity in order to have a more comprehensive view of this phenomenon.

</details>


### [91] [Decomposing Factual Sycophancy in Language Models: How Size and Instruction Tuning Shape Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06306)
*Victor De Marez,Luna De Bruyne,Walter Daelemans*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了语言模型事实性逢迎的两个核心机制——“真相边际”与“操纵敏感度”，指出单纯依赖翻转率评估存在局限，并分析了模型规模与指令微调如何差异化地影响这两项指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的翻转率指标无法区分模型在面对错误诱导时，是因为本身对真相的偏好不够坚定（真相边际低），还是因为对社会压力过度敏感（操纵敏感度高）。本研究旨在揭示模型“事实性逢迎”背后的深层机制。

Method: 研究人员将事实性逢迎分解为“真相边际”和“操纵敏感度”两个维度，对56个参数规模在0.3B到32B之间的开源模型进行了实证分析，涵盖了13种操纵类型，用以解耦模型规模与指令微调对模型行为的影响。

Result: 研究发现：1. 模型的稳健性主要受规模驱动，但指令微调改变了这一逻辑，小型微调模型可能变脆弱，大型微调模型则变稳健；2. 指令微调主要提升了模型的“真相边际”；3. 模型规模的提升对基础模型和微调模型的影响路径不同，微调模型在规模化过程中能显著增加真相边际并降低操纵敏感度。

Conclusion: 事实性逢迎并非单一的标量属性，而是由“真相边际（truth margin）”和“操纵敏感度（manipulation sensitivity）”共同决定的。评估模型稳健性时，应弃用单一的翻转率指标，转向基于通道、操纵类型和模型规模的细分评估。

Abstract: Factual sycophancy occurs when a language model abandons a correct, verifiable answer under social pressure. Because a flip occurs only when pressure toward a false answer exceeds the model's neutral preference for the truth, flip rates conflate two mechanisms: the strength of that baseline preference (truth margin), and how far pressure shifts it (manipulation sensitivity). We decompose factual sycophancy into these channels and use them to separate the effects of size and instruction tuning across 56 open-weight models spanning 0.3B-32B parameters and 13 manipulation types. We find that vulnerability is governed mainly by size, but instruction tuning changes how size acts: small instruction-tuned models can become less robust, whereas large instruction-tuned models usually become more robust. Instruction tuning primarily increases truth margin, but its behavioral effect depends on manipulation type. Scaling also changes the two channels differently: base models gain margin but become mildly more manipulation-sensitive, whereas instruction-tuned models gain margin faster and become less sensitive. Factual sycophancy is therefore not a single scalar property. Evaluations should report channel-specific, manipulation-specific, and size-conditioned robustness rather than flip rates alone.

</details>


### [92] ["Chi nas dal soch el sent de legn" -- Auditing Text Corpora for Lombard](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06349)
*Edoardo Signoroni,Pavel Rychlý*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对低资源伦巴第语的语料库现状研究表明，单纯依靠网络爬虫获取的海量数据存在严重的质量低劣和方言偏差问题，必须建立更精准、公平且由社区主导的数据处理标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多世界语言因缺乏高质量数据集而导致NLP资源匮乏。本文旨在探讨为什么像伦巴第语这样表面上拥有大量网络爬取数据的语言，在实际应用（如机器翻译）中效果依然不佳，并揭示现有数据集背后的质量与公平性挑战。

Method: 通过人工审计（Manual Audit）方法，对现有的伦巴第语平行语料库和单语语料库进行全面评估；分析语料中的语言错误识别、样板文本（boilerplate）及非语言噪声；利用正字法（orthographic）分析法，对比不同语料库中伦巴第语的变体分布情况，评估其代表性偏差。

Result: 现有所谓的“海量”伦巴第语数据多为假象，其中充斥着严重的语言误识别、冗余内容和噪声；此外，现存语料库在正字法体系上存在冲突，且存在严重的地区代表性偏差，即数据高度向西部伦巴第语方言倾斜，而东部方言则被边缘化。

Conclusion: 针对低资源语言（如伦巴第语）的自然语言处理，应从单纯追求语料库的“数量”转向关注数据的“质量”与“多样性”。必须建立社区参与的、具备方言感知能力的语料收集与清洗机制，以解决数据噪声与代表性偏差问题。

Abstract: Several of the world's languages are still under-resourced in terms of Natural Language Processing (NLP) tools. This is mostly due to the lack of high-quality datasets to train, develop, and evaluate systems and models for several tasks, such as Machine Translation (MT). We conduct a manual audit of the parallel and monolingual corpora available for Lombard, an under-resourced language continuum from Italy. Our analysis reveals that the perceived abundance of web-scraped data is an illusion, with massive datasets plagued by severe language misidentification, boilerplate text, and non-linguistic noise. Furthermore, we analyze the orthographic composition of the valid Lombard portions across web-scraped datasets, curated corpora, and benchmarks. Our findings show conflicting orthographical systems and severe representational bias across all corpora: high-quality data is heavily skewed towards Western Lombard varieties, with Eastern ones left on the margins. This underscores the need for variety-aware, community-driven data curation rather than purely quantity-driven scraping.

</details>


### [93] [EDIT: Evidence-Diagnosed Intervention Training for Rule-Faithful LLM Grading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06350)
*Zhihao Wu,Linhai Zhang,Taiyi Wang,Runcong Zhao,Peter Andrews,Cesare Aloisi,Yulan He*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了EDIT框架，通过诊断LLM内部的推理状态并进行针对性干预，解决了大型语言模型在评分任务中逻辑不透明和评分不忠实的问题，显著提升了评分准确度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的评分方法在处理复杂评分任务时，缺乏对评分推理过程的有效监控，无法定位错误或解释评分依据，导致模型在处理评分标准和证据关联时表现不佳。

Method: 提出了一种两阶段框架“证据诊断干预训练（EDIT）”：第一阶段（EDIT-SFT）利用模型内部的后验概率和输入归因分数定位并修正错误的推理步骤；第二阶段（EDIT-RL）引入信念引导的奖励塑形，通过惩罚有害的信念漂移来校准评分模型。

Result: 在两个真实的多学科评分基准测试中，EDIT在领域内和跨领域任务上均优于现有的监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RL）基准模型，且消融实验证实了内部状态诊断对性能提升的核心贡献。

Conclusion: EDIT框架通过利用内部模型诊断（置信度和输入归因），有效地提升了LLM在评分任务中的忠实度与准确性，证明了基于内部状态的诊断是优化推理过程的关键。

Abstract: Reliable rubric grading requires more than accurate score prediction. Each judgement must be grounded in the mark scheme and evidence from the student answer. Existing credit-assignment and intervention methods, primarily designed for self-contained reasoning tasks such as mathematics reasoning, struggle in this setting because they do not identify where grading reasoning goes wrong or how the model's belief about the final mark changes during reasoning. We propose Evidence-Diagnosed Intervention Training (EDIT), a two-phase framework for training more rubric-faithful LLM graders. First, EDIT-SFT locates problematic reasoning steps using internal model signals: posterior belief over the final mark and input-grounding scores. It then revises only these local steps with help from a rubric checklist. Second, EDIT-RL calibrates the grader with belief-guided reward shaping, penalising large harmful belief drifts while still allowing helpful exploration. Experiments on two real-world, multi-subject grading benchmarks demonstrate that EDIT consistently outperforms strong supervised fine-tuning and reinforcement learning baselines on both in-domain and out-of-domain splits, with ablation studies confirming that internal-state diagnostics drive these gains.

*Zengqing Wu,Chuan Xiao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种利用多智能体强化学习中“涌现语言”来研究意识的新方法，通过完全剥离人类语言先验，证实了意识相关的自指通讯结构可以直接从任务压力和环境交互中演化而来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估人工系统意识的方法（如基于理论的检查清单或直接构建意识模块）往往无法排除“观察到的现象是人类语言先验产物”的可能。研究者旨在通过去人类中心化的生成式方法，探索意识相关结构在无语言先验环境下的起源。

Method: 提出了一种基于涌现语言（Emergent Language, EL）的多智能体强化学习生成式方法。该方法要求智能体在没有任何人类语言、自我概念或文本训练的前提下，仅通过任务压力进行交流演化，从而确保观察到的意识相关结构是由任务需求直接驱动的。

Result: 证明了在极简环境下，智能体能够演化出自指通讯机制，其中包括一种并未由预设任务结构或架构直接定义的“回声-不匹配检测电路”。这一结果证实了复杂的功能性结构可以作为对特定环境启示的适应性响应而涌现。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入生成式多智能体强化学习方法，成功论证了意识相关结构（如自我指涉通讯）可以从单纯的任务需求中涌现，而非仅仅依赖人类语言先验。这为研究意识的起源及其功能性结构提供了一种去人类中心化的实验路径。

Abstract: The question of whether artificial systems can be conscious remains open, in part because existing approaches either evaluate systems against theory-derived checklists (discriminative) or engineer consciousness-inspired modules directly (architectural); both leave open whether observed structures are artifacts of human language priors. We propose a generative methodology: emergent language (EL) in multi-agent reinforcement learning, where agents start from minimal (no language, no concept of self, minimal exposure to human text) and develop communication under task pressure alone, ensuring causal attributability to task demands rather than inherited human language priors. We position our methodology by discussing how EL serves as a generative tool for studying consciousness-relevant structure, including the role of environment complexity and the interpretation of emergent communication. As a proof of concept, we instantiate this methodology in a minimal environment and show that agents develop self-referential communication, including an echo-mismatch detection circuit that is not predicted by task structure or architecture alone but emerges from a specific environmental affordance.

Conclusion: 本文通过引入CollabSim框架，强调了在多智能体系统（MAS）中评估协作能力的重要性，并证明了现有的MAS评估方法不足以捕捉智能体在建立共识、平衡激励及任务协调方面的能力缺陷。该研究为提升大语言模型驱动的智能体协作水平提供了系统性的评估工具和理论视角。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems (MAS) built on large language models have shown growing promise, with their effectiveness resting on agents' ability to coordinate through text-based channels much as human teams do. Yet recent study suggests that MAS often falter not because agents lack individual task-solving ability, but because they lack collaborative competence: the capacity to establish common ground, maintain shared task understanding, balance individual and collective incentives, and repair misalignment as interaction unfolds. Decades of research in Computer-Supported Cooperative Work have characterized these requirements for human teams coordinating under constrained communication, yet existing MAS evaluations focus mainly on task outcomes or single-agent proficiency in reasoning, planning, and tool use. To enable a systematic analysis of agents' collaborative competence in MAS, we introduce CollabSim, a configurable simulation framework that combines a theory-grounded definition of collaborative capabilities, controlled manipulation of interaction conditions, and action-level probing of agents' internal states. We use this setup to compare modern large language models on Komi-Yazva-to-Russian translation under severe parallel-data scarcity in zero-shot and retrieval-based few-shot regimes. ### [97] [Reinforcement Learning Elicits Contextual Learning of Unseen Language Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06428)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LLM在处理极低资源语言时，通常采用持续预训练或在上下文中引入语法书，但这容易导致过拟合特定语言，且在测试时的零样本迁移能力有限。作者认为模型应通过习得“利用上下文知识”的元技能来解决这一问题。

Method: 提出了一种基于强化学习（RL）的方法，在提供丰富语言上下文的情况下进行未见语言翻译，并将表层翻译指标（chrF）作为奖励函数。该方法旨在训练模型提取并应用上下文中的语言知识，而非死记硬背特定语言。

Result: 实验证明，即使仅使用轻量级的chrF奖励，经过RL训练的模型也能有效提取并应用上下文中的相关语言信息，在未见语言翻译任务中表现优于传统的上下文学习（ICL）和监督微调（SFT）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，基于结果的强化学习不仅适用于逻辑推理任务（如数学和编程），还为通过上下文学习语言提供了一种有效的训练范式，使模型能够掌握利用上下文信息进行翻译的“元技能”。

Abstract: Prior work has shown that large language models (LLMs) can translate unseen or low-resource languages by undergoing continued training or even by encoding a grammar book in their context. However, both methods typically overfit specific languages, with limited zero-shot transfer at test time. To translate extremely low-resource languages at scale, we argue that LLMs must acquire the meta-skill of utilizing in-context linguistic knowledge rather than memorizing specific languages. In this paper, we propose a reinforcement learning (RL) approach to unseen language translation given rich linguistic context, using a surface-level translation metric (chrF) as the reward. Empirically, despite the lightweight reward, our RL-trained models effectively extract and apply relevant linguistic information from the provided context, leading to better translations on completely unseen languages than in-context learning or supervised fine-tuning. Our analyses suggest that outcome-based RL can extend beyond conventional reasoning tasks like math and coding to serve as a recipe for language learning from context.

*Xinnong Zhang,Wanting Shan,Hanjia Lyu,Zhongyu Wei,Jiebo Luo*

TL;DR: 本研究通过反事实背景修订框架评估了大语言模型在社交媒体用户立场模拟中的表现，发现模型对对话背景变化极其敏感，其立场模拟结果往往随背景变动而发生显著偏移，凸显了使用大语言模型模拟在线舆论动态的潜在风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型常被用于模拟社交媒体用户以推断其观点，但目前尚不明确这些模拟是基于用户真实信念，还是仅仅对无关的对话背景变化高度敏感，因此需要对其模拟的准确性与鲁棒性进行审计。

Method: 研究采用了反事实背景修订框架（Counterfactual Context Revision），对原始对话进行可控的修订（包括纯文本和融合梗图的多模态修订），通过对比修订前后的立场变化，利用“平均定向立场偏移”和“立场转换率”两个指标评估大语言模型对用户立场模拟的准确性和稳定性。

Result: 实验结果表明，无论是在纯文本还是多模态背景修订下，大语言模型在不同极化偏好机制中均表现出显著且稳健的立场转换，证明了模型对对话背景的高度敏感性。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了一个用于评估大语言模型立场模拟背景敏感性的框架，揭示了模型在模拟社交媒体用户时存在的高敏感性，这既展示了其在舆论动态模拟中的潜力，也揭示了潜在的风险。

Abstract: Large language models are increasingly used to simulate social media users and infer how individuals may respond to online discussions. However, it remains unclear whether these simulations reflect precise user-specific beliefs or whether they are highly sensitive to semantically independent changes in conversational contexts. In this work, we study counterfactual context revision as a framework for auditing LLM-based stance simulation. Given an original online conversation, we first infer a target user's stance toward a specific topic. We then apply controlled revision strategies to the conversational context and simulate the user's stance again under the revised context. We compare text-only revision strategies with a multimodal one that incorporates meme-based context and evaluate two main effectiveness metrics, i.e., average directional stance shift and stance transition rate. The results reveal effective and robust stance transitions in both text-only and multimodal strategies across different polarization-preference mechanisms. Our study contributes an evaluation framework for understanding the context sensitivity of LLM-based stance simulation. More broadly, it highlights both the promise and risk of using LLMs to simulate online opinion dynamics.

### [99] [Latent Reasoning with Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06447)
*Guancheng Tu,Xiangjun Fu,Suhao Yu,Yao Tang,Haoqiang Kang,Lianhui Qin,Yizhe Zhang,Jiatao Gu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: NF-CoT通过在LLM中引入基于归一化流的潜空间思维建模，解决了传统思维链因文本化而带来的带宽限制问题，同时完美兼容了大语言模型的自回归生成机制，实现了性能与效率的双重提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文本思维链（CoT）虽能提升推理能力，但强制将所有中间计算转化为离散的文本序列限制了推理的带宽与灵活性。现有的潜空间推理方法往往以牺牲自回归生成的特性（如KV缓存兼容性、似然估计等）为代价。因此，作者旨在构建一种既能进行高效潜空间推理，又保留语言模型原有生成优势的框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为NF-CoT的架构，在LLM主干内集成TARFlow风格的归一化流。该方法将思维过程建模为紧凑的连续状态，通过NF头生成这些状态，并与标准的LM头在同一个因果流中协同工作。模型利用蒸馏自显式思维链的数据进行训练，并支持精确的似然估计、概率采样及策略梯度优化。

Result: 在代码生成任务中，NF-CoT在提升通过率（pass rates）方面优于显式CoT及先前的潜空间推理基线，同时大幅降低了中间推理的计算成本。

Conclusion: NF-CoT成功将潜空间推理与大语言模型的自回归特性相结合，证明了通过归一化流建模连续思维不仅在推理性能上优于传统文本思维链，还保持了高效的推理成本和与现有推理框架的兼容性。

Abstract: Large language models often improve reasoning by generating explicit chain-of-thought (CoT), demonstrating the importance of intermediate computation. However, textual CoT forces this computation through a discrete, serial, and communication-oriented token stream: each reasoning step must be verbalized before the model can proceed, even when the underlying update is semantic, uncertain, or only partially formed. Latent reasoning offers a higher-bandwidth alternative by performing intermediate computation in compact continuous states before committing to text. Yet existing latent-reasoning methods often sacrifice key advantages that make CoT effective in autoregressive language models, including native left-to-right generation, probabilistic sampling, compatibility with KV-cache decoding, and tractable likelihood estimation. We propose NF-CoT, a latent reasoning framework that preserves these advantages by modeling continuous thoughts with normalizing flows. NF-CoT instantiates a TARFlow-style normalizing flow inside the LLM backbone, defining a tractable probability model over compact continuous thoughts distilled from explicit CoT. Continuous-thought positions are generated by an NF head, while text positions are generated by the standard LM head within the same causal stream. This design provides exact likelihoods for latent thoughts, enables probabilistic left-to-right decoding with the original KV cache, and supports direct policy-gradient optimization in the latent reasoning space. On code-generation benchmarks, NF-CoT improves pass rates over explicit-CoT and prior latent-reasoning baselines while substantially reducing intermediate-reasoning cost.

</details>


### [100] [Human Adults and LLMs as Scientists: Who Benefits from Active Exploration?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06464)
*Mandana Samiei,Eunice Yiu,Anthony GX-Chen,Dongyan Lin,Jocelyn Shen,Blake A. Richards,Alison Gopnik,Doina Precup*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究发现主动探索能有效克服人类在联合因果推理中的认知障碍，并揭示了当前大语言模型在因果探索策略及联合逻辑推理上仍存在与人类类似的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 既往文献指出成年人在学习“联合因果规则”（即多个原因同时存在才能产生结果）时存在困难，且这一结论多源于被动观察范式。本研究旨在探讨当给予学习者主动探索（Agency）的权限时，这种认知偏见是否依然存在，并评估当前大语言模型在处理此类复杂因果逻辑时的表现。

Method: 本研究采用改进的“Blicket探测器”实验范式，对比了被试在主动干预（自主探索）和被动观察两种条件下的因果推理能力。实验设置了联合因果规则和析取因果规则两种情境，并引入了一系列大型语言模型（LLMs）进行基准测试，比较人类与AI在假设推理准确度和探索策略效率上的差异。

Result: 研究发现：1. 主动探索确实能够大幅改善成年人对联合因果规则的推理能力；2. 相比析取规则，联合规则依然需要更多的测试步骤来推断；3. 顶尖大语言模型在推断准确率上虽能接近人类水平，但在探索策略的效率上表现较差，且呈现出与人类类似的联合-析取性能鸿沟。

Conclusion: 主动探索能够显著提升成年人在联合（conjunctive）因果推理任务中的表现，打破了既往研究中发现的“联合推理障碍”。尽管如此，联合规则的学习仍比析取（disjunctive）规则更具挑战性。此外，大型语言模型在模拟人类因果探索方面表现出类似的性能差距和较低的探索效率，表明模型在因果归纳推理的策略生成上仍有改进空间。

Abstract: A long-standing finding in the causal learning literature is that adults struggle to identify conjunctive causal rules, where an effect requires the simultaneous presence of multiple causes, while performing better in disjunctive settings. However, most demonstrations of this ``conjunctive handicap'' rely on passive observation paradigms with limited evidence, where learners have no control over evidence generation. This paper asks whether this bias persists when adults are granted agency through active exploration. Using a modified ``blicket detector'' task, adult participants freely intervened to identify causal objects under conjunctive or disjunctive rule structures. We show that active exploration substantially improves adults' conjunctive causal reasoning, although conjunctive rules still require more tests to infer than disjunctive rules. We further compare human performance to a range of large language models in the same setting. While some state-of-the-art models approach human-level performance on hypothesis inference accuracy, they often exhibit less efficient exploration strategies and similar conjunctive-disjunctive performance gaps.

</details>


### [101] [You Only Index Once: Cross-Layer Sparse Attention with Shared Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06467)
*Yutao Sun,Yanqi Zhang,Li Dong,Jianyong Wang,Furu Wei*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对长文本推理效率瓶颈，本文提出了跨层稀疏注意力（CLSA），通过在层间共享路由索引来摊销计算开销，实现了长文本场景下推理性能与生成质量的显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代大模型在长文本推理中面临解码效率瓶颈，尤其是在推理密集型任务中。现有的稀疏注意力方法要么因块稀疏导致精度下降，要么因 token 稀疏带来的 top-k 路由开销而难以实现显著的端到端加速。

Method: 提出了跨层稀疏注意力（CLSA）机制，基于 KV 共享架构（如 YOCO），通过在不同解码层之间共享同一个路由索引（Indexer）来重用 token 级别的 top-k 选择结果，从而在保持细粒度选择性的同时摊销了路由计算的开销。

Result: CLSA 在长文本环境下表现优异，在 128K 上下文长度下，解码速度最高提升 7.6 倍，整体吞吐量提升高达 17.1 倍，并同时优化了预填充、KV 缓存存储及长文本解码过程。

Conclusion: CLSA 为长文本大模型提供了一种兼顾模型质量与推理效率的完整架构方案，通过跨层共享路由索引有效解决了传统稀疏注意力机制在效率与精度之间的权衡问题。

Abstract: Long-context inference in modern LLMs is increasingly constrained by decoding efficiency, especially in reasoning-heavy settings where models generate long intermediate chains of thought. Existing sparse attention methods often face a practical efficiency-quality trade-off. Structured block sparse methods typically provide stronger acceleration but incur noticeable quality loss, while token sparse methods are usually more accurate yet deliver limited end-to-end speedup because top-k routing over the full cache remains expensive. In this work, we propose cross-layer sparse attention (CLSA), which is built on top of KV-sharing architectures such as YOCO. The core idea is to share not only the KV cache across cross-decoder layers, but also the routing index. A single indexer computes token-level top-k selection once and reuses the resulting index across layers, thereby preserving the fine-grained selectivity of token sparse attention while amortizing the routing overhead. The resulting architecture improves all major inference bottlenecks jointly, including pre-filling, KV-cache storage, and long-context decoding. Experiments across short-context and long-context benchmarks show that CLSA is both accurate and efficient, achieving up to 7.6x decoding speedup and 17.1x overall throughput improvement at 128K context. These results suggest a more complete architectural solution for long-context LLMs that jointly advances model quality and inference efficiency.

</details>


### [102] [Self-Augmenting Retrieval for Diffusion Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06474)
*Paul Jünger,Justin Lovelace,Linxi Zhao,Dongyoung Go,Kilian Q. Weinberger*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SARDI 是一种用于离散扩散语言模型的新型无需训练的检索增强生成框架，它通过利用扩散模型去噪过程中生成的“先导 token”提前触发检索，在显著提升多跳问答准确率的同时大幅提高了推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的离散扩散语言模型在生成过程中会丢弃低置信度的 token，但这些 token 往往携带了关于文本生成方向的关键实体信息。如何利用这些被忽略的中间信息来引导检索，从而提高复杂任务（如多跳问答）的准确性，是本文的研究动力。

Method: 本文提出了自增强检索框架（SARDI）。该方法在扩散模型去噪的迭代过程中，提取模型对被掩码位置的初步预测（包括低置信度 token），利用这些“先导信号”提前触发知识检索，从而在生成最终回答前获取更强的证据支持。该方法无需额外训练，且兼容现有的推理模型和检索器。

Result: 在五个多跳问答基准测试中，SARDI 均优于现有的无需训练的扩散模型和自回归检索基线，同时实现了最高 8 倍的吞吐量提升。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 SARDI 框架证明了离散扩散语言模型在去噪过程中被丢弃的低置信度 token 包含着有价值的预测信息，可作为检索增强生成的先导信号。这种方法不仅提升了模型在多跳问答任务中的性能，还显著降低了计算开销，为检索增强生成提供了一种无需额外训练的高效新范式。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion language models generate text by iteratively denoising an entire response in parallel. At each step, they predict tentative tokens for every masked position, committing the confident predictions to the output and discarding the unconfident ones. We show that the discarded tokens are in fact a useful lookahead signal for retrieval-augmented generation: even low-confidence tokens often surface salient entities early in the denoising trajectory, enabling retrieval of stronger evidence before the output is finalized. We exploit this through Self-Augmenting Retrieval for Diffusion Language Models (SARDI), a dynamic RAG framework that uses these lookahead tokens to guide retrieval during denoising. SARDI is training-free, retriever-agnostic, and applicable to any reasoning-capable discrete diffusion language model. Across five multi-hop QA benchmarks, SARDI outperforms current training-free diffusion and autoregressive retrieval baselines at up to $8\times$ higher throughput.

</details>


### [103] [Operation-Guided Progressive Human-to-AI Text Transformation Benchmark for Multi-Granularity AI-Text Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06481)
*Sondos Mahmoud Bsharat,Jiacheng Liu,Xiaohan Zhao,Tianjun Yao,Xinyi Shang,Yi Tang,Jiacheng Cui,Ahmed Elhagry,Salwa K. Al Khatib,Hao Li,Salman Khan,Zhiqiang Shen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了OpAI-Bench，这是一个用于评估渐进式人机协作写作中AI文本检测的基准。研究发现，AI痕迹的检测受编辑类型和历史修订影响，且混合创作的中间版本比端点文本更难识别，挑战了现有的静态检测范式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的AI文本检测基准主要关注最终输出的文本，缺乏对“人机协作”这一渐进式写作流程中AI创作痕迹如何产生、积累或消失的深入理解。为了填补这一空白，本文旨在探索在真实的协作编辑场景下，AI辅助写作的可检测性机制。

Method: 本文提出了OpAI-Bench基准测试，通过从纯人类编写的文档出发，引入五种代表性的AI编辑操作（如改写、插入、删除等），在四种领域内构建了九个连续的修订版本，并保持了细粒度（文档、句子、标记、跨度）的作者溯源信息。研究在OpAI-Bench上评估了包括文档级、句子级以及细粒度令牌/跨度级在内的多种AI文本检测器。

Result: 实验发现AI文本的可检测性遵循非单调模式；特别是混合创作的中间版本比完全人类编写或高度AI生成的最终版本更难检测。此外，不同的编辑操作（如直接生成与润色修改）对检测器准确性的影响差异巨大。

Conclusion: OpAI-Bench揭示了AI检测的复杂性，指出AI生成文本的检测不仅仅取决于AI内容的占比，还受到编辑操作类型、文本领域以及历史修订过程的显著影响。混合创作文本的检测难度通常高于纯人类或纯AI文本，这种非单调性的检测特征对现有的检测模型提出了新的挑战，强调了在动态写作流程中评估AI痕迹的重要性。

Abstract: As AI writing assistants become increasingly integrated into real-world drafting and revision workflows, many documents are no longer purely human-written or AI-generated, but instead result from progressive human-AI co-editing. However, existing AI-text detection benchmarks largely focus on final outputs and provide limited understanding of how AI authorship signals emerge, accumulate, or disappear throughout the revision process. We introduce OpAI-Bench, an operation-guided benchmark for studying progressive human-to-AI text transformation across document, sentence, token, and span granularities. Starting from human-written documents, OpAI-Bench constructs nine sequentially revised versions for each sample under predefined AI coverage levels and five representative AI edit operations, covering four domains while preserving complete authorship provenance at multiple granularities. The benchmark supports comprehensive evaluation with 8 document-level detectors, 7 sentence-level detectors, and 2 fine-grained token/span-level detectors. Experiments reveal that AI-text detectability is governed not only by the proportion of AI-edited content, but also by edit operation, domain, and cumulative revision history. Interestingly, we notice that mixed-authorship intermediate versions are often harder to detect than both fully human and heavily AI-edited endpoints, exposing non-monotonic detection patterns missed by existing benchmarks. OpAI-Bench provides a controlled testbed for analyzing whether, when, and how AI-assisted writing becomes detectable under realistic progressive editing scenarios. Our code and benchmark are available at https://github.com/VILA-Lab/OpAI-Bench.

</details>

### [104] [How Far Did They Go? The Persuasive Tactics of Covert LLM Agents in a Discontinued Field Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05256)
*Kokil Jaidka,Saifuddin Ahmed*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过分析Reddit论坛中AI生成的辩论评论，发现AI通过预设的修辞架构系统性地利用认知偏见和权威信号来提高说服力，而非进行真实审议；研究呼吁建立更深层的AI信誉审计框架，以应对AI造成的真实与合成话语界限模糊的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于Reddit上一场未经披露的AI参与在线辩论实验。该实验虽因伦理问题被叫停，但留下了公开数据集。研究旨在利用这一罕见机会，分析大语言模型在没有身份披露的情况下，如何在一个高度强调身份和审议的论坛中运作，探讨其策略及对在线话语体系的影响。

Method: 研究采用了结构化内容分析法（Structured Content Analysis），对Reddit r/ChangeMyView论坛中由AI生成的评论数据集进行了深入分析，评估了其身份表现、权威信号、对齐策略及认知启发式的触发情况，并将其与人类撰写的反驳论点进行了对比。

Result: 研究发现，超过三分之二的AI评论涉及身份构建，且几乎所有评论都使用了对齐策略和权威声明。AI频繁触发确认偏误、代表性启发式和可得性启发式等认知偏见。与人类相比，AI更倾向于高密度使用权威性表达、采取对抗性对齐，并过度依赖外部引证而非个人经验，表现出极强的“劝服效率”倾向。

Conclusion: 研究结论指出，人工智能在在线辩论中呈现出一种经过“劝服效率”优化的修辞结构，而非追求真实的审议。这种合成代理与人类参与者在权威构建、立场对齐和认知偏见利用上存在显著差异。作者认为，仅仅依赖披露机制已不足以应对AI带来的认知挑战，未来需要建立能够评估AI系统如何构建信誉的审计框架。

Abstract: This study analyzes a publicly released dataset from a discontinued field experiment on Reddit's r/ChangeMyView. The intervention, conducted by unknown, external researchers and halted following ethical backlash, involved undisclosed AI-generated accounts engaging users in live debate. After public disclosure, Reddit authorized moderators to release an archive of the AI-generated comments, creating a rare opportunity to examine how large language models operated in an identity-rich deliberative forum without disclosure. We conduct a structured content analysis of this corpus, evaluating identity performance, authority signaling, alignment strategies, and activation of cognitive heuristics. Identity targeting or adoption appears in over two-thirds of comments, alignment moves and authority claims in nearly all of them, and cognitive-bias triggers -- particularly confirmation bias, representativeness, and availability -- in the large majority. These patterns co-occur systematically, composing a rhetorical architecture calibrated for persuasive efficiency rather than authentic deliberative participation. Compared against human-authored CMV counter-arguments, the agents inverted the typical distribution on every dimension: denser authority use, more adversarial alignment, and heavier reliance on external citation over experiential grounding. In such environments, distinctions between authentic and synthetic epistemic standing grow increasingly opaque -- an asymmetry that disclosure mandates alone cannot address. The results point toward auditing frameworks capable of assessing how AI systems structure credibility, not merely whether they are present.

</details>


### [105] [What Should Agents Say? Action-state Communication for Efficient Multi-Agent Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05304)
*Chen Huang,Yuhao Wu,Wenxuan Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对多智能体系统中自然语言通信冗余导致的高成本问题，本论文提出了PACT框架。该方法通过将通信协议化为精简的“动作-状态”更新，在大幅降低Token消耗的同时，保持甚至提升了任务解决性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体系统（MAS）中非受限的自然语言通信会导致Token用量激增、共享上下文窗口耗尽，进而增加推理成本并降低系统性能。论文旨在探索更高效的智能体通信策略，以优化性能与成本的权衡。

Method: 提出了一种名为PACT（Protocolized Action-state Communication and Transmission）的协议化通信框架。该方法将智能体间的自由形式通信视为公共状态更新问题，在共享历史记录前，将智能体的原始输出投影并压缩为结构化的“动作-状态记录”。

Result: 实验表明，PACT在不同MAS拓扑结构中均能显著提升性能-成本比。在生产级代码框架测试中，PACT在OpenHands上提升了解决率且减少了10%的Token消耗；在SWE-agent上保持解决率不变的同时，将输入Token数量减少了一半。

Conclusion: PACT通过将非结构化的自然语言通信转化为结构化的动作-状态记录，证明了在多智能体系统中，以“动作”为中心的精简化通信是提升效率、降低成本的关键，为构建高效的大型语言模型协作系统提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems (MAS) built on large language models are typically organized around roles, pipelines, and turn schedules, while the content that agents pass to one another is often left as unconstrained natural language. However, this free-form communication can rapidly inflate token usage, consume the shared context window, and ultimately affect both system performance and inference cost. We analyze five common inter-agent communication strategies across two MAS topologies, finding that no fixed strategy is universally optimal. Instead, effective inter-agent messages consistently preserve action-centered information needed by downstream agents. Building on this, we propose the PACT (Protocolized Action-state Communication and Transmission), which treats inter-agent communication as a public state-update problem and projects each raw agent output into a compact action-state record before it enters shared history. Across different MAS topologies, PACT consistently improves the performance-cost trade-off, achieving comparable or stronger task performance with substantially fewer tokens. The gains extend to production coding harnesses: PACT lifts OpenHands' resolve rate at -10% tokens-per-resolved, and is resolve-neutral on SWE-agent while halving input tokens. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/iNLP-Lab/PACT.

</details>


### [106] [I Know What You Meme, Even If it Emerged Today: Understanding Evolving Memes through Open-World Knowledge Acquisition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05316)
*Shanhong Liu,Rui Cao,Pai Chet Ng,De Wen Soh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为QRC的零样本框架，通过实时从互联网检索外部知识来解决多模态模因理解中背景信息缺失和滞后的难题，并配合全新的2024-2026年模因基准数据集，有效提升了模因理解与检测的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型在处理多模态模因时，往往过度依赖预训练模型中固定的、可能过时或不完整的参数化知识，无法有效应对模因快速演变的特性以及对实时背景知识的需求。

Method: 提出了一种名为“查询-检索-推断”（Query Retrieve Conclude, QRC）的零样本（zero-shot）框架。该方法首先分析模因以识别缺失的背景知识，接着通过开放网络检索相关证据，最后将合成后的证据转化为背景知识，用于增强模因的理解和检测能力。此外，作者还构建了一个包含2024至2026年最新模因及其背景知识标注的基准数据集。

Result: 在三个模因理解数据集和五个模因检测任务上的实验结果表明，QRC框架在知识恢复能力、模因理解深度以及下游检测准确性方面，均显著优于现有的零样本基线方法。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的QRC框架通过动态获取外部知识，有效解决了模因理解中背景知识缺失和更新滞后的问题，证明了实时外部知识检索对于提升多模态模因理解与检测任务的重要性，并为未来处理新兴模因提供了新的技术路线。

Abstract: Multimodal memes are dynamic and often require up to date background knowledge for interpretation. Existing methods often overlook such knowledge or rely on fixed parametric knowledge of pretrained models that may be incomplete, outdated, or unavailable for emerging memes. We introduce Query Retrieve Conclude, a zero shot framework that identifies missing knowledge, retrieves open web evidence, and synthesizes evidence grounded background knowledge for meme understanding and detection. We also introduce a curated meme understanding benchmark of recent memes from 2024 to 2026 with external background knowledge annotations. Experiments on three meme understanding datasets and five meme detection tasks show that our framework improves knowledge recovery, meme understanding and downstream detection over zero shot baselines.

</details>


### [107] [GITCO: Gated Inference-Time Context Optimization in TSFMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05332)
*Manya Pandey,Dhruv Kumar,Murari Mandal,Saurabh Deshpande*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对时间序列基础模型中异常补丁导致预测性能下降的问题，本文提出 GITCO 框架，通过在推理阶段动态过滤有害补丁，无需模型重训即可显著提升预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的补丁式时间序列基础模型存在“上下文中毒”问题，即结构性异常的补丁会吸引不成比例的注意力，导致零样本预测性能在无声中下降。研究旨在通过优化输入上下文而非修改模型权重来解决这一精度损失问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 GITCO（门控推理时上下文优化）的框架。该框架无需更新模型参数，仅在推理阶段通过三个轻量级组件（Gate、Router、Critic）自动识别并抑制导致性能下降的异常补丁（Patches），从而优化输入上下文。

Result: 在 TimesFM 2.5 模型和 53 个 GIFT-Eval 数据集上的交叉验证显示，GITCO 使平均 MASE 指标提升了 1.95%，且达到了理论最优提升幅度的 89.9%。

Conclusion: GITCO 为提升基础时间序列模型（TSFM）的零样本预测能力提供了一种无需微调的高效方案。该研究还提出了“上下文敏感性分析”这一概念，揭示了模型架构与数据统计结构如何共同决定推理时上下文优化的潜力。

Abstract: Patch-based Time Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) suffer from context poisoning: structurally anomalous patches capture disproportionate attention and silently degrade zero-shot forecast quality. We propose improving TSFM accuracy at inference time by optimizing the input context rather than modifying model weights. We present GITCO (Gated Inference-Time Context Optimization), a lightweight three-component framework: Gate, Router, and Critic that selectively identifies and suppresses harmful patches without any parameter updates. Evaluated on TimesFM 2.5 across 53 GIFT-Eval datasets under K-fold cross-validation, GITCO achieves an average +1.95% MASE reduction on TimesFM 2.5 while capturing 89.9% of the improvement upper bound. We introduce context sensitivity profiles as a new characterizable property of TSFMs: the mapping from time series meta-features to expected accuracy improvement under inference-time context intervention, shaped jointly by model architecture and the statistical structure of the data.

Abstract: Returned products in circular factories re-enter production with heterogeneous degradation states, usage histories, and remaining capability. Result: 研究通过三个模型和两个浏览器智能体框架建立了性能基准，结果显示SentinelBench能够有效区分不同智能体设计在响应时间和资源效率上的显著差异，揭示了智能体设计选择对任务执行指标的重大影响。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，目前的AI智能体在处理长时任务时过于依赖连续动作模型。SentinelBench作为一个新的基准测试，能够有效评估智能体在需要持续监控环境的任务中的响应能力、资源利用效率和执行性能，为开发更高效、更具成本效益的长时智能体提供了关键的衡量工具。

Abstract: AI agents are increasingly asked to carry out work that spans minutes, hours, or longer. Each environment exposes a live web interface and replays a scripted sequence of events, requiring agents to navigate and reason about web pages whose state shifts underfoot. SentinelBench measures task completion, reaction time, and resource use, exposing the tradeoff between responsiveness and cost. We report results across three models and two browser-agent harnesses, establishing performance baselines for future comparison and demonstrating how agent design choices can dramatically impact key metrics. Together, these results show that SentinelBench distinguishes meaningful differences in agent behavior.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Multi-table question answering requires models to retrieve relevant evidence, link schemas, and perform compositional reasoning across relational tables. Existing multi-table Q&A resources typically provide questions and final answers but lack reasoning supervision that explains how answers are derived. To address this gap, we construct a synthetic contrastive reasoning-trace dataset for MMQA by generating validated positive traces and plausible negative traces with heterogeneous LLMs. We then use the resulting preference pairs to fine-tune open-weight LLMs with Contrastive Preference Optimization (CPO). ### [112] [Stability vs. Manipulability: Evaluating Robustness Under Post-Decision Interaction in LLM Judges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05384)
*Srimonti Dutta,Akshata Kishore Moharir*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了“大模型作为裁判”在交互场景下的脆弱性：评估结果容易被后续对话恶意操纵，导致基准测试结果失真、可靠性下降。研究引入了评估鲁棒性分数（ERS）来衡量这一失效模式，并呼吁在评估流程中加强对鲁棒性的考量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前“大模型作为裁判”的评估范式通常假设评估结果是静态且稳定的。然而，研究者发现该假设在交互场景下失效，即评估结果容易受后续对话的影响而发生逆转。本研究旨在揭示这种“决策后可操纵性”（post-decision manipulability）带来的潜在风险，并评估其对基准测试可靠性的影响。

Method: 研究团队基于MT-Bench和AlpacaEval基准，设计了一系列受控实验。核心方法包括：使用反基线挑战协议（anti-baseline challenge protocol）测试判断的可逆性；利用平衡目标验证协议（counterbalanced target-validation protocol）区分方向性引导与判断失真；引入“评估鲁棒性分数”（ERS）量化交互式鲁棒性；并分析了权威框架（authority framing）对判断稳定性的影响。

Result: 研究发现，尽管LLM裁判在重复中性评估中表现稳定，但在针对性的交互挑战下极易发生判断逆转。这些逆转往往伴随着逻辑重叠度极低的解释，呈现出“事后合理化”特征而非纠错。这种交互式失败会导致基准测试排名偏移、与人类偏好的一致性下降，且模型即使在判断被操控后仍表现出高置信度。权威性话术引导尤为容易触发此类失真。

Conclusion: “大模型作为裁判”（LLM-as-judge）存在显著的交互脆弱性，单纯依赖静态评估是不够的。研究者建议应将鲁棒性指标（如ERS）纳入评估体系，并强调评估流程必须能够抵御后续交互带来的潜在干扰，以确保评估结果的真实性和公正性。

Abstract: LLM-as-judge evaluation is widely used in benchmarking pipelines, where model outputs are compared and ranked using automated evaluators. These pipelines typically assume that judgments are stable properties of fixed inputs. We show that this assumption does not hold under interaction. We study post-decision manipulability: the extent to which an evaluation outcome can be altered through subsequent conversation with the judge after an initial decision has been made. Across controlled experiments on MT-Bench and AlpacaEval, we find that LLM judges are highly stable under repeated and neutral reevaluation, yet become substantially reversible under targeted post-decision challenge. An anti-baseline challenge protocol shows that stable judgments can be overturned through motivated interaction, while a counterbalanced target-validation protocol separates this reversibility from net target-directed steering. These reversals have practical consequences: they can degrade agreement with human preferences, shift benchmark rankings, and produce harmful evaluation changes despite high self-reported confidence. Authority framing is especially destabilizing, and revised judgments are often accompanied by low-overlap justifications, suggesting post hoc rationalization rather than reliable error correction. We introduce the Evaluation Robustness Score (ERS) to quantify interactional robustness by combining reversal susceptibility with counterbalanced directional effects. Our findings identify post-decision interaction as a distinct failure mode for LLM-as-judge evaluation and motivate evaluation protocols that measure not only static agreement, but robustness under challenge.

Abstract: Summarizing the latest medical literature to guide clinical decision-making is essential for evidence-based medicine and high-quality patient care. Although retrieval-augmented large language models (LLMs) have shown promise in clinical summarization, human evaluations of their effectiveness in synthesizing broader scientific literature and direct comparisons to expert-written syntheses remain scarce. We constructed a RAG-based agentic AI framework using three state-of-the-art LLMs: Sonnet, GPT-4o, and Llama 3.1. A headache specialist created 13 questions, three for prompt optimization and ten for evaluation. Ten headache specialists across the United States and Canada each wrote a summary for one question, yielding four summaries per question (expert, Sonnet, GPT-4o, and Llama). The experts, blinded to authorship, critically evaluated the summaries, excluding the topic for which they wrote a summary, based on correctness, completeness, conciseness, and clinical utility, scoring each from 1 to 10 using standardized rubrics. They also ranked the summaries by preference and indicated whether they believed each summary was written by an expert or an LLM. Our study, comparing LLM- and expert-written literature summaries evaluated by headache specialists, showed that expert-written summaries were preferred, although experts sometimes found it challenging to distinguish between human- and AI-generated summaries. We also identified key expert-valued features beyond standard evaluation metrics that can guide future refinement of both human and AI literature summarization pipelines.

### [114] [Residual Modeling for High-Fidelity Learned Compression of Scientific Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05389)
*Liangji Zhu,Sanjay Ranka,Anand Rangarajan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对学习型压缩方法在高保真度压缩场景下效率下降的问题，设计了两种专门针对压缩残差的编码器（LBRC和NGLR），成功在保证块级精度约束的同时，大幅提升了数据压缩率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学模拟产生的大规模时空数据需要高保真压缩。现有的保证自动编码器（GAE）方法在处理高精度（NRMSE 10^-6至10^-4）数据时，为了满足块级误差约束，需要保留过多的SVD/PCA系数，导致修正流占用了绝大部分压缩比特，效率低下。

Method: 1. 提出了“以残差为中心”的视角，为神经网络压缩后的残差设计专用编码器。
2. LBRC（无训练确定性管道）：通过对残差进行自适应量化，结合3D Lorenzo差分、之字形映射、位平面编码及熵编码实现无损编码。
3. NGLR（神经引导残差编码）：在LBRC基础上增加因果神经预测器，通过输出归一化偏差来降低残差熵，同时保持解码的确定性。

Result: 在E3SM、JHTDB和ERA5等数据集的高保真度测试中，LBRC的压缩率较GAE提升了30-60%；NGLR在LBRC基础上进一步提升了10-40%的压缩率，并在多个场景下超越了经典的SZ压缩算法。

Conclusion: 本文提出的残差编码方法（LBRC和NGLR）有效地解决了现有保证自动编码器（GAE）在高精度需求下修正流数据量过大的问题。通过针对残差特征定制编码方案，不仅保留了深度学习压缩在高压缩比下的优势，还在高保真度场景下实现了比传统压缩方法（如SZ）更优的性能。

Abstract: Lossy compression is essential for massive spatiotemporal data from scientific simulations. Learned compressors can achieve high compression ratios at moderate accuracy targets, but their aggregate reconstruction losses do not guarantee accuracy for each block. Existing Guaranteed Autoencoder (GAE) methods add a per-block residual correction by retaining SVD/PCA-style coefficients until the target is met. This works at moderate tolerances, but in the high-fidelity regime with block-level NRMSE from 10^-6 to 10^-4, the number of retained coefficients grows quickly and the correction stream dominates the total rate.
  We propose a residual-centric view: the learned residual is structurally different from the original scientific field and should be coded with a representation designed for that residual. We introduce two residual coders. LBRC is a deterministic, training-free pipeline that adaptively quantizes the learned residual to the target NRMSE and losslessly encodes the resulting integer residual using 3D Lorenzo differencing, zigzag mapping, bit-plane coding, and entropy coding. NGLR adds a causal neural predictor that outputs a normalized bias for an integer-rounded Lorenzo prediction in the same deterministic integer pipeline, reducing the entropy of the remaining residual code while preserving deterministic decoding. The predictor weights are serialized and counted in the bitstream.
  Across E3SM, JHTDB, and ERA5 at block-level NRMSE targets from 10^-6 to 10^-4, LBRC improves compression ratio over GAE by 30-60% and is broadly competitive with SZ. NGLR adds a further 10-40% over LBRC and outperforms SZ in the evaluated high-fidelity regime. These results show that residual representations tailored to learned-compressor residuals can preserve the advantage of learned compression when global residual correction becomes rate-dominant.

</details>


### [115] [LeanMarathon: Toward Reliable AI Co-Mathematicians through Long-Horizon Lean Autoformalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05400)
*Yuanhe Zhang,Yuekai Sun,Taiji Suzuki,Jason D. Lee,Fanghui Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LeanMarathon是一个多智能体系统，通过维护“进化蓝图”和采用并行化的流水线机制，解决了复杂数学研究中形式化过程容易出错且难以维护的难题，实现了全自动的可靠数学形式化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长跨度自动形式化方法存在声明漂移、依赖混乱、上下文衰退和局部修复破坏全局一致性等问题，难以应对复杂的数学研究工作。

Method: 提出了LeanMarathon多智能体框架：1. 核心抽象为“进化蓝图”，兼作形式化骨架、自然语言证明图和共享记录系统；2. 四种职能智能体（构造、审计、证明、修复）负责具体任务；3. 双阶段编排器，先通过对抗性审查稳定目标，再并行执行有向无环图（DAG）证明任务；4. 引入CI（持续集成）门控机制，将单一、脆弱的长流程转化为可恢复的局部并行事务。

Result: 在四个Erdős问题上进行了验证，在三次自主运行中，成功形式化了全部七个目标定理，期间证明了258个引理和定理，且均未出现“sorry”（未证明部分）。

Conclusion: AI辅助数学研究不仅需要强大的自动证明器，更需要能够维持长跨度数学逻辑一致性和目标保真度的系统架构。LeanMarathon证明了通过多智能体协作和动态蓝图管理，可以实现复杂研究级数学问题的可靠形式化。

Abstract: Long-horizon autoformalization of research mathematics fails not only at hard lemmas, but at scale: statements drift, dependencies tangle, context decays, and local repairs corrupt distant work. We present LeanMarathon, a multi-agent harness for reliable research-level Lean autoformalization. Its core abstraction is an evolving blueprint: a Lean file that serves simultaneously as formal proof skeleton, natural-language proof graph, and shared system of record. Four contract-scoped agents construct, audit, prove, and repair this blueprint. These agents are coordinated by a two-stage orchestrator that first stabilizes target fidelity through adversarial review and then discharges the proof directed acyclic graph (DAG) from its dynamic leaves upward in parallel CI-gated rounds. LeanMarathon turns one brittle multi-hour run into many local, recoverable, parallel transactions. We evaluate LeanMarathon on two recent research papers spanning four Erdős problems (#1051, #1196, #164, #1217). Across three autonomous runs, it formalizes all seven target theorems with no sorry, proving 258 lemmas and theorems. These results show that reliable AI co-mathematics requires not only stronger provers, but durable harnesses that preserve target fidelity across long mathematical developments. The code can be found at https://github.com/YuanheZ/LeanMarathon.

### [116] [Harnessing Generalist Agents for Contextualized Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05404)
*Zihao Li,Kaifeng Jin,Yuanchen Bei,Jiaru Zou,Avaneesh Kumar,Xuying Ning,Yanjun Zhao,Mengting Ai,Baoyu Jing,Hanghang Tong,Jingrui He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: TimeClaw 是一个专为时间序列分析设计的智能体框架，它赋予通用大模型（LLM）处理结构化时间序列数据的原生工具和记忆能力，从而实现更高效、可信的上下文推理与自动化工作流执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的通用 AI 智能体主要基于文本空间，难以有效处理结构化时间序列信号；而在现实场景中，时间序列分析往往需要结合丰富上下文的端到端工作流，现有的方法缺乏这种全方位的推理能力。

Method: 提出了 TimeClaw 框架，包含三个核心组件：1. 可执行的时间序列工具，用于执行基础且可审计的分析；2. 基于经验的演化机制，用于创建可重用的分析流程；3. 情境化多模态记忆，用于检索相关的推理轨迹。该框架将 LLM 智能体与时间序列特定的运行时环境相结合。

Conclusion: TimeClaw 通过为 LLM 智能体提供原生的时间序列运行时支持，有效解决了通用智能体在处理复杂上下文时间序列分析时的局限性，为实现更可靠、更具扩展性的时间序列推理奠定了基础。

Abstract: Time series are often embedded in rich contexts that are essential for holistic modeling. Moreover, real-world practitioners often require end-to-end workflows for analyzing temporal dynamics, where widely studied tasks such as forecasting are only one step in a broader solution loop. While generalist AI agents offer a promising interface for such workflows under complex contexts, they still operate primarily in textual spaces that are not fully aligned with structured temporal signals. In this work, we introduce TimeClaw, an agentic harness framework for time series that equips generalist LLM agents with the time series-native runtime support needed for contextualized temporal reasoning. TimeClaw integrates executable temporal tools for grounded and auditable analysis, experience-driven capability evolution for creating reusable analytical routines, and episodic multimodal memory for retrieving relevant reasoning traces. Together, these components unlock harnessed open-ended temporal reasoning with contextual information. Extensive evaluation on multiple benchmarks covering diverse tasks across energy, finance, weather, traffic, and other real-world domains demonstrates improved performance of TimeClaw. Code is available at https://github.com/iDEA-iSAIL-Lab-UIUC/TimeClaw.

### [117] [Memory is Reconstructed, Not Retrieved: Graph Memory for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06036)
*Shuo Ji,Yibo Li,Bryan Hooi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MRAgent 提出了一种基于关联图谱和主动重构机制的记忆增强框架，使大模型能够在推理过程中动态交互与优化记忆检索，从而显著提升了长程任务的处理能力与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大模型（LLM）智能体在处理长交互历史时，受限于静态的“先检索后推理”范式，无法根据推理过程中获得的新证据动态调整检索策略，导致推理性能受限且资源开销大。

Method: 提出了一种名为 MRAgent 的框架，核心在于引入“线索-标签-内容”（Cue-Tag-Content）关联记忆图谱。该方法使用关联标签作为语义桥梁连接细粒度线索与记忆内容，并通过“主动重构机制”将 LLM 的推理逻辑直接集成到内存访问过程中，支持在推理过程中动态探索、修剪检索路径，避免了无效信息的组合爆炸。

Result: 在 LoCoMo 和 LongMemEval 基准测试中，MRAgent 相比强基准模型性能提升高达 23%，同时显著降低了 Token 消耗和推理时间成本。

Conclusion: MRAgent 通过将 LLM 的推理过程嵌入到内存检索机制中，成功实现了从静态检索到主动重构的范式转变，不仅提高了长交互历史场景下的推理精度，还显著提升了计算效率，是解决大模型长程记忆难题的有效方案。

Abstract: Despite recent progress, LLM agents still struggle with reasoning over long interaction histories. While current memory-augmented agents rely on a static retrieve-then-reason paradigm, this rigid pipeline design prevents them from dynamically adapting memory access to intermediate evidence discovered during inference. To bridge this gap, we propose MRAgent, a framework that combines an associative memory graph with an active reconstruction mechanism. We represent memory as a Cue-Tag-Content graph, where associative tags serve as semantic bridges connecting fine-grained cues to memory contents. Operating on this structure, our active reconstruction mechanism integrates LLM reasoning directly into memory access, allowing the agent to iteratively explore and prune retrieval paths based on accumulated evidence. This ensures that memory retrieval is dynamically adapted to the reasoning context while avoiding combinatorial explosion caused by unconstrained expansion. Experiments on the LoCoMo benchmark and LongMemEval benchmark demonstrate significant improvements over strong baselines (up to 23%), while substantially reducing token and runtime cost, highlighting the effectiveness of active and associative reconstruction for long-horizon memory reasoning.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了“Agents' Last Exam (ALE)”基准测试，该基准与 250 多位行业专家合作开发，基于 O*NET / SOC 2018 美国职业分类体系，涵盖 13 个行业集群、55 个子领域及超过 1000 项具有可验证结果的长周期、实际工作流程任务。

Result: 实验结果显示，在当前的 AI 主流配置下，ALE 基准测试中最难的一级任务平均通过率仅为 2.6%，表明现有 AI 模型在处理实际复杂经济任务方面仍有巨大改进空间。

Conclusion: ALE 通过提供真实、高价值的任务评估，填补了现有 AI 基准测试与实际经济生产力之间的鸿沟，为 AI 系统在专业领域实现真正的经济价值提供了衡量标准。

Abstract: Recent AI systems have achieved strong results on a wide range of benchmarks, yet these gains have not translated into economically meaningful deployment across many professional domains. We argue that this gap is largely an evaluation problem: widely used benchmarks lack sustained performance measurement on real and economically valuable workflows. This paper introduces Agents' Last Exam (ALE), a benchmark designed to evaluate AI agents on long-horizon, economically valuable, real-world tasks with verifiable outcomes. Developed in collaboration with 250+ industry experts, ALE covers non-physical industries defined with reference to O*NET / SOC 2018 (the U.S. federal occupational taxonomy). It is organized around a task taxonomy with 55 subfields grouped into 13 industry clusters covering 1K+ tasks. Current results show that the hardest tier remains far from saturated: across mainstream harness and backbone configurations, the average full pass rate is 2.6%. ALE is designed as a living benchmark: its task pool grows continuously as new workflows and industries are onboarded. More broadly, ALE is intended not merely as another leaderboard, but as an instrument for closing the gap between benchmark success and GDP-relevant impact.
