### [274] [Revisiting Prototype Rehearsal for Exemplar-Free Continual Learning: Manifold-Aware Boundary Sampling with Adaptive Class-Balanced Loss](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05695)
*Hongye Xu,Bartosz Krawczyk*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对无样本类增量学习（EFCIL），通过引入“流形感知”和“自适应类平衡”策略改进了传统的原型重演方法，不仅解决了样本合成的边界对齐和类别不平衡问题，还在性能上超越了主流的漂移补偿方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的无样本类增量学习（EFCIL）中，原型重演方法在性能上逐渐落后于漂移补偿方法。作者认为其根源不在于重演思想本身，而在于现有方法忽视了旧类原型与其邻近敌对类之间的关系，且无法有效解决合成样本与新数据之间的类别不平衡问题。因此，作者旨在通过改进原型重演机制来重新审视并提升其在该领域的竞争力。

Method: 该论文提出了一种流形感知的原型重演框架，包含两个核心模块：1. 约束扩张过采样（Constrained Expansive Over-Sampling）：通过将旧类原型向新类的邻近“敌对”特征进行插值，生成能够保持类间分离并符合数据流形的边界感知样本；2. 自适应类平衡损失（Adaptive Class-Balanced loss）：根据时间动态调整类别权重，在训练初期增强旧类原型的梯度影响力，并随新任务任务积累逐步衰减，从而有效缓解类不平衡问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在多个EFCIL基准测试上均达到了最先进（State-of-the-Art）的性能表现，成功弥补并反超了现有的漂移补偿方法，验证了其所提策略在处理特征漂移和类不平衡方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了原型重演在无样本类增量学习（EFCIL）中依然具有巨大的潜力。通过引入流形感知策略和自适应类平衡机制，原型重演方法不仅能够弥补与漂移补偿方法之间的性能差距，甚至在多个基准测试中实现了超越，证明了通过优化重演机制而非仅仅依赖漂移补偿是解决灾难性遗忘的有效途径。

Abstract: Exemplar-free class-incremental learning (EFCIL) aims to acquire new classes over time without storing raw data. Historically, prototype rehearsal, which samples around stored class prototypes and mixes them with current-task data, has been a popular strategy to reduce catastrophic forgetting. However, recent drift-compensation methods that explicitly realign prototypes in the evolving feature space consistently outperform prototype-based rehearsal, raising the question of whether rehearsal itself is fundamentally limited. We argue that the performance gap stems not from the idea of prototype rehearsal per se, but from how it is typically instantiated: existing approaches treat prototypes as isolated class summaries that ignore information from nearby enemy classes, and fail to correct the emerging class imbalance between a handful of synthetic old-class samples and hundreds of real instances from newly introduced classes. Building on this hypothesis, we revisit prototype rehearsal and propose a manifold-aware variant that restores its competitiveness in EFCIL. First, we introduce Constrained Expansive Over-Sampling, which interpolates each old-class prototype toward its nearest enemy features from new classes, generating boundary-aware rehearsal samples that better follow the underlying data manifold while preserving inter-class separation. Second, we design an Adaptive Class-Balanced loss that performs time-based class weighting, amplifying gradients from older prototypes when they are most informative and gradually annealing their influence as richer supervision from later tasks accumulates. Together, these components turn prototype rehearsal into a drift-resilient, imbalance-aware mechanism that closes, and often reverses, the gap to recent drift-compensation methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance across multiple EFCIL benchmarks.

</details>

Abstract: In-season crop type mapping is critical for food security in the face of increasingly extreme climate-related threats to crops. Currently, the USDA Cropland Data Layer provides crop type labels at 30m resolution and is available the February after harvest, but no product exists that maps crop types before harvest with satisfactory accuracy that would allow emergency managers to respond to crop threats in near real time. Furthermore, the relative advantages of a wide range of algorithms have not been evaluated in a way that accounts for interannual variability, until this study. Here, Harmonized Landsat-Sentinel surface reflectance imagery time series and crop rotation history information are combined to map corn in Iowa and almonds in California at 30m resolution accurately by early June in unseen years, with robust quantification of uncertainty due to phenology and crop distribution. Thousands of model configurations across ten machine learning algorithms were compared using a year-wise cross-validation and a suite of metrics. Hyperparameter search revealed Support Vector Machines to be the most successful algorithm overall, with a mean F1 score of 0.74 (0.59) across five unseen validation years for almonds by early June in California (corn by early June in Iowa). Interannual variation was a large source of uncertainty, but patterns showed the potential to further improve performance with ensemble approaches or ancillary data. Future work may extend these methods to include multiclass maps of all crop types, CONUS-wide maps, and in-season crop yield forecasting.

### [277] [Beyond Soft Masks: Hard-Perturbation Mixup Explainer for Robust GNN Explainability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05756)
*Jialiang Yin,Zheng Zhao,Linsey Pang,Bo Dong,Bin Shi,Jiaxing Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的GNN事后解释方法多采用软掩码，无法完全消除标签无关信息的干扰，导致冗余结构泄露至混合过程，进而引发OOD（分布外）问题，损害了解释的保真度，限制了GNN在高风险领域的应用。

Method: 提出了一种基于广义图信息瓶颈（GIB）的硬扰动混合解释（HPME）框架。该方法利用图池化技术提取离散的解释性子图，并通过信息容量约束来彻底压缩标签无关信息；同时引入了一种基于结构级替换的新型混合策略，通过生成分布内（In-distribution）的解释样本，有效缓解了分布偏移（Distribution Shift）问题。

Result: 在多个合成数据集和真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，HPME在生成鲁棒且可解释的解释方面达到了当前最先进（SOTA）的性能水平。

Abstract: Graph Neural Networks (GNNs) have demonstrated remarkable performance across a range of applications involving graph-structured data, particularly in high-stakes domains. However, the opaque nature of their decision-making processes limits their trustworthiness and broader adoption. Existing post-hoc explanation methods aim to improve explainability by identifying subgraphs that influence GNN predictions and adopt mixup strategies to alleviate the out-of-distribution (OOD) issue caused by using subgraphs for prediction. Yet, these approaches typically rely on soft masks, which are inherently unable to fully eliminate label-irrelevant information, allowing redundant structures to leak into the mixup process and hindering the resolution of the OOD problem, thereby degrading explanation fidelity. In this work, we propose HPME, a Hard-Perturbation Mixup Explanation framework grounded in a generalized Graph Information Bottleneck, which leverages graph pooling to extract discrete explanatory subgraphs and to yield an information-capacity bound to thoroughly compress label-irrelevant components. Furthermore, we introduce a novel mixup strategy built upon structure-level replacement, generating in-distribution explanations to effectively mitigate the distribution shift. Extensive experiments on diverse tasks demonstrate that HPME achieves state-of-the-art performance in generating robust and interpretable explanations across both synthetic and real-world datasets.

### [278] [Domain-Adapted Small Language Models with Hybrid Post-Processing: Achieving Cost-Efficient, Low-Latency Multi-Label Structured Prediction via LoRA Fine-Tuning on Scarce Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05781)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿大型语言模型（LLMs）在处理特定领域结构化评估任务时存在高延迟、高成本及数据隐私泄露的风险。

Method: 提出了一种神经-符号混合框架，利用LoRA对LLaMA 3.1 8B模型进行高效微调（仅训练2.05%参数），并结合确定性规则后处理层，通过针对性的难负样本增强技术提升关键决策边界的性能。

Abstract: Deploying frontier large language models (LLMs) for domain-specific structured evaluation tasks often incurs substantial latency, cost, and data privacy overhead. We present a hybrid framework that combines a fine-tuned small language model (LLaMA 3.1 8B, with only 2.05% trainable parameters via LoRA) and a deterministic rule-based post-processing layer. Running on a single NVIDIA A100 GPU, inference completes in approximately 2 seconds, which is 2-5x faster than frontier-model APIs. The system costs only $0.013 per evaluation compared with $0.025-$0.055 for proprietary alternatives, resulting in 46-76% cost savings. These results demonstrate that domain-adapted small language models, when combined with deterministic post-processing, can match frontier-model accuracy for structured compliance evaluation while substantially reducing operational cost, latency, and privacy risk.
  Keywords: small language models, parameter-efficient fine-tuning, LoRA, domain adaptation, hybrid inference, compliance evaluation, structured output.

### [279] [Causal Longitudinal Prior-Fitted Networks for Counterfactual Outcome Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05797)

Abstract: Longitudinal treatment decisions require predicting potential outcomes under future treatment sequences in the presence of time-varying confounding, heterogeneous patient dynamics, and limited domain-specific data. Existing longitudinal causal estimators typically train a new model for each cohort or simulator. We introduce Causal Longitudinal Prior-Fitted Networks (CausalLongPFN), a prior-fitted in-context predictor for longitudinal causal prediction. CausalLongPFN is competitive with domain-trained longitudinal baselines on counterfactual benchmarks and performs strongly on factual MIMIC-III prediction, suggesting that broad synthetic causal pretraining can provide a useful frozen alternative when repeated domain-specific training is costly or impractical.

### [280] [CaliDist: Calibrating Large Language Models via Behavioral Robustness to Distraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05799)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的校准方法多关注预测概率与真实准确率的一致性，却忽视了模型在面对无关或误导性信息时表现出的“行为鲁棒性”。作者认为，模型在“认知压力”下的稳定性应被视为评估其真实可信度及置信度的重要依据。

Method: 提出了一种名为 CaliDist 的事后校准方法。该方法通过在输入提示中添加语义干扰项，量化大语言模型在面对干扰时的预测和不确定性变化，并将这种稳定性信号作为权重，对模型原始的置信度得分进行自适应缩放。

Result: 在七个自然语言理解基准测试和六种不同大模型上的实验表明，CaliDist 在预期校准误差 (ECE) 和 Brier 分数方面均优于现有强基准。平均而言，ECE 从 23% 降低至 7%，实现了约 70% 的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: 研究证明，模型的“行为稳定性”是衡量其可信度与校准准确性的关键信号。将对干扰信息的鲁棒性纳入校准过程，能够显著提升大语言模型的置信度估计质量，使其在面对无关信息时表现出更优的校准性能。

Abstract: Existing calibration methods for Large Language Models (LLMs) often overlook a critical dimension of trustworthiness: a model's {\em behavioral robustness} to irrelevant or misleading information. In this paper, we argue that a model's true confidence should reflect its stability under cognitive pressure. We introduce \textsc{CaliDist}, a novel post-hoc calibration approach that directly measures and penalizes a model's susceptibility to distraction. \textsc{CaliDist} quantifies how an LLM's predictions and uncertainty change when its input prompt is perturbed with semantic \textit{distractors}. This stability (or lack thereof) signal is then used to adaptively scale the model's initial confidence score. Our extensive experiments on seven Natural Language Understanding classification benchmarks using six distinct LLMs show that \textsc{CaliDist} consistently achieves lower Expected Calibration Error (ECE) and Brier Score compared with strong baselines. Remarkably, our method reduces the ECE from 23\% to 7\% on average--a relative improvement of 70\%--demonstrating that behavioral stability is a powerful signal for calibration. We make our code and datasets available at github.com/m-anas-j/CaliDist.

### [281] [SALT: When More Rollouts Don't Help in Group-Based Policy Optimization and How to Make Them Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05800)
*Powei Chang,Jinpeng Zhang,Chaoqun Sun,MiniWell Tsao,Lianrui Li,Jianxiang Xiang,Chenyu Wang,Yukang Gao,Dongying Kong*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对 GRPO 在强化学习中因梯度符号抵消导致的更新失效问题，提出了一种名为 SALT 的几何插件。通过自适应重加权梯度通道，SALT 有效增强了模型训练的更新效率，在不增加计算开销的情况下提升了模型推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于 GRPO（群相对策略优化）的强化学习方法在增加采样数量时，往往会出现由于策略梯度特征集中在低秩有符号几何结构中，导致在聚合时发生严重的符号抵消（Cancellation），从而削弱了模型学习效果的问题。作者旨在解决这一失效模式，提升更新的有效性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SALT（Subspace-Adaptive geometry pLug-in componenT）的插件组件。该方法首先通过采样梯度的 Gram 矩阵估计出一个主导共享子空间，将群相对更新系数分解为共享通道和残差通道，并在检测到严重的符号抵消时，自适应地放大残差通道的权重，从而优化更新的几何特性。

Result: 实验结果表明，在多种以推理为导向的强化学习基准测试及不同模型规模下，SALT 能够改善更新的几何结构，并在不修改奖励模型或采样过程的前提下，实现了性能的显著提升。

Conclusion: SALT 通过有效缓解群相对策略梯度在聚合时的符号抵消问题，显著增强了强化学习在可验证奖励任务中的更新效率。该方法证明了在不增加采样成本的情况下，通过利用梯度几何结构进行自适应重加权，可以显著提升模型的推理能力，为大规模语言模型的强化学习训练提供了一种高效的优化策略。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) often adopts GRPO-style group-relative updates, sampling multiple rollouts per prompt to construct normalized learning signals. However, merely increasing the number of rollouts does not reliably strengthen learning: under GRPO-style group normalization, per-rollout policy-gradient features can concentrate into a low-rank, signed geometry, causing substantial cancellation during aggregation and weakening the effective update. We address this failure mode with SALT, a Subspace-Adaptive geometry pLug-in componenT that uses sample-wise gradient geometry to reweight the coefficients of group-relative updates. SALT estimates a dominant shared subspace from the mini-batch Gram geometry, decomposes group-relative coefficients into shared and residual channels, and adaptively amplifies the residual channel when signed cancellation is severe. Across diverse reasoning-oriented RLVR benchmarks and model scales, SALT improves effective update geometry and performance without modifying the reward model or the rollout sampling procedure

### [282] [Robust and sparse support vector machine via hybrid truncated loss for supervised classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05814)
*Yuliang Yang,Chen Chen,Yuxiang Liu,Huiru Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对SVM中损失函数选择的难题，本文提出了一种混合截断损失函数（Lht），通过优化算法设计和多视图扩展，实现了对异常值的高鲁棒性、高计算效率及优异的分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出一种兼具稀疏性和有界性的混合截断损失函数（Lht）；2. 建立Lht-SVM模型，并引入P-平稳点理论导出最优性条件；3. 设计结合工作集策略（working-set strategy）的交替方向乘子法（ADMM）以降低计算复杂度；4. 将模型扩展至多视图场景（MvLht-SVM），整合结构信息与视图权重以满足一致性和互补性原则。

Abstract: The support vector machine (SVM) is a widely used classifier, but choosing an appropriate loss function remains difficult. Convex losses such as the hinge loss and least-squares loss are sensitive to outliers, while bounded non-convex losses often lead to high computational cost. To address this, we propose a hybrid truncated loss function ($L_{\mathrm{ht}}$) that is both sparse and bounded, and build the $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM model for single-view classification. We introduce the P-stationary point and use it to establish the first-order necessary and sufficient optimality conditions. Based on these conditions, we design an alternating direction method of multipliers with a working-set strategy that reduces computational cost and achieves global convergence. We further extend $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM to multi-view learning by adding structural information and view weights, resulting in Mv$L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM, which follows both the consensus and complementarity principles. Experiments on synthetic, real-world, and image datasets show that $L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM achieves higher accuracy with fewer support vectors and better noise robustness than five single-view methods, while Mv$L_{\mathrm{ht}}$-SVM outperforms six multi-view methods in accuracy, precision, recall, and F1-score.

Conclusion: 一致性训练是一种灵活且可扩展的对齐框架，能够统一应对多种模型病态行为。研究揭示了不同一致性目标（ACT, MLPCT, AttCT）共享的残差流机制，并指出其在多种安全威胁下的有效性及跨威胁泛化能力。

Abstract: Consistency training encourages models to behave similarly across different contexts, and has shown promise for reducing misalignment. Second, we apply consistency training to four additional safety threats: persona in-context learning attacks, adversarial frustration, prefill attacks, and conditional misalignment. Across several models and threat settings, we find that consistency training reduces misalignment well beyond the sycophancy and jailbreak settings studied in prior work. We also find cases of cross-threat generalization, where training against one failure mode improves robustness to another, and identify a shared residual-stream mechanism underlying ACT, MLPCT, and AttCT, while distinguishing BCT as mechanistically distinct. Our results suggest that consistency training is a flexible and extensible framework for alignment, capable of unifying defenses against a broader class of model pathologies.

Abstract: Designing neural architectures for time-series forecasting and anomaly detection remains a resource-intensive task that often requires substantial domain expertise. We present GenAutoML, an agentic framework that leverages Large Language Models (LLMs) as neural architects to bridge natural-language requirements and executable PyTorch implementations. The framework incorporates a Sandboxed Reflection Loop for autonomous code refinement and a Signature-Aware Runtime that enforces architectural consistency and execution safety. To improve robustness under non-stationary conditions, we further introduce a Dynamic Reversible Instance Normalization (Dyn-RevIN) wrapper. Experiments on the ETTh1, ETTm1, and Weather benchmarks demonstrate that GenAutoML can dynamically generate task-specific neural architectures tailored to dataset characteristics. Among the generated models, WaveInterferenceNet achieves inference latency below 0.01 ms per sample while maintaining competitive predictive performance. By emphasizing computational efficiency, architectural adaptability, and stable optimization behavior, GenAutoML enables the creation of ultra-lightweight neural networks suitable for resource-constrained and latency-sensitive Edge AI deployments.

### [285] [Deciphering Two Training Clocks in Grokking via Deep Linear Network Theory with Conditional ReLU Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05863)
*Hu Tan,Kuo Gai,Shihua Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过“双时钟”理论解释了Grokking现象，揭示了神经网络在训练过程中通过不同的时间尺度分别完成数据的快速拟合与模型表征的缓慢简化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解释“Grokking”（即模型在训练误差降为零后，测试准确率仍随时间延迟而大幅提升）的现象，探讨为何模型拟合训练数据与学习简单底层规则存在显著的时间尺度差异。

Method: 通过数学形式化定义两个训练时钟（分类损失衰减与表征简化），利用深度线性网络进行理论推导，证明了交叉熵损失在对数尺度上的快速衰减，以及在权重衰减作用下结构性能量在多项式尺度上的收敛。此外，通过链式法则估计分析了ReLU MLP在固定激活模式下的两阶段梯度动力学。

Result: 证明了深层线性网络中存在“双时钟”机制，即分类损失的快速收敛与受Schatten类惩罚影响的结构化能量的缓慢收敛分离；在ReLU MLP中，通过分析固定激活模式区域，证明了分类器头可以比嵌入块获得更大的有效梯度，从而支持了“先拟合、后表征简化”的训练阶段划分。

Conclusion: 该研究通过“双时钟”理论揭示了Grokking现象的本质：神经网络的训练分为两个阶段，即快速的拟合阶段（损失函数下降）和缓慢的表征简化阶段（结构正则化），并解释了这一机制在深层线性网络和ReLU MLP中的体现。

Abstract: Grokking suggests that fitting the training data and learning a simple underlying rule may occur on different time scales. We formalize this phenomenon by separating the fast decay of the classification loss from the slower simplification of the learned representation, and we call the resulting pair of stopping times two training clocks. For deep linear networks, we show that a post-margin gap-growth or one-step tail-contraction condition reduces the cross-entropy loss to level epsilon on a logarithmic time scale. In contrast, when layerwise weight decay is present, the induced regularization on the end-to-end map can be expressed as a Schatten-type penalty; under a sharp late-time Kurdyka-Lojasiewicz tail, this structural energy closes on a polynomial time scale. The two clocks, therefore, separate fitting from representation simplification. We then explain how the same mechanism can appear in ReLU MLPs. In regions where the activation patterns on the training set remain fixed, the network reduces to a linear model in the active coordinates. In a two-layer ReLU embedding model, chain-rule estimates further show that the classifier head can receive larger effective gradients than the embedding block under controlled downstream norms. This supports a two-stage mechanism in which the classifier fits first, while the representation continues to simplify later. We use modular addition as the main experimental setting. The deep linear theory provides the rigorous core of the analysis. But the ReLU results are formulated as conditional reductions that account for empirical behavior without claiming a global proof for nonlinear training dynamics.

</details>


### [286] [TS-ICL: A Flexible Time-Indexed Foundation Model for Time Series via In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05878)
*Etienne Le Naour,Tahar Nabil,Adrien Petralia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TS-ICL 是一种新型 Transformer 架构，通过上下文学习统一了时间序列的预测与缺失值填补任务，能够有效处理现实中复杂、不规则且部分缺失的数据，在多个基准测试中刷新了性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前时间序列基础模型大多仅专注于单一的预测任务，而现实中的时间序列数据往往是不规则且部分缺失的。现有方法难以有效处理这些复杂的观测条件，因此需要一种能同时处理预测、缺失值填补并适应退化采样条件的通用基础模型。

Method: 提出了一种名为 TS-ICL 的概率性上下文学习编码器-回归 Transformer。核心方法包括：1. 将时间序列任务统一建模为时间戳对齐的回归问题；2. 引入一种新型因果数据先验来生成合成依赖结构，从而自然地整合协变量；3. 设计了能够联合执行预测与填补任务的架构，使其具备处理不规则和部分观测数据的能力。

Result: TS-ICL 在缺失值填补任务中达到了最新的行业领先水平（SOTA），同时在单变量和考虑协变量的预测基准测试中表现出与主流预测基础模型相当的竞争力，特别是在处理部分观测的“回顾窗口”（look-back windows）时表现极其出色。

Conclusion: TS-ICL 证明了将预测与填补任务统一在单一架构下的可行性与优越性。通过利用上下文学习（ICL）和因果数据先验，该模型为处理现实世界中不规则、部分缺失的时间序列数据提供了一种通用且高效的解决方案，确立了时间序列基础模型的新基准。

Abstract: Foundation models mark a profound paradigm shift in time series modeling, with task-specific models being superseded by general-purpose zero-shot models. Yet, current approaches primarily focus on forecasting, while real-world time series are often irregularly and partially observed, requiring models that can jointly forecast, impute missing values, and handle degraded sampling conditions. To address these challenges, we introduce TS-ICL, a novel probabilistic In-Context Learning encoder--regressor Transformer that unifies forecasting and imputation. TS-ICL formulates time series tasks as timestamp-aligned regression and naturally incorporates covariates by training on synthetic dependency structures generated from a novel causal data prior. Empirically, TS-ICL achieves a new state-of-the-art in imputation, while remaining competitive with leading forecasting foundation models across both univariate and covariate-aware benchmarks. It shows particularly strong performance in forecasting with partially observed look-back windows.

</details>


### [287] [When Denser Credit Is Not Enough: Evidence-Calibrated Policy Optimization for Long-Horizon LLM Agent Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05885)
*Yuanfan Li,Qi Zhou,Wenjing Duan,Lu Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决长程LLM智能体在强化学习中因样本稀疏导致的信用分配偏差和训练震荡问题，本文提出了ECPO算法，通过证据校准和方差门控机制提升了策略优化的鲁棒性，在不增加显著计算代价的前提下大幅提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的长程LLM智能体强化学习方法（如GiGPO）在稀疏和延迟奖励下，试图通过锚定状态分配步级信用，但在采样不足时，稀有但侥幸成功的动作会导致严重的统计偏差和训练不稳定性。

Method: 提出了一种无Critic（critic-free）的策略优化算法ECPO，包含两个核心模块：1. 证据校准动作优势（Evidence-Calibrated Action Advantage），通过对轨迹进行规范化动作分组并对低频样本估计进行收缩（shrinkage）处理；2. 方差门控信用加权（Variance-Gated Credit Weighting），旨在抑制那些受噪声主导的锚定状态，从而缓解“锚定偏差”导致的训练震荡。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebShop任务上使用Qwen2.5-1.5B/7B进行验证，ECPO表现优于现有最优基准方法（如GiGPO），在Qwen2.5-1.5B模型上成功率分别提升了5.2和7.3个百分点，且仅增加了0.1%的计算开销。

Conclusion: ECPO通过引入证据校准机制，成功解决了长程LLM智能体在稀疏奖励环境下的信用分配不稳定性问题，证明了在无需额外Critic模型的情况下，通过统计校准也能有效提升策略优化的鲁棒性和性能。

Abstract: Long-horizon LLM agents require reinforcement learning methods that can assign credit to intermediate decisions under sparse and delayed rewards. Recent group-based methods such as GiGPO improve over GRPO by constructing step-level advantages at repeated anchor states. However, we show that such dense credit can be statistically unreliable: under limited rollouts, rare but lucky actions may receive overly large advantages, producing divergent anchor bias and late-stage training oscillation. We propose Evidence-Calibrated Policy Optimization (ECPO), a critic-free policy optimization algorithm that calibrates step-level credit before policy updates. ECPO combines Evidence-Calibrated Action Advantage, which groups rollouts by canonical actions and shrinks low-count estimates, with Variance-Gated Credit Weighting, which suppresses anchor states dominated by within-action noise. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebShop with Qwen2.5-1.5B/7B show that ECPO consistently outperforms strong baselines, improving GiGPO by +5.2/+7.3 success points on ALFWorld/WebShop with Qwen2.5-1.5B while adding only 0.1% additional advantage-computation overhead.

### [288] [High-Dimensional Theory of LoRA Fine-Tuning in a Solvable Attention Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05899)
*O. Duranthon,F. Boncoraglio,L. Zdeborová*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文利用高维统计理论分析了LoRA技术，建立了预训练与微调的数学模型，阐明了预训练对LoRA的影响，并为微调优化提供了理论指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了从高维统计学角度理解大型注意力模型中低秩适应（LoRA）技术的底层工作机制，特别是探究预训练阶段与微调阶段之间的相互作用。

Method: 建立了一个可解的单头注意力层模型，模拟大规模预训练任务与有限数据下的秩一（rank-one）LoRA微调过程。在高维极限下，使用序参量（order parameters）对这两个阶段进行精确的渐近表征，并导出测试误差和表示对齐的显式预测。

Result: 研究得出了测试误差和表示对齐的显式数学预测；揭示了预训练对LoRA的影响表现为一种有效的噪声项；发现测试误差与表示质量之间可能存在失配现象；并提出了一种基于该理论的主动微调应用方案。

Conclusion: 本文通过高维统计理论揭示了LoRA在预训练与微调过程中的内在机制，证明了预训练的影响可由有效的噪声项刻画，并为优化微调过程（如主动微调）提供了理论依据和指导。

Abstract: We develop a high-dimensional statistical theory of low-rank adaptation (LoRA) in attention models, capturing the interplay between pre-training and fine-tuning. We introduce a solvable framework in which a single-head attention layer is first pre-trained on a data-abundant task and subsequently adapted via a rank-one LoRA update on limited data. In the high-dimensional limit, both stages admit a sharp asymptotic characterization in terms of a finite set of order parameters, yielding explicit predictions for test errors and representation alignment. Our analysis shows that the impact of pre-training on LoRA is summarized by an effective noise term, from which we derive prescriptions for the optimal pre-training procedure. We also demonstrate a regime with a mismatch between the value of the test error and representation quality, and propose an application of our theory to active fine-tuning.

### [289] [Addressing Imbalance in Multi-Label Data via Label-Specific Distance-based Oversampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05927)
*Bin Liu,Jun Wu,Haoyu Peng,Ao Zhou,Jin Wang,QiaoSong Chen,Grigorios Tsoumakas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多标签分类中的不平衡问题，本文提出了一种标签特定距离的过采样方法（LSDMLO），通过利用标签相关的加权特征空间生成高质量的合成样本，有效解决了传统方法因忽略特征与标签语义关联而导致的标签混淆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有针对多标签分类的过采样方法多基于全局欧氏距离进行启发式合成，忽略了不同特征对不同标签的语义相关性差异，导致合成样本产生标签不一致、标签混淆以及过拟合问题。因此，需要一种能够考虑标签特异性并保持标签一致性的采样策略。

Method: 提出了一种名为“标签特定距离多标签过采样（LSDMLO）”的新方法。该方法不再使用全局欧氏距离，而是基于加权的标签相关特征空间，为每个标签计算特定的距离度量。通过这种方式，在边界区域识别出标签一致的邻居作为种子样本，进而生成更具代表性且标签一致的合成样本。

Result: 实验结果表明，LSDMLO方法在多种基分类器下，性能均优于现有的先进多标签采样算法，能够更有效地缓解多标签数据集中的类别不平衡问题。

Conclusion: 本文提出的LSDMLO方法通过引入标签特定距离，有效解决了多标签分类中数据不平衡导致的问题。该方法在保证合成样本与原始数据标签分布一致性的前提下，增强了模型处理边界样本的能力，验证了其在多标签学习任务中的优越性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: The complex imbalanced label distribution poses a crucial challenge to multi-label classification, as most classifiers are biased towards the majority class and high-frequent labels. Oversampling is an efficient and flexible solution that augments instances to provide a more balanced training dataset for multi-label classifiers. Most existing oversampling methods create synthetic instances in a heuristic way that essentially relies on neighborhood information retrieved using Euclidean distance within the entire feature space. However, they fail to consider the varying semantic relevance of features to different labels, leading to label inconsistency among proximate neighbors and further introducing label confusion and overfitting to synthetic instances. To overcome the above issue, we propose a novel sampling approach called Label-Specific Distance-based Multi-Label Oversampling (LSDMLO) that creates more useful and well-labeled synthetic instances to address the imbalance in multi-label datasets. LSDMLO derives the label-specific distance to identify label-consistent neighbors based on the weighted pertinent feature space, which facilitates selecting seed instances that express more label correlations in boundary areas and generating synthetic instances aligned with the label distribution of original data. The comprehensive experiments verify that the proposed LSDMLO outperforms the state-of-the-art multi-label sampling approaches under various base classifiers.

</details>

Result: 研究发现，目前的许多GDPR要求在技术实践中尚无法完全实现。机器学习供应链中的责任归属与技术实现问题在现有研究中被严重忽视。特别是“黑暗中的模型”这一现象，由于缺乏透明度和可追溯性，使得下游模型的合规性维护变得极其困难。

Conclusion: GDPR下的数据权利（更正权与删除权）在复杂的机器学习供应链中面临严峻挑战。本文强调了跨学科研究的重要性，并指出当前技术水平与法律合规之间存在巨大鸿沟，亟需建立透明、可追溯的ML供应链机制以实现真正可信的AI。

Abstract: The rights to rectification and erasure, as established under the General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR), are central to protecting individuals' privacy. However, their effective enforcement in machine learning (ML) systems remains challenging. Existing work has largely addressed these rights from either a legal or a technical perspective in isolation and disregards the fact that models are produced in complex supply chains involving multiple actors across development, distribution, and deployment. This paper presents a holistic survey of challenges in implementing the rights to rectification and erasure in ML models. Drawing on academic literature and guidance from data protection authorities, we find that many GDPR requirements cannot yet be technically met in practice. Our findings further suggest that issues arising in ML supply chains are insufficiently addressed in research. To tackle this gap, we introduce the notion of models in the dark -- derived models created further downstream in an ML chain without sufficient transparency or traceability -- and analyse the urgent challenges posed by this phenomenon. By adopting an interdisciplinary perspective, this work contributes to bridging the gap between legal requirements and the technical implementation of data subject rights in ML, ultimately supporting the development of trustworthy artificial intelligence.

### [291] [Dead Directions: Geometric Singular Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05957)
*Tejas Pradeep Shirodkar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文在奇点学习理论与信息几何之间搭建了桥梁，提出了一种在原始坐标系中利用费舍尔度量退化特征（方向性费舍尔曲率）直接计算奇点几何不变量（如RLCT）的新方法，并将其应用于深度网络分析与优化器设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奇点学习理论与信息几何长期以来研究对象一致但方法脱节：前者依赖于复杂的消解坐标（Resolved coordinates），后者依赖于在过参数化模型中往往失效的非退化假设。研究者旨在通过原始参数坐标建立两者的直接联系，从而解决过参数化模型中的奇点几何分析问题。

Method: 该研究定义了“死亡方向”（dead direction）作为两个理论的桥梁，通过分析费舍尔度量在该方向上的退化行为（即方向性费舍尔曲率的衰减率）来替代传统的希罗纳卡消解。在深度学习应用中，结合了K-FAC分解来刻画层级结构，并利用商空间定理处理对称性，最终构建了一个基于几何性质的G等变优化器（DDCAdam）。

Result: 论文提供了一种无需后验采样的几何特性提取方法，能够通过单一检查点的梯度和激活信息读取出学习理论中的关键参数（RLCT等）。此外，它为现代神经网络架构（如残差连接、注意力机制）提供了封闭形式的架构性能预测，并成功设计出与模型几何对称性一致的优化器。

Conclusion: 该研究成功在奇点学习理论与信息几何之间建立了一座桥梁，证明了可以通过方向性费舍尔曲率在原始坐标系中直接获取渡边（Watanabe）的三元组（λ, m, ν），无需进行复杂的代数几何消解。研究还揭示了深度神经网络中激活值与梯度侧速率的对偶性，并提出了DDCAdam优化器，为在非退化假设失效的复杂模型中进行精确的几何与学习理论分析提供了实用工具。

Abstract: Singular learning theory and information geometry have studied the same parameter spaces in mostly separate vocabularies: the former computes Bayesian invariants in resolved coordinates, the latter works in original coordinates under a non-degeneracy assumption that overparameterised models routinely violate. We bridge them through one primitive, the dead direction: a unit vector along which the Fisher metric degenerates, equivalently a tangent to the analytic singular set with a definite KL order, set by how fast the KL divergence vanishes. The two readings name the same vector; our central move shows its KL order is recoverable as the decay rate of the directional Fisher curvature approaching the singularity, in original parameter coordinates and without a Hironaka resolution. A selection rule on smooth fibres translates this rate into Watanabe's single-direction contribution to the real log canonical threshold, and we extend the recovery to multi-component crossings, multiplicity $m$, the singular fluctuation $ν$ (universal in the KL order for 1D directions), prior-RLCT shifts, and tempered posteriors. We then lift this rate to a deep network: a multi-layer K-FAC factorisation writes each Fisher block as a product of activation- and gradient-side rates with a duality between them, instantiated at modern-network primitives (residual streams, layer normalisation, attention). A quotient theorem carries the rate to the gauge quotient $Θ/G$ under gradient flow on a $G$-invariant metric; SGD qualifies, standard Adam does not, and we construct a $G$-equivariant Adam-family preconditioner (DDCAdam) that does. The bridge yields a parameter-coordinate handle on singular geometry, closed-form per-architecture predictions, and a trajectory-rate readout of Watanabe's triple $(λ, m, ν)$ from one checkpoint's forward and backward passes, without posterior sampling.

</details>


### [292] [Steering Vectors are an Adversarial Attack Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05958)
*Abzal Aidakhmetov,Donato Crisostomi,Tommaso Mencattini,Adrian Robert Minut,Iacopo Masi,Emanuele Rodolà*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究发现，通过在引导数据集中注入少量投毒数据，攻击者可以操控大模型的激活向量，在保持正常功能的同时实现隐蔽越狱。作者同时提出了一种有效的正交化防御机制来抵御此类攻击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着激活引导技术在无需微调即可控制 LLM 行为方面的广泛应用，用户间共享引导数据集和向量变得普及。作者旨在评估这种共享生态在面对恶意篡改时的安全性。

Method: 研究者提出了一种隐蔽数据投毒攻击，通过替换引导数据集中 4-6% 的 token，将生成的激活向量对齐到反拒绝方向（anti-refusal direction）。同时，本文测试了拒绝方向正交化（refusal-direction orthogonalization）作为防御手段的效果。

Result: 在多个开源模型系列和属性组合上的实验表明，投毒向量的攻击成功率（ASR）提升了 19% 至 51%，最高达到 55%。提出的防御方案能恢复约 82% 的 ASR 差距，且不损害模型的良性行为。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了激活引导（activation steering）技术在模型安全方面的漏洞。攻击者可通过毒化引导数据集，在不影响模型正常功能的前提下，实现隐蔽的越狱攻击。通过拒绝方向正交化防御机制，可以有效减轻这一风险。

Abstract: Activation steering has become a popular way to control Large Language Model (LLM) behavior without fine-tuning. Since the technique is plug-and-play, users share datasets and precomputed vectors to steer model activations. However, we show that a \emph{stealth data poisoning attack} silently compromises this pipeline. By substituting $4{-}6\%$ of tokens in the steering dataset, an attacker can silently align the resulting vector with an anti-refusal direction. This jailbreaks the target model while preserving the intended steering effect on benign prompts. Under this threat model, a malicious actor can distribute an apparently safe bundle containing texts, vectors, and weights, alongside an equivalence certificate that the end-user can verify. We test the attack on two open-weight model families and eight model-attribute combinations, observing that poisoned vectors reach an absolute attack success rate (ASR) of $20{-}55\%$, $+19\%$ to $+51\%$ over a clean reference. Finally, we find that a refusal-direction orthogonalization defense can recover ${\approx}82\%$ of the ASR gap without harming benign behavior.

### [293] [LLM Explainability with Counterfactual Chains and Causal Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05972)
*Nirit Nussbaum-Hoffer,Nitay Calderon,Liat Ein-Dor,Roi Reichart*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用因果图揭示大语言模型内部推理机制的方法，通过概念映射与MCMC启发的反事实数据增强，实现了模型高阶推理过程的可视化与解释，为理解“黑盒”大模型提供了一种透明化的新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管利用大语言模型（LLM）恢复外部世界的因果关系已有研究，但大模型本身的推理机制依然是“黑盒”。本文旨在将因果图技术反向应用于大模型自身，使其感知和组织高阶概念以产生预测的过程透明化，从而提高模型的可解释性。

Method: 提出了一种四阶段方法：首先识别类判别性且人类可理解的概念；其次将输入映射到大模型感知到的概念状态；接着引入基于MCMC启发的反事实增强程序，通过反事实链扩展稀疏观测数据；最后利用σ-CG算法进行稳定的因果发现，构建出可解释的因果图。

Result: 在疾病诊断、情感分析及“LLM作为评判者”等任务中，该方法构建的因果图在预测保真度和结构稳定性上表现良好；同时，基于MCMC的反事实增强技术有效提升了数据的收敛性，所生成的因果图能够准确捕捉大模型推理中的关键依赖关系。

Conclusion: 本研究通过因果图成功实现了对大语言模型推理过程的透明化建模，证明了将模型内部概念组织方式可视化不仅是可行的，而且对于理解大模型推理逻辑具有重要的科学意义和应用价值，为大模型的概念级可解释性奠定了基础。

Abstract: Causal graphs provide a high-level language for making mechanisms transparent. Recent work uses Large Language Models (LLMs) to recover causal graphs of external-world processes. Instead, in this paper, we use causal graphs to model LLM inference itself, providing stakeholders with a transparent view of how the model perceives and organizes high-level concepts to produce a prediction. We propose a four-phase method for constructing such graphs. Given a target LLM and a set of textual examples, our method discovers class-discriminative, human-interpretable concepts and maps each input to LLM-perceived concept states. We then introduce an MCMC-inspired counterfactual augmentation procedure that expands the sparse observational data through chains of counterfactuals. This enables stable causal discovery with $σ$-CG, yielding informative, interpretable graphs. We apply our method to three LLMs across disease diagnosis, sentiment analysis, and LLM-as-a-judge classification tasks. We evaluate the learned graphs for predictive fidelity and structural stability, and the MCMC-inspired augmentation for convergence and downstream utility. Our results show that the discovered causal graphs capture meaningful dependencies consistent with LLMs' reasoning. Together, this paper provides a foundation for concept-level explainability of LLMs.

</details>


### [294] [Compress-Distill: Reasoning Trace Compression for Efficient Knowledge Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05988)
*Maxime Griot,Paul Steven Scotti,Tanishq Mathew Abraham*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了对大型推理模型的长思维链进行压缩以用于知识蒸馏的方法。结果显示，虽然压缩轨迹显著提高了训练和推理效率（训练速度提升至多7.6倍，输出缩短至多19倍），但代价是下游任务准确率会有一定程度的下降，这是一种典型的精度与效率权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理模型生成的长思维链（Chain-of-Thought）在知识蒸馏过程中成本高昂，且会导致学生模型输出过于冗长。研究旨在探索通过事后压缩这些推理轨迹，是否能在保持模型推理能力的同时，提升训练与推理的效率。

Method: 研究通过两个强大的教师模型（Qwen3.5-397B-A17B 和 gpt-oss-120B）生成大规模正确推理轨迹，并使用指令微调模型对这些轨迹进行事后压缩（将其缩减至原始字符长度的8.6%至21.0%）。研究通过对比压缩轨迹训练与原始轨迹训练、以及长度匹配的直接截断法，系统评估了训练效率、推理速度及下游任务准确率。

Result: 实验表明，压缩轨迹可将训练Token减少至原始的12%-30%，训练速度提升2.0-7.6倍，推理输出缩短3-19倍。虽然模型压缩轨迹通常优于朴素截断法，但在所有规模下，原始长轨迹在下游准确率上仍表现最优。对于0.8B规模模型，压缩轨迹缩小了与原始轨迹的性能差距，但并未超越。

Conclusion: 推理路径压缩在精度与效率之间提供了一种权衡，而非完全的性能提升。学生模型保留了原始轨迹高达96%的准确率，同时获得了高达18倍的每Token效率提升。尽管压缩轨迹在小规模模型中优于直接截断，但在所有实验规模下，原始长链式思考（Chain-of-Thought）轨迹仍保持着最高的下游准确率。

Abstract: Reasoning models produce long chain-of-thought traces that are costly to distill and encourage verbose student outputs. We study post-hoc compression of such traces before knowledge distillation. Two teachers, Qwen3.5-397B-A17B and gpt-oss-120B, generate about 283k correct traces each; two instruction-tuned models then compress them to 8.6-21.0% of their original character length. Across a 48-run main grid plus seven Qwen-teacher truncation ablations, compressed traces reduce training tokens to 12-30% of raw, speed up training by 2.0-7.6x, and shorten inference outputs by 3-19x with smaller reductions under the shorter gpt-oss teacher. However, raw traces retain the highest downstream accuracy at every scale and for both teachers. A length-matched raw-trace truncation ablation shows that compression is not merely benefiting from a smaller token budget: model-compressed traces usually beat or match naive truncation, especially for smaller students, while maintaining shorter inference outputs. Overall, reasoning-trace compression offers an accuracy-efficiency trade-off rather than a free improvement: students retain up to 96% of raw-trace accuracy while gaining up to 18x higher per-token efficiency, and at the 0.8B scale under LoRA compressed traces narrow the raw-vs-compressed gap but do not exceed raw.

</details>

To mitigate these limitations, we propose HoT-SSM, a parameter efficient and higher-order temporal graph reasoning with state space models. For each visit, HoT-SSM constructs hypergraphs by grouping semantically related clinical concepts into hyperedges using domain knowledge, thereby preserving visit-level clinical context. Further, to model the temporal dynamics while learning the representations, we introduce a novel dynamic hypergraph-based state space model that explicitly captures patients latent state evolution over time while preserving long-range information. The learned representations are used for downstream clinical prediction and reasoning. Experiments on MIMIC-III and MIMIC-IV datasets shows significant performance improvement over the current state-of-the-art models, demonstrating the effectiveness of jointly modeling higher-order clinical interactions and long-range temporal dependencies.

While diffusion models have achieved remarkable success in generating static data, their direct extensions to sequential settings often fail to capture temporal dependence and information structure. Designing diffusion models that can simulate sequential data in an adapted manner, and hence without anticipation of future information, therefore remains an open challenge.
  In this work, we propose a sequential forward-backward diffusion framework for adapted time series generation. Our approach progressively injects and removes noise along the sequence, conditioning on the previously generated history to ensure adaptiveness. A novel score-matching objective is introduced for efficient parallel training. We derive rigorous statistical guarantees under a generic framework, then establish score approximation, score estimation, and distribution estimation results with ReLU networks serving as a concrete instance. ### [297] [Adaptive Oscillatory-State Alignment for Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06010)
*Zhangyao Song,Ziqiong Li,Xiangfei Qiu,Chao Zha,Yinfei Xu,Tao Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的周期性预测方法通常依赖于预定义的周期、全局频谱分量或固定的可学习模板，但在处理现实世界中振荡行为随时间演变的非平稳动态（如振幅、相位和频率的漂移）时，这些固定模板往往会与潜在的时间状态失配，导致预测精度下降。

Method: 提出了一种名为AOSNET的希尔伯特引导预测框架。该方法不再依赖固定的周期模板，而是提取观测序列与可学习全局振荡先验的解析信号描述符；通过一个由描述符条件控制的门控机制，实现局部状态的自适应对齐，在保留可靠信息的同时对失配区域进行软校正。

Conclusion: AOSNET通过将周期性预测从“固定模板匹配”重塑为“自适应振荡状态对齐”，有效解决了现实世界中时间序列非平稳性（如振幅调制、相位漂移和频率变化）带来的挑战，提供了一种更灵活、鲁棒且高效的长期预测方案。

Abstract: Long-term time series forecasting benefits from inductive biases that expose recurring temporal structure. Existing periodic forecasting methods typically model recurrence through predefined periods, global spectral components, or fixed learnable templates. However, real-world temporal dynamics are rarely rigidly periodic: oscillatory behavior often evolves through amplitude modulation, phase drift, and local frequency variation. Under these conditions, fixed-template periodic modeling can become fundamentally mismatched to the underlying temporal states. We propose AOSNET, a Hilbert-guided forecasting framework that reformulates periodic forecasting from fixed template matching to adaptive oscillatory-state alignment. AOSNET extracts analytic-signal descriptors from both the observed sequence and a learnable global oscillatory prior, then adaptively aligns local states through a descriptor-conditioned gate that selectively preserves reliable observations while softly correcting mismatched regions. The learned prior serves not as a rigid repeated template but as a flexible oscillatory reference interpreted through local state dynamics. Experiments on eight benchmarks demonstrate state-of-the-art or highly competitive accuracy with fast inference speed. Controlled synthetic studies isolating amplitude modulation, phase drift, and local frequency variation confirm that the advantage of oscillatory-state alignment consistently increases as non-stationarity intensifies.

### [298] [OPRD: On-Policy Representation Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06021)
*Shenzhi Yang,Guangcheng Zhu,Bowen Song,Haobo Wang,Mingxuan Xia,Xing Zheng,Yingfan Ma,Zhongqi Chen,Weiqiang Wang,Gang Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）方法存在两大局限：一是大词汇量下蒙特卡洛 KL 估计带来的采样方差问题；二是仅关注输出概率而忽略了教师模型的中间隐藏状态，未能充分利用模型潜力。

Method: 提出了“在线策略表示蒸馏”（OPRD）方法，通过在相同的 rollout 上对齐学生模型和教师模型在选定层上的隐藏状态，绕过了语言模型头（LM head），从而实现了更深层次的结构信息传递。

Result: 实验表明，OPRD 在 AIME 2024/2025 和 AIMO 基准测试中成功缩短了学生与教师之间的性能差距，优于传统 OPD 基准。此外，相比顶级 top-k OPD，OPRD 的训练速度快 1.44 倍，内存占用降低 54%。

Conclusion: OPRD 是一种高效且有效的蒸馏范式，通过将知识从输出空间提升到隐藏状态空间，不仅克服了传统输出空间蒸馏的采样方差和信息丢失问题，还在保持高性能的同时显著提升了训练效率。

Abstract: On-policy distillation (OPD) supervises the student only in output space by matching next-token probabilities. This output-only paradigm has two limits: (1) sampling variance from Monte Carlo KL estimates over large vocabularies (e.g., Qwen's ~150k tokens) persists throughout training, and (2) it treats the teacher as a black-box, discarding all intermediate hidden states after the LM head. We propose On-Policy Representation Distillation (OPRD), which lifts distillation into hidden-state space by aligning student and teacher representations across selected layers on the same rollouts, bypassing the LM head entirely. Theoretically, OPRD eliminates sampling variance and provides richer per-layer structural information. Empirically, OPRD closes the student-teacher gap on AIME 2024/2025 and AIMO, while output-space OPD baselines plateau below the teacher. OPRD also trains 1.44x faster and uses 54% less memory than top-k OPD. Code: https://github.com/ShenzhiYang2000/OPRD.

### [299] [Catastrophic Forgetting as Accessibility Collapse: A Three-Level Framework for Knowledge Persistence in Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06032)
*Ayushman Trivedi,Bhavika Melwani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示灾难性遗忘本质上是一种“访问失败”而非“知识擦除”：即便模型功能上遗忘了旧任务，其内部表示层仍存储了大量有效信息，可通过优化访问机制（如重置分类器）高效恢复旧任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对连续学习中灾难性遗忘现象，挑战了“旧知识被彻底擦除”的传统观点，旨在探究遗忘是否源于网络对已存储知识的可访问性失效，而非知识本身的丢失。

Method: 提出了一个包含知识存储、表示和可访问性的三层分析框架，并通过ResNet-18在CIFAR-100连续学习任务上进行实验。分析方法包括检查点持久性测试、线性探测（Linear Probing）、表示几何分析、分类器重置恢复实验以及层级可恢复性分析。

Result: 实验发现：尽管模型在行为上表现出对早期任务的完全遗忘（准确率降至0%），但线性探测仍能提取出原始任务约76%的表示信息；仅通过重置并重新训练输出层分类器，即可恢复约75.7%的任务性能；且早期和中间层保留了高度可恢复的任务信息，证明了知识以分布式高维表示形式留存在网络中。

Conclusion: 灾难性遗忘并非旧知识的彻底物理消除，而是对已保留信息的“可访问性”丧失。神经网络在表现出行为上的遗忘后，仍能在中间层保持高质量的任务相关表示，仅需通过重置分类器即可恢复大部分性能，这为缓解遗忘提供了新的研究视角。

Abstract: Catastrophic forgetting is commonly interpreted as the irreversible erasure of previously acquired knowledge during sequential learning. In this work, we investigate an alternative perspective: that forgetting may arise not from complete destruction of task representations but from a loss of accessibility to preserved information. We introduce a three-level framework separating knowledge storage, representation, and accessibility, and evaluate each component through a series of continual-learning experiments on sequential CIFAR-100 classification using ResNet-18. Our analysis combines checkpoint persistence, linear probing, representation geometry, classifier-reset recovery, and layer-wise recoverability experiments. We observe complete behavioral forgetting of earlier tasks, with task accuracy collapsing from 54.8% to 0%, while linear probe performance retains approximately 76% of the original representational information. Furthermore, retraining only the final classifier restores 75.7% of the original task performance without modifying the backbone network. Layer-wise analysis reveals that early and intermediate layers preserve highly recoverable task information despite severe degradation at later stages. Projection-energy and principal-angle analyses indicate that retained knowledge persists as distributed high-dimensional representations rather than through preservation of a small dominant subspace. These findings suggest that catastrophic forgetting is better characterized as an accessibility failure than complete representational erasure, and that substantial task-relevant information remains embedded within neural representations even after functional forgetting has occurred.

Method: 利用截断纽曼级数（Truncated Neumann Expansion）结合结构化掩码和并行残差修正技术，消除矩阵求逆过程中的顺序依赖；针对低位宽（INT）量化，设计了缓解矩阵幂运算导致动态范围扩大的策略，并根据块大小自适应调整近似阶数和残差步长。

We propose a fast, Matrix Multiplication (MatMul)-based algorithm tailored for strictly lower-triangular matrices arising in chunk-wise linear attention. Motivated by the rapid growth of Neumann-series terms and the diagonal concentration of the inverse matrix, we employ a truncated Neumann expansion with structural masking and parallel residual correction to eliminate sequential dependencies. We further extend our method to low-bits INT by mitigating the dynamic range expansion arising from repeated matrix power operations, and adapt the approximation order and residual step to the chunk size to minimize computational cost while preserving the model's accuracy. Experiments on Qwen3.5-family models demonstrate up to 5$\times$ kernel-level speedup and a 20% reduction in decode-layer overhead, while preserving accuracy under both floating-point and low-precision inference. Our method offers an efficient and hardware-friendly solution for scalable linear attention.

### [301] [Online KL-Regularized Reinforcement Learning with Function Approximation under Misspecification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06053)
*Haoyang Hong,Zichen Wang,Quanquan Gu,Huazheng Wang*

Method: 提出了一种适用于情境赌博机（Contextual Bandits）和分层强化学习（Episodic RL）的KL偏差分析公式，并采用基于回归的算法配合吉布斯（Gibbs）策略更新进行优化。

This work introduces KL misspecification formulations for contextual bandits and episodic RL and analyzes regression-based algorithms with Gibbs policy updates. High-probability KL-regret guarantees with explicit misspecification terms are established, recovering the standard realizable KL-regularized setting as a special case.

### [302] [MDP-GRPO: Stabilized Group Relative Policy Optimization for Multi-Constraint Instruction Following](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06058)
*Mohammad Mahdi Salmani-Zarchi,Zahra Rahimi,Heshaam Faili,Mohammad Javad Dousti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 GRPO 在低方差奖励下的不稳定性，本文提出了 MDP-GRPO 算法，通过多温度采样、双锚点优势计算、前景理论塑形及非对称正则化，显著提升了模型的多约束指令遵循能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多约束指令遵循任务中，标准的组内策略优化（GRPO）算法在处理离散且低方差的奖励时会出现不稳定性，表现为低方差放大、均值归一化盲区和零方差崩溃等问题，导致学习过程难以收敛。

Method: MDP-GRPO 引入了四项改进措施：1. 多温度采样（Multi-temperature sampling）以增加奖励分布的离散度；2. 双锚点优势函数（Dual-anchor advantages）以解决均值归一化带来的盲区并恢复梯度；3. 基于前景理论（Prospect-theoretic）的奖励塑形以限制更新并惩罚违规；4. 非对称 KL 正则化以优化策略更新。

Result: 实验结果表明，MDP-GRPO 在 FollowBench、IFEval 等基准测试中表现优于标准 GRPO，在 Llama-3.2-3B 模型上的严格约束满足度提升了最高 5.0%，同时在小规模组下也能保持稳定收敛，且未损害模型在 MMLU 和 ARC 等基准上的通用能力。

Conclusion: MDP-GRPO 通过解决传统 GRPO 在稀疏、低方差奖励下的稳定性问题，为多约束指令遵循任务提供了一种更鲁棒的强化学习方案，且在保证模型通用能力的同时提升了指令遵循的精确度。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is ideal for multi-constraint instruction following, yet standard group-relative policy optimization (GRPO) becomes unstable under discrete, low-dispersion rewards, where within-group reward distributions are frequently homogeneous. We identify and formalize three pathologies of z-score group normalization in this regime: low-variance amplification, mean-centering blindness, and zero-variance collapse. To address them, we propose MDP-GRPO, which stabilizes learning through (1) multi-temperature sampling to increase reward dispersion, (2) dual-anchor advantages to restore gradients in homogeneous groups and stop mean-centering blindness, (3) prospect-theoretic shaping to bound updates and penalize violations based on Kahneman and Tversky's theory, and (4) asymmetric KL regularization. Evaluated on FollowBench, IFEval, and a curated multi-constraint dataset, MDP-GRPO outperforms standard GRPO, improving strict constraint satisfaction by up to 5.0% on Llama-3.2-3B. Our method also enables stable convergence with small group sizes while preserving general capabilities on MMLU and ARC.

</details>


### [303] [On Advantage Estimates for Max@K Policy Gradients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06080)
*Shota Takashiro,Soichiro Nishimori,Paavo Parmas,Yongmin Kim,Kohsei Matsutani,Gouki Minegishi,Yusuke Iwasawa,Takeshi Kojima,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对推理时间目标优化中优势估计不一致和方差大的问题，提出了MaxPO算法。通过引入“留二法”（L2O）基线，在保证梯度无偏的前提下实现了优势函数的精确居中，从而显著降低了梯度方差并提升了大语言模型的后训练性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强化学习微调推理模型时，基于稀疏奖励的探索效率低下。尽管直接优化推理时间目标（如pass@K和max@K）是一种有效的补充策略，但现有方法在梯度估计器设计（如信号选择、基线使用及归一化）上缺乏统一的标准，导致各方法间的关系模糊且性能存在提升空间。因此，作者旨在从理论上理顺这些估计器，并优化基线设计以提升优化效率。

Method: 1. 理论分析：推导并对比了现有的推理时目标（如pass@K和max@K）策略梯度估计器，揭示了其在基线设计和优势居中处理上的不一致性。
2. 算法创新：提出了“留二法”（Leave-Two-Out, L2O）基线，在保持策略梯度无偏性的同时，实现了批处理优势的精确居中。
3. 框架实现：基于上述理论构建了MaxPO（Maximum Policy Optimization）方法，并提供了二次时间复杂度的实现方案，可自然地融入组内强化学习流程。
4. 统一视角：推导了max@K的规范化有限批次优势估计公式。

Result: 1. 证明了现有领先方法的优势估计器虽无偏，但未能实现优势函数居中。
2. 提出的L2O基线能够显著降低梯度估计的方差。
3. 在实验中，MaxPO算法在多项任务上表现优于现有的非居中优势估计方法。
4. 成功推导出max@K的典型有限批次优势形式，明确了现有各种估计器的理论关联。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入“留二法”（Leave-Two-Out）基线，解决了推理时目标优化中优势函数未居中导致的问题。MaxPO方法不仅理论上保证了策略梯度的无偏性，还在实验中证明了其能够有效降低梯度方差，并在大语言模型后训练任务中取得了优于现有非居中方法的性能。该研究统一了针对max@K目标的优势估计器视角，为推理时强化学习提供了更高效、更稳定的优化框架。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards is widely used for post-training reasoning models, but sparse outcome rewards make exploration difficult. A complementary approach is to optimize inference-time objectives such as pass@K and max@K directly, yet existing policy-gradient estimators for these objectives use different signals, baselines, and normalizations, making their relationships unclear. We study this issue through baseline design and advantage centering. Starting from the advantage estimator of a leading method in the field, we show that it is policy-gradient unbiased but yields a non-centered advantage. We then introduce a Leave-Two-Out baseline that preserves policy-gradient unbiasedness while making realized batch advantages exactly centered. The resulting method, MaxPO, has an efficient quadratic-time implementation and integrates naturally into group-based RL for LLM post-training. We further derive the canonical finite-batch advantage for max@K, providing a unified view of existing advantage estimators. Empirically, we verify that the L2O baseline reduces gradient variance and outperforms non-centered alternatives.

</details>


### [304] [OrderGrad: Optimizing Beyond the Mean with Order-Statistic Policy Gradient Estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06096)
*Paavo Parmas,Yongmin Kim,Kohsei Matsutani,Shota Takashiro,Soichiro Nishimori,Takeshi Kojima,Yusuke Iwasawa,Yutaka Matsuo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: OrderGrad 是一种通用的梯度估计框架，它通过简单的奖励重加权，使策略梯度算法能够优化收益分布的顺序统计量（如 VaR、CVaR、中位数等），从而有效解决期望收益优化无法满足的风险控制和探索需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的策略梯度方法主要侧重于优化期望收益，但在许多实际应用中，人们更关注收益的分布特性，例如尾部风险（Tail Risk）、异常值鲁棒性或寻找“Best-of-K”解。为了填补这一空白，需要一种能够直接且高效地优化这些分布属性的梯度估计方法。

Method: 作者引入了 OrderGrad，这是一类针对顺序统计量目标的似然比和重参数化梯度估计器。该方法通过将有限样本的 L-统计量（即排序奖励的加权平均）作为优化目标，利用简单的奖励变换技术，使得现有的策略梯度算法无需复杂改动即可直接优化 VaR、CVaR、截尾均值、中位数及 Top-m/Best-of-K 等复杂目标。

Result: 研究表明，OrderGrad 能够针对给定的采样大小和权重向量提供无偏的梯度估计。在包括大语言模型（LLM）数学推理在内的实际任务中，该方法证明了在目标与期望优化不匹配的情况下，通过调整排名权重，可以有效实现风险规避、增强鲁棒性及提升探索性能。

Conclusion: OrderGrad 提供了一种通用、即插即用的框架，通过简单的奖励转换即可对各种顺序统计量目标进行无偏梯度估计。该方法不仅在理论上保证了梯度的无偏性，还在 LLM 数学微调及其他任务中证明了其在风险规避、鲁棒性提升和最优解发现方面的有效性，克服了传统策略梯度方法仅优化期望收益的局限性。

Abstract: Policy-gradient methods usually optimize expected return, but many real world applications care about distributional properties of returns: tail risk, outlier robustness, or best-of-K discovery. We introduce OrderGrad, a family of likelihood-ratio and reparameterization gradient estimators for order-statistic objectives. OrderGrad optimizes finite-sample L-statistics, i.e., weighted averages of sorted rewards or costs, recovering objectives such as VaR, CVaR, trimmed means, medians, and top-m/best-of-K criteria by changing only the rank weights. For any fixed sample size and rank-weight vector, OrderGrad provides an unbiased gradient estimator for the corresponding order-statistic objective. The method is implemented as a simple reward transformation that can then be used in an otherwise standard policy-gradient or reparameterized update. We study the resulting estimator's variance behavior and evaluate it on tasks where mean optimization is mismatched to the deployment objective, including LLM math post-training and other tasks. OrderGrad provides a unified, plug-and-play route to risk-averse, robust, and exploratory learning.
  Code: https://github.com/paavo5/ordergrad

</details>


### [305] [A Sliced-Wasserstein Framework on Correlation Matrices for EEG Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06104)
*Chen Hu,Rui Wang,Jiale Zhou,Jingjun Yi,Shaocheng Jin,Yidong Song,Yefeng Zheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于 Pullback Euclidean Metrics 的 Sliced Wasserstein (PEMSW) 框架，通过在全秩相关矩阵流形上定义新的度量标准（CorSW），显著提升了 EEG 解码模型在域泛化任务中的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的 EEG 解码管道常依赖于协方差描述符，但其对通道缩放敏感。虽然全秩相关矩阵是解决尺度不变性的有效替代方案，但尚缺乏在该流形上有效的分布度量方法，因此需要开发新的距离度量框架以提升 EEG 解码的鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Method: 本文提出了 PEMSW 框架，并在全秩相关矩阵流形上实例化了两种 Correlation Sliced-Wasserstein (CorSW) 差异：基于 Off-Log Metric (OLM) 和 Log-Scaled Metric (LSM)。在此基础上，构建了一个用于 EEG 解码的域泛化 (DG) 框架，利用这些测度来处理分布偏移问题。

Result: 在三个 EEG 数据集上的实验结果表明，PEMSW 框架在处理分布偏移时具有更好的泛化性能，并且相比现有方法，该方案在保持低训练开销的同时，不会增加任何推理时的计算成本。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于 Pullback Euclidean Metrics 的 Sliced Wasserstein (PEMSW) 框架，成功将其应用于全秩相关矩阵流形上的 EEG 解码任务。该方法通过引入 OLM 和 LSM 几何结构，有效提升了跨域 EEG 数据的泛化能力，且具有训练开销低、推理无额外负担的优点。

Abstract: Electroencephalography (EEG) offers noninvasive, millisecond resolution recordings of neuronal activity and is widely used in neuroscience and healthcare. Many EEG decoding pipelines rely on covariance descriptors for their robustness to noise, but such representations are sensitive to channel-wise scaling. Recent studies have therefore advocated full-rank correlation matrices as a scale-invariant alternative for EEG decoding. In this paper, we propose a general framework for Sliced Wasserstein (SW) discrepancies on manifolds endowed with Pullback Euclidean Metrics (PEMs), termed Pullback Euclidean Metric Sliced Wasserstein (PEMSW). Within this framework, we instantiate two Correlation Sliced-Wasserstein (CorSW) discrepancies on the manifold of full-rank correlation matrices under two recently introduced correlation geometries, \textit{i.e.}, the Off-Log Metric (OLM) and Log-Scaled Metric (LSM). Building on CorSW, we further develop a domain generalization (DG) framework for EEG decoding. Experiments on three EEG datasets demonstrate improved generalization under distribution shifts, with low training overhead and no additional inference cost. The source code is available at https://github.com/ChenHu-ML/CorSW.

</details>


### [306] [Adaptive state-action abstractions via rate-distortion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06123)
*Fernando E. Rosas*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种强化学习中动态调整抽象粒度的新原则：通过监控学习误差与抽象误差的平衡，自动优化模型分辨率，从而在显著降低计算复杂度的情况下保持高效的任务执行能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 婴儿在学习行走时通过先粗略后精细的策略解决复杂问题，但现有的强化学习算法缺乏一种通用原则来指导学习过程中抽象粒度的动态调整，导致难以高效处理复杂任务的层级表征。

Method: 本文提出了一种基于“误差平衡”的动态抽象细化原则：当学习误差与抽象引起的误差相当时，即对模型进行细化。具体实现上，采用性能证书（Performance Certificate）方法，将值函数误差分解为贝尔曼残差（学习误差）和双模拟度量（抽象误差），并利用基于率失真理论的软状态-动作抽象策略，实现状态和动作空间分辨率的连续调整。

Result: 在多种表格环境中的验证表明，该方法能够通过对状态和动作空间进行显著的损耗压缩，在保持接近最优性能的同时，显著降低计算复杂度，验证了该抽象调整策略的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入误差平衡原则，成功在强化学习中实现了动态抽象粒度的自适应调节。该方法证明了在学习误差与抽象误差相当时进行细化是优化性能的关键，为处理复杂任务的层级学习提供了理论基础和实践路径。

Abstract: When learning to walk, infants seem to address a coarse version of the problem first - stay upright, reach the caregiver - and refine it only when further practice at that resolution stops paying off. Reinforcement learning offers multiple techniques for building simple versions of complex tasks, but lacks general principles for how to dynamically adjust the granularity of these abstractions during learning. This paper proposes one such principle: refine the abstraction as soon as the learning error within it becomes comparable to the error induced by the abstraction itself. Here, we investigate one way of formalising this principle via a performance certificate that decomposes value error into two terms: a learning error bound captured by a Bellman residual, and an abstraction error bound given by a bisimulation metric. The resulting switching strategy is implemented by soft state-action abstractions built from rate-distortion principles, whose resolution along state and action axes can be continuously adjusted. We validate this construction in a range of tabular settings, showing that near-optimal performance can be achieved under substantial lossy compression of state and action information.

</details>


### [307] [Tight list replicability bounds via a novel sphere covering theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06148)
*Ari Blondal,Hamed Hatami,Pooya Hatami,Chavdar Lalov,Sivan Tretiak*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入拓扑球面覆盖定理，为学习理论中的“列表可复现性”提供了精确的理论界限，并针对半空间分类问题优化了可复现算法的列表大小需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨学习理论中“列表可复现性”这一框架，试图明确解决列表大小（list size）与精度参数以及假设类自然复杂度测度之间的量化关系。

Method: 论文通过将学习理论问题转化为拓扑学问题，证明了一个基于Borsuk-Ulam定理的全新球面覆盖定理（若d维球面被开集覆盖且每个集合位于开半球内，则至少d+1个集合有公共交集），以此推导列表可复现性的界限，并针对大间隔半空间设计了特定的可复现算法。

Result: 1. 证明了一个新的拓扑球面覆盖定理；2. 获得了VC类中列表大小与精度之间关系的精确界限；3. 证明了对于一般大间隔半空间，最优列表大小为环境维度d，而当间隔足够大时，该值可降至⌈d/2⌉ + 1。

Conclusion: 该研究通过拓扑学工具成功建立了列表可复现性（list replicability）的精确界限，揭示了算法复杂性与学习精度之间的本质联系，并证明了在不同间隔设置下VC类和半空间分类器的最优列表大小。

Abstract: In recent years, list replicability has emerged as a framework for formalizing reproducibility in learning theory. A central question is how the required list size relates to the accuracy parameter and natural complexity measures of the hypothesis class.
  To achieve sharp bounds on list replicability, we prove a novel topological sphere covering theorem, derived from the Borsuk-Ulam theorem. Specifically, if the $d$-sphere is covered by open sets, each of which lies in an open hemisphere, then $d+1$ of these sets must have a common intersection. Using this result, we obtain a sharp bound on the relationship between list size and accuracy for VC classes. We also show that for large-margin half-spaces, provided the margin is not too large, the optimal list size equals the ambient dimension. However, when the margin is taken to be very large, we devise a replicable algorithm achieving the minimal list size of $\lceil d/2 \rceil + 1$.

</details>


### [308] [Trust-Aware Predictive Emissions Monitoring for Gas Turbine Fleets with Limited Labelled Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06156)
*Rebecca Potts,Aiden Durrant,Rick Hackney,Georgios Leontidis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对燃气轮机机队标注数据不足的问题，本文提出了一种信任感知概率框架，通过多维不确定性量化提供可解释的预测置信度，有效提升了跨资产排放预测的可靠性与透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于机器学习的排放监测系统（PEMS）在燃气轮机机队中的推广面临挑战，主要原因是仅少数资产拥有标注数据，如何在标注数据有限的情况下确保跨机队预测的准确性与可靠性成为关键问题。

Method: 提出了一种信任感知概率框架，结合了多头循环预测模型、学习型置信度估计、基于集成的集成不确定性量化、辅助特征预测、特征空间距离分析以及运行范围诊断。通过在有标注数据上校准上述信号，为每个预测样本生成可解释的信任分数。

Result: 实验表明，置信度过滤机制将平均绝对误差（MAE）从全量覆盖时的0.202降低至最高置信度10%样本下的0.070。此外，该框架能准确识别未标注及分布外（OOD）样本，表现出更强的不确定性，验证了置信度指标与预测误差的高度相关性。

Conclusion: 该研究提出的信任感知概率框架能够有效量化燃气轮机排放预测的不确定性，为在无标注数据资产上的部署提供了可靠的置信度指标，证明了该方法在工业场景中实现透明、可信排放监控的可行性。

Abstract: Machine learning-based predictive emissions monitoring systems offer a practical alternative to direct emissions measurement, but their deployment across gas turbine fleets is challenging when emissions labels are available for only a small subset of assets. In this work, a trust-aware probabilistic framework is proposed for fleet-level gas turbine NOx prediction under limited labelled supervision. The framework combines a multi-head recurrent prediction model with learned confidence estimation, ensemble-based uncertainty quantification, auxiliary feature prediction, feature-space distance analysis, and operating-range diagnostics. These signals are calibrated on labelled data to produce interpretable per-sample trust scores, providing indicators of prediction reliability on unlabelled turbines, supporting the identification of predictions that should be treated with greater caution during fleet-level deployment. Confidence-based filtering reduces MAE from 0.202 at full coverage to 0.070 for the highest-confidence 10\% of predictions, demonstrating that confidence estimates are meaningfully related to prediction error. Unlabelled and out-of-distribution samples exhibit increased uncertainty and reduced confidence, indicating that the framework responds appropriately to distributional shift. The results show that the proposed trust framework provides actionable reliability information for emissions prediction on unlabelled turbines, supporting more transparent and trustworthy deployment of PEMS across industrial fleets.

### [309] [On the training of physics-informed neural operators for solving parametric partial differential equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06164)
*Nanxi Chen,Chuanjie Cui,Airong Chen,Sifan Wang,Rujin Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文对物理信息神经算子（PINO）的训练流程进行了深入的实证研究，提出了优化架构选择、损失函数平衡及采样策略的有效方案，并证实了改善PINN训练的算法同样能显著提升PINO的性能和稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管物理信息神经算子（PINO）结合了神经算子的跨实例泛化能力与物理信息学习的数据效率，但目前缺乏对其训练机制的深入理解，导致其训练过程往往不如数据驱动的神经算子或物理信息神经网络（PINN）稳健。需建立系统化的训练流程以克服这些优化障碍。

Method: 通过对比DeepONet、FNO和CViT三种神经算子架构，在五个参数化PDE系统上进行评估；系统分析了架构选择、优化器、损失平衡和配置点采样策略对训练的影响；引入并验证了PINN中的梯度冲突和因果违规 mitigation 算法在PINO训练中的有效性。

Result: 研究发现，CViT作为算子骨干网络在所有基准测试中表现最强且最稳健；PINO训练中存在与PINN类似的梯度冲突和因果违规问题；通过优化训练流程，物理信息学习方法在各种数据制度下均能实现高性能，且在特定场景下优于纯数据驱动方法。

Conclusion: 本文系统性地揭示了物理信息神经算子（PINO）训练中的优化挑战，通过优化架构、损失函数平衡和采样策略，证明了经过精心设计的物理驱动训练流程在数据效率和泛化能力上可以媲美甚至超越纯数据驱动模型。研究证实了针对PINN的优化策略在PINO中依然有效。

Abstract: Physics-informed neural operators (PINOs) aim to learn solution operators for partial differential equations by using the governing physics as supervision, rather than relying solely on paired input-output simulation data. By incorporating physical constraints into the training objective, PINOs combine the cross-instance generalization of neural operators with the data efficiency of physics-informed learning. Despite this promise, how to train PINOs efficiently and robustly remains less well-understood than the training of either data-driven neural operators or physics-informed neural networks (PINNs). To bridge this gap, we examine key components of the PINO training pipeline, including architecture design, optimizer choice, loss balancing, and collocation-point sampling strategy. We study three representative operator backbones, Deep Operator Network (DeepONet), Fourier Neural Operator (FNO), and Continuous Vision Transformer (CViT), across five diverse parametric PDE systems. Our results show that CViT provides consistently strong and stable performance across the considered benchmarks. Beyond architecture, we find that several optimization pathologies previously identified in PINN training naturally arise in PINOs, including gradient conflicts and causal violation. We also find that mitigation algorithms developed for PINNs remain effective in the PINO setting. We further compare physics-informed and data-driven training under different data regimes, revealing that a carefully designed physics-informed training pipeline can match, and in some cases, outperform purely data-driven neural operators. Taken together, these findings provide a systematic empirical understanding of the optimization challenges in PINO training and inform a practical pipeline for efficient and robust physics-informed operator learning. Code and data are available at https://github.com/NanxiiChen/PI-CViT.

</details>

### [313] [Non-Negative Matrix Factorization for Event Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06205)
*Raphaël Romero*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的非负矩阵分解（NMF）方法通常需要对连续时间事件数据进行分箱或平滑预处理，但这会导致实体层面的异质性丢失以及细粒度时间特征的模糊。研究旨在开发一种直接在连续时间事件上操作的方法，以保留原始数据的时空结构。

Method: 提出了一种名为 EventNMF 的模型，该模型将每个实体的事件建模为泊松过程，其强度函数通过非负 B 样条基函数进行分解。该方法无需预先进行分箱或平滑处理，直接在原始事件时间上运行，并利用简单的估计程序提取跨实体共享的解释性时序模板。

Result: 研究表明，标准的分箱计数方法实际上是该模型中使用零阶样条的一种特殊情况。通过合成数据模型与现有方法的对比，证明了 EventNMF 在偏差-方差权衡方面的优势，并在多个真实世界数据集上验证了其提取时序模板的有效性。

Conclusion: EventNMF 证明了在处理连续时间事件数据时，无需将数据分箱即可直接建模的优越性。该模型不仅具有坚实的数学基础，还提供了一种高效、易于实现且具有高解释性的分析框架，能够有效挖掘不同领域中的潜在时序模式。

Abstract: Continuous-time event data, in which entities emit instantaneous events over time, arises naturally across many domains such as neuroscience, seismology, and social networks. Non-negative matrix factorization (NMF) is a natural tool to uncover interpretable structure in such data, but it has so far only been applied after binning or smoothing the entity-level counting measures. This preprocessing step comes with the risk of erasing entity-level heterogeneities and fine-grained temporal features. In this paper, we introduce EventNMF, a continuous-time non-negative factorization model that operates directly on event times: each entity's events are modeled as a Poisson process whose intensity factorizes through a non-negative B-spline basis, and a simple estimation procedure recovers interpretable temporal templates shared across entities. The resulting method is mathematically principled, easy to implement, and computationally efficient. We further show that standard binned-count approaches arise as the special case of degree-zero splines, explore bias-variance tradeoffs and compare against existing methods on a synthetic latent factor model, and demonstrate the effectiveness of EventNMF on several real-world applications.

### [315] [Tracing the Oracle: Improving Diffusion Timestep Scheduling for 3D CT Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06236)
*Yujia Wu,Zhaoqiang Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 TrO 的扩散模型采样调度框架，通过动态规划优化时间步分配，解决了 3D CT 重建中少步采样导致的截断误差问题，实现了高效率与高保真度的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的预训练扩散模型在解决 3D CT 逆问题时推理成本高昂，且传统的均匀采样时间步难以适应扩散模型的非均匀演化特性，导致严重的截断误差，限制了少步采样下的重建精度。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Tracing the Oracle (TrO)”的即插即用时间步调度框架。该方法首先通过对少量样本进行高密度采样构建“参考预言机（Oracle）”轨迹，随后利用动态规划算法，最小化少步采样轨迹与预言机轨迹之间的累积误差，从而确定最优的时间步分配策略。

Result: 在 AAPM 数据集上的实验表明，将 TrO 与现有的 3D CT 重建方法（如 DDS）结合，在 10 步以内的严苛采样预算下，显著提升了重建的保真度，并比启发式调度方法展现出更高的计算效率。

Conclusion: TrO 框架通过动态规划实现了扩散模型采样时间步的全局最优分配，显著提升了 3D CT 重建在极低步数（<=10步）下的图像质量与计算效率，验证了非均匀时间步调度在处理复杂反问题时的重要性。

Abstract: Pretrained diffusion models demonstrate impressive potential in solving highly ill-posed 3D computed tomography (CT) inverse problems, while the inference process suffers from significant computational overhead. Furthermore, existing uniform timestep schedules fail to capture the non-uniform evolution of the reverse conditional diffusion stochastic differential equation, thereby introducing substantial truncation errors. To overcome this limitation, we propose Tracing the Oracle (TrO), a plug-and-play framework for improved timestep scheduling. Specifically, we treat densely sampled numerical integration trajectories on a few samples as the reference oracle. The optimized schedule is extracted by leveraging dynamic programming to globally minimize the cumulative error between the few-step approximation and the oracle. This mechanism precisely allocates the limited sampling steps to critical evolution stages that are highly susceptible to truncation errors. Our extensive experiments on the AAPM dataset across multiple 3D CT reconstruction tasks demonstrate that, when combined with the state-of-the-art 3D CT reconstruction method DDS, our optimized timesteps significantly improve reconstruction fidelity and computational efficiency compared to existing heuristic schedules, especially under a strict budget of no more than 10 sampling steps.

### [316] [Generative Criticality in Large Language Model Temperature Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06238)
*Huajian Ruan,Jinyang Li,Xingyu Guo,Lingxiao Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文将统计场论引入大语言模型生成过程，通过分析 Token 嵌入向量的统计特征，揭示了 LLM 在不同 Softmax 温度下表现出类似物理系统中“连续相变”的临界行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大模型生成机制研究多侧重于应用层，缺乏对生成过程统计物理本质的深入理解。研究者旨在通过统计场论工具定量探测大模型输出的集体统计结构，并探究解码策略与相变现象之间的深层联系。

Method: 将大模型生成的 Token 嵌入向量视为一维链上的连续自旋变量，构建统计场论框架；通过计算连通两点关联函数的磁化率（Susceptibility）和系综平均嵌入场的序参数（Order parameter），分析 Softmax 温度 $T$ 对系统状态的影响；并使用 TwoNN 方法评估内在维度以进行验证。

Result: 研究发现模型在特征温度 $T_c$ 附近表现出明显的磁化率峰值（符合幂律标度）以及序参数的剧烈变化；在该温度以下，模型输出坍缩至单一语义方向，且内在维度在 $T_c$ 处达到极小值。该现象在不同规模的模型（Qwen3: 0.6B--32B）及不同提示词类别中均具有稳健性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明大语言模型生成的文本序列中存在类似于统计物理中连续相变的集体行为，即在临界温度 $T_c$ 附近，模型从发散的无序状态转变为向单一语义方向收敛的有序状态。这一发现为理解生成过程中的随机性与语义稳定性提供了物理学视角。

Abstract: We propose a statistical-field framework for text generated by large language models (LLMs), treating token embeddings as continuous spin variables on a one-dimensional chain. Defining a susceptibility from the connected two-point correlator and an order parameter from the ensemble-averaged embedding field, we vary the \texttt{softmax} temperature $T$ and observe a sharp susceptibility peak near a characteristic $T_c$ with power-law-like scaling, a concurrent rapid change in the order parameter, and a collapse onto a single semantic direction below $T_c$. The intrinsic dimension estimated by the two nearest neighbor (TwoNN) method independently corroborates these findings, reaching a minimum near $T_c$. Results are robust across model scales (Qwen3: 0.6B--32B) and prompt categories. While the phenomenology closely resembles a continuous phase transition, the non-equilibrium nature of autoregressive generation warrants further investigation. Our framework provides quantitative tools for probing the collective statistical structure of LLM outputs and suggests connections between decoding strategies and critical phenomena.

### [317] [Your GFlowNet Secretly Learns an Optimal Transport Plan](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06272)
*Ian Maksimov,Nikita Morozov,Denis Belomestny,Sergey Samsonov*

TL;DR: 本文揭示了非循环GFlowNets与最优传输问题之间的理论联系，提出利用GFlowNets高效求解大规模图结构上的最优传输规划。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的最优传输求解器在处理大规模图结构时往往面临计算复杂度的挑战。本文旨在利用GFlowNets在采样结构化对象方面的优势，探索其在解决图上最优传输问题中的应用潜力，并从理论上论证其学习目标与最优传输规划的一致性。

Method: 研究建立了非循环GFlowNets与Kantorovich形式最优传输问题之间的理论对等性。通过将GFlowNet的最小流目标函数重构，证明了其学习到的策略本质上是求解带有图诱导最短路径代价的最优传输规划。该方法通过边流（edge flows）和神经网络参数化，能够处理大规模图上的OT计算。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法求解出的传输规划与精确的OT求解器得到的结果高度一致，验证了GFlowNets能够有效地学习高质量的传输方案，并具备在大规模图上进行扩展的能力。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将非循环GFlowNets与最优传输（OT）理论联系起来，证明了最小流GFlowNets可以作为求解大规模图结构上最优传输问题的有效工具，为在复杂离散空间中处理传输规划问题提供了新的算法框架。

Abstract: Generative Flow Networks (GFlowNets) are a framework for sampling structured objects via stochastic trajectories in a directed graph. In this work, we establish a theoretical connection between non-acyclic GFlowNets and optimal transport (OT). We show that fixing the initial flow distribution in a minimum-flow GFlowNet reduces its objective to a Kantorovich OT problem with graph-induced shortest path costs. At the optimum, the learned GFlowNet policy therefore encodes an optimal transport plan from the source distribution to the target distribution: we show that sampling trajectories from the minimum-flow GFlowNet recovers the corresponding optimal coupling. Our formulation enables applying the GFlowNet learning framework to OT problems on large graphs via edge flows and neural parameterization. Experiments confirm agreement with exact OT solvers and demonstrate that GFlowNets can learn high-quality transport plans.

</details>


### [318] [PAC-Bayesian Adversarially Robust Generalization for Message Passing Graph Neural Networks: A Sensitivity Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06293)
*Ziling Liang,Xinping Yi,Qingsong Wen,Shi Jin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对图神经网络在对抗攻击下的泛化性分析问题，提出了一种基于敏感度感知的PAC-Bayesian框架，通过利用雅可比矩阵的低秩特性优化各向异性高斯后验，大幅提升了鲁棒泛化界，摆脱了对网络宽度的过度依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图神经网络（GNNs）对抗鲁棒性分析通常依赖于各向同性高斯后验，且在全参数空间内控制扰动，这忽略了参数敏感度的异质性，导致复杂度项过度依赖网络宽度，使得现有的泛化界不够紧致，无法有效指导鲁棒模型的构建。

Method: 1. 将敏感度感知的PAC-Bayesian框架从深层神经网络扩展至消息传递图神经网络（MPGNNs）；2. 通过计算权重参数的输出雅可比矩阵，量化不同参数块对网络输出的敏感度；3. 利用雅可比矩阵秩受限于类别数 $K$ 的特性，构建雅可比对齐敏感度矩阵；4. 采用各向异性高斯后验分布并优化协方差，以更紧致地界定KL散度。

Result: 该方法成功将泛化界中对隐层宽度的依赖降低至与分类类别数 $K$ 相关，显著提升了泛化界的紧致性。理论分析表明，这种改进能够更准确地反映对抗攻击下的实际鲁棒泛化性能。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入敏感度感知分析框架，成功改进了图神经网络在对抗环境下的泛化界，证明了该方法能够降低对网络宽度的依赖，从而提供更紧致的理论保证，为设计鲁棒的图神经网络提供了新的理论指导。

Abstract: Whilst the vulnerability of graph neural networks (GNNs) to adversarial attacks poses a critical threat to graph representation learning, the understanding of the robust generalization behavior remains a fundamental challenge in the adversarial setting. Recently, PAC-Bayesian margin-based generalization analysis substantially advances this line of research by providing a flexible and data-dependent analytical framework. However, existing robust analyses often rely on isotropic Gaussian posteriors and control weight perturbations in the full parameter space, which limits the ability to capture heterogeneous parameter sensitivity yet hinges on hidden-width-dependent complexity terms, resulting in not-tight-enough generalization bounds. In this paper, we extend a recently proposed sensitivity-aware PAC-Bayesian framework from deep neural networks to message passing GNNs (MPGNNs) and derive a tighter robust generalization bound in the adversarial setting. Specifically, we first quantify how sensitive the perturbations across different parameter blocks are to the network outputs by deriving the output Jacobians with respect to the weight parameters. Exploiting the fact that these Jacobian matrices have rank at most $K$ in $K$-class graph classification, we then construct Jacobian-aligned sensitivity matrices and use anisotropic Gaussian posteriors with optimized covariances to upper bound the KL divergence in a tight way. Notably, by refining the spectral-norm dependence on the learned weights and reducing the leading dimension factor from hidden-width-dependent terms to the number of classes $K$, our analysis yields much tighter robust generalization guarantees for MPGNNs, thereby guiding their designs to enhance adversarial robustness.

### [319] [Reactive Flux Matching: Mechanism Discovery and Adaptive Sampling of Rare Events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06295)
*Rishal Aggarwal,David Ryan Koes,Nicholas M. Boffi,Eric Vanden-Eijnden*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“通量匹配”（Flux Matching）的新框架，无需预知动力学信息，即可直接从反应轨迹数据中学习反应路径场和数据驱动的反应坐标，克服了传统方法在非马尔可夫空间下的局限性，并能优化后续的采样效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的路径采样方法虽然能生成反应轨迹，但如何从复杂的数据中提取直观的反应机理仍是一个难题。此外，基于提交函数（committor）的传统方法在投影到非马尔可夫集体变量时往往失效，因此需要一种更稳健、更具解释性的数据驱动框架来分析反应路径和确定反应坐标。

Method: 该研究提出了一种基于变分原理的框架，通过最小化平方损失泛函（类似于生成模型中的流匹配），直接从反应轨迹集合中学习：1. 当前速度场 $u(z)$：其流线描绘了主要的反应路径；2. 标量势 $h(z)$：通过反应电流的加权亥姆霍兹-霍奇分解（Helmholtz-Hodge decomposition）获得，作为数据驱动的反应坐标。该方法不依赖于系统的潜在动力学或平稳分布。

Result: Flux Matching 方法在分子系统中的应用得到了验证，能够准确生成当前速度轨迹并有效进行速率常数计算。此外，其学习到的标量势的水平集可用于构建自适应接口，从而显著提升增强采样方法的效率。

Conclusion: “通量匹配”（Flux Matching）框架为分析反应轨迹提供了一种有效且通用的工具。该方法能够从反应轨迹数据中自动学习反应路径和反应坐标，无需先验动力学信息，并能有效克服传统提交函数（committor）方法在非马尔可夫投影下的局限性，为复杂分子系统的机理研究提供了新思路。

Abstract: Path sampling methods generate ensembles of reactive trajectories connecting metastable states, but extracting mechanistic insight from these data remains nontrivial. We introduce Flux Matching, a framework that learns two complementary objects directly from reactive trajectory data: a current velocity $u(z)$, whose streamlines trace the dominant reaction pathways, and a scalar potential $h(z)$, obtained from a weighted Helmholtz-Hodge decomposition of the reactive current, that serves as a data-driven reaction coordinate. Both minimize quadratic functionals over the reactive path ensemble, analogous to the flow matching loss in generative modeling, and require no knowledge of the underlying dynamics or stationary distribution. Unlike committor-based methods, $u$ and $h$ remain well-defined under projection onto non-Markovian collective variables, and their level sets in turn provide adaptive interfaces for improved sampling with enhanced sampling methods. Flux Matching is validated through the generation of current velocity trajectories and rate constant calculations on molecular systems.
